
-----title
江阴 (出生地)

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年12月</a>　回江阴故里居住，筑二老堂。作品：依韵和工部兄雪五首。<div id='poem_523722' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523722' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523722?labeling=true' target='_blank'>依韵和工部兄雪五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523722")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523722_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523722'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523722'>风撼柴门夜不关，黎明琼玉遍人寰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523722'>举头寒掩东隅日，纵目高疑西域山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523722'>朝路昔宁飘袂上，禅房今喜点炉间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523722'>亦知尘雾难撄拂，万径行踪绝往还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523723'>知酬素景风尘外，坐隔清游咫尺间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523723'>飞洒却羞来傍鬓，安仁年少不重还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523723'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523723_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523724' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523724' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523724?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523724'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523724'>从此何忧家事关，明年粒米厌区寰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523724'>腰青不见飞花女，头白先看对面山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523724'>弦冻未应停绿绮，胶彊仍喜彀黄间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523724'>平铺万顷茅檐冷，欲问城居几日还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523724'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523724_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523725' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523725' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_523725_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523725'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523725'>门似柴桑画亦关，歘惊阊阖堕人寰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523725'>郊原那异熬波海，垄阜浑疑聚米山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523725'>望远恨无楼百尺，逃寒阻共屋三间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523725'>阿兄诗句清奇甚，格律都高汉以还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523725'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523725_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523726' id='poem_sentence_0_523726'>偶兹穷腊憩乡关，无蒂花飞遍海寰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523726'>粉饰门闱疑省户，云屯观阙想神山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523726'>飘狂不绝三冬里，积厚遥追二纪间<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：乡中二十五年无此雪。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523726'>闻说旗亭增酒价，沈酣准拟典衣还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523726'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523726_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a><div id='poem_523671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吾家故事子侄登第必有酬献诗什去岁立悌立经二侄并中科选未有庆以诗者偶示四韵</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_523671'>充闾秀气我家多，又喜双龙并化梭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523671'>同榜连荣追绍圣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，传名跻甲首宣和<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523671'>朝班鸣玉犹升舍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，冠岁横金又中科<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：权之中科日已服紫锡带。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523671'>四叶登华谁得似，会看盛事入编摩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523671'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_523671'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_523671_0'>⑴ 自注：予与伯兄大成同中绍圣四年第。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_523671_0'>⑵ 自注：顺之、权之并蒙恩升甲，吾家前未有。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_523671_0'>⑶ 自注：顺之为奉礼郎，以国子上舍生试入等。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_523671_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年12月</a>　十二月二十四日钦宗即位二十九日尊徽宗为太上皇作贺表。作品：贺孝慈渊圣皇帝登宝位表。<div id='poem_1214260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺孝慈渊圣皇帝登宝位表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214260")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214260'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214260'>祗遵圣诏，光绍皇图，历数在躬，华夷交戴<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214260_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下睿哲天纵，钦明日跻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214260_comment'></div>主鬯十年，懋毓震闱之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214260_comment'></div>收畿千里，益宅寰宇之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214260_comment'></div>骏命所归，神器允属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214260_comment'></div>臣夙有厚幸，蚤依末光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214260_comment'></div>奉匴以升，实相阼阶之冠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214260_comment'></div>建储之始，首叨潜府之僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214260_comment'></div>方兹圣作之初，阻预班朝之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214260_comment'></div>无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1214260_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1126')">1125-1126年</a><div id='poem_1214259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214259?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺太上皇表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214259")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214259'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214259'>圣谟独断，神器传归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214259_comment'></div>绵宗社于无疆，浃人神而胥庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214259_comment'></div>恭惟道君皇帝陛下跻时嘉靖，体道希微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214259_comment'></div>唐尧闻康衢之谣，有熊喜大庭之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214259_comment'></div>谓青宫之预建，顾黄屋以何心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214259_comment'></div>爰降册书，俾嗣历服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214259_comment'></div>巍巍荡荡，难名不宰之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214259_comment'></div>继继绳绳，永昌无为之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214259_comment'></div>臣出尸祠馆，阻造朝班，无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1214259_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214360' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214360' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214360?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺耿左丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214360")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214360_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214360'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214360'>光被宸辉，进陪国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214360_comment'></div>人惟求旧，允资攀附之贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214360_comment'></div>政贵有常，行迪太和之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214360_comment'></div>华夏咸喜，天人同符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214360_comment'></div>恭惟某官气禀天和，时推人杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214360_comment'></div>备忠孝之令德，兼文武之全才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214360_comment'></div>知谋天下之蓍龟，文藻人中之星斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214360_comment'></div>久负经纶之蕴，荐膺清切之除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214360_comment'></div>方睿神渊默以居潜，赖耆明始终之庇职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214360_comment'></div>朱邸著讲论之益，青宫遍调护之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214360_comment'></div>逮九五之时升，擢二八以自辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214360_comment'></div>俾司枢筦，实本兵权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214360_comment'></div>属强敌之长驱，拥全师而深入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214360_comment'></div>人心恟惧，神器震摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214360_comment'></div>逮兹多垒之秋，尽出万全之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214360_comment'></div>料敌制胜，有嘉右府之枢机；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214360_comment'></div>经体赞元，遂进中台之纲辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214360_comment'></div>惟兹旧学，光辅初元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214360_comment'></div>谅辰告于远猷，以日下于膏泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214360_comment'></div>愈峻具瞻之望，行膺爰立之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214360_comment'></div>伏念某涉世阔疏，谋身拙直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214360_comment'></div>顷滥尸于礼寺，亦叨预于宫僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214360_comment'></div>夤缘亲依，仰窥千虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214360_comment'></div>幸会奖与，实积三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214360_comment'></div>兹闻涣号之颁，深激懦衷之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214360_comment'></div>四蛇入穴，欣已附升云之龙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214360_comment'></div>六鹢退飞，无阶同贺厦之燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214360_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1214360_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺吴少宰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214414")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214414'>显膺纶綍，册拜钧衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214414_comment'></div>一言兴邦，独定公于社稷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214414_comment'></div>百官承式，亟冠位于疑丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214414_comment'></div>天人具孚，华夏咸喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214414_comment'></div>恭惟某官膺天大任，为世真儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214414_comment'></div>早以异材，遍跻膴仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214414_comment'></div>紫微司制，众钦华国之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214414_comment'></div>青琐纳言，自许经邦之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214414_comment'></div>谋猷屡告，权近不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214414_comment'></div>久安均逸之居，益养具瞻之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214414_comment'></div>继锋车之峻召，陟玉堂之近班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214414_comment'></div>凛然松柏之后凋，卓尔蓍龟之前识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214414_comment'></div>临大节而不可夺，可谓稷契之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214414_comment'></div>遭变事而知其宜，赞成舜禹之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214414_comment'></div>俄寇氛之俶扰，致神器之震摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214414_comment'></div>诸老生语如寒蝉，见大夫窜若狡兔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214414_comment'></div>天祐国步，公辅政机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214414_comment'></div>智略如神，而从容于仓卒之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214414_comment'></div>言辞如涌，而启发于睿神之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214414_comment'></div>力排出狩之议，坐成坚守之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214414_comment'></div>不移宗彝，再造王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214414_comment'></div>宋昌之迎代邸，谋协天心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214414_comment'></div>谢安之击淮淝，威破寇胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214414_comment'></div>爰膺帝制，进秉国成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214414_comment'></div>大开众正之门，力赞惟新之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214414_comment'></div>窜斥壬佞，拔举滞淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214414_comment'></div>形孝爱之风，念宸衷付托之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214414_comment'></div>谨号令之出，绳祖武艰难之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214414_comment'></div>太平之期，指日可俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214414_comment'></div>某羁单乏助，朴拙自将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214414_comment'></div>欣闻大号之扬，倍激懦衷之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214414_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1214414_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又贺少宰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214415")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214415'>光膺典册，进拜钧衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214415_comment'></div>君陈之入告谋猷，久隆帝眷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214415_comment'></div>周公之丕视功载，遂总国成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214415_comment'></div>纶綍诞扬，朝野交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214415_comment'></div>窃以坐庙堂而谋王体，秉机轴而亮天工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214415_comment'></div>上则燮和于阴阳，外则镇抚于蛮貊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214415_comment'></div>用人得失，系国重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214415_comment'></div>故当光明盛大之时，必有魁伟俊杰之辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214415_comment'></div>假羽翼而横绝，强精神而折冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214415_comment'></div>恭惟某官本朝宗工，斯民先觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214415_comment'></div>有经天纬地之文，而济以淹该之学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214415_comment'></div>有尊主强国之术，而持以肃括之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214415_comment'></div>方抡材三舍之初，即冠名群俊之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214415_comment'></div>纸价骤贵，众共服于文鸣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214415_comment'></div>帝席屡前，上特惊于见晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214415_comment'></div>粤从词禁，擢预政机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214415_comment'></div>遵制扬功，上继承于先烈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214415_comment'></div>料敌制胜，尽开拓于故疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214415_comment'></div>果符审象之求，亟付赞元之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214415_comment'></div>无偏无陂，已简记于渊衷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214415_comment'></div>有猷有为，伫扩摅于远业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214415_comment'></div>伏念某斗筲小器，刀笔下材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214415_comment'></div>册府徵文，尝预俊游之末；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214415_comment'></div>铨曹浮食，亦叨职守之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214415_comment'></div>流落七年，浮沈三郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214415_comment'></div>钦闻大涣，窃抃危悰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214415_comment'></div>久困风波，今幸帡幪之庇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214415_comment'></div>未填沟壑，永依播植之公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214415_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1214415_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
涟水

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1092')">1091-1092年</a>　居涟水，丁内艰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a><br /><a DetailSwitch("0f0320e9b75641d6b76d134fb76c3ead");'><span id='0f0320e9b75641d6b76d134fb76c3ead_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7c9892aa3f6941bba7aea2a8a84939f6_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>，32岁</div><div id='7c9892aa3f6941bba7aea2a8a84939f6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a><br /></div><div class='label1' id='46a3076bcfc74499b8e95b8be7a83420_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("46a3076bcfc74499b8e95b8be7a83420");'><span id='46a3076bcfc74499b8e95b8be7a83420_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1106')">1104-1106年</a>，33-35岁</div><div id='46a3076bcfc74499b8e95b8be7a83420' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　日读佛经。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年3月</a>　祝康病卒，作其墓志。作品：左朝议大夫致仕祝公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1214522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左朝议大夫致仕祝公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214522")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214522'>公讳康，字道济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214522_comment'></div>崇宁元年守鲁郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214522_comment'></div>时某分教诸生，公遇之厚，因与公之子天辅周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214522_comment'></div>后十三年，天辅之子将仕郎温彦踵门泣曰：「先大考葬宜有铭，先考欲求夫子为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214522_comment'></div>今敢以治命请，傥行许之，是赐逮三世也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214522_comment'></div>乃摭其状，叙曰：祝氏著籍单州成武，今为滑州韦城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214522_comment'></div>公之父曰咨，两第进士，积官至太常少卿、纠察在京刑狱，赠金紫光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214522_comment'></div>娶天水尹氏女，生公，是为永嘉郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214522_comment'></div>祖曰惟岳，卒官虞部员外郎，赠户部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214522_comment'></div>曾祖曰密，赠殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214522_comment'></div>公性夷澹，无浮念外好，独喜视书，载籍略皆诵记，名能文辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214522_comment'></div>四贡礼部，一为举首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214522_comment'></div>以门荫补将作监主簿，第试异等，赐明经出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214522_comment'></div>入刑部为习学公事法直官，又为检法详定官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214522_comment'></div>入大理寺为法直官，又为评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214522_comment'></div>入书局为官制检详文字，又为元丰编敕所删定官，删定一路敕令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214522_comment'></div>又为元祐所删定官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214522_comment'></div>入尚书省为刑部员外郎，又为郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214522_comment'></div>除知赵、晋、潞、兖四郡，管勾南京鸿庆宫，遂得谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214522_comment'></div>官自承事郎十迁为左朝议大夫，勋自武骑尉十一迁为柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214522_comment'></div>服佩朱衣、银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214522_comment'></div>初，金紫公屡更中外法理之选，小大之狱，申理枉桡甚众，故公于刑名之学目濡耳染，不习以能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214522_comment'></div>元丰中神宗皇帝欲入仕者通习文法，始建律学，又每岁聚天下士课试刑法，录上第者显擢之，凡廷尉宪部臣属皆推择除授，而公与兄庶首被识拔，并游法寺，衣冠慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214522_comment'></div>公于断狱，论议持平，人谓不冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214522_comment'></div>至刊定律令，立言寓意非法家识虑所及，故凡置局辄预，累朝刑典，悉关其手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214522_comment'></div>出刺全赵，施张纲络，如世吏师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214522_comment'></div>大姓某某以奸侠乱吏治，前二千石欲制者，辄持短长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214522_comment'></div>公疏其宿负，逮系累月，案致其罪，郡中股栗，民吏大惊，相戒毋犯公法，盖公前此未尝更民事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214522_comment'></div>达官势人荐其材者四十辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214522_comment'></div>在上党，颛以爱利为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214522_comment'></div>岁比不登，诱温户出粟廪，饿者全活万计，死者具衣槥收瘗之，遗爱至今诵民口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214522_comment'></div>在东鲁，为朝廷大兴学，岁贡贤能辟雍，复古宾兴法，公读诏奋曰：「吾邦孔孟旧里、周公封国也，修起学宫宜甲他郡」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214522_comment'></div>因撤旧宇一新之，为夏屋三百区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214522_comment'></div>间从众儒论难经训，文风大振，隶弟子籍者数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214522_comment'></div>郡事靡密烦碎，必躬亲之，结课异等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214522_comment'></div>既受代，天辅为郓州州学教授，近请之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214522_comment'></div>崇宁四年三月丁卯，以疾卒于郓，春秋六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214522_comment'></div>公天资粹和，志行高整，好延誉人，而乐人规己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214522_comment'></div>接待僚吏，施恩甚厚，有过者平镌使改，不使丽罪，人皆德之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214522_comment'></div>内行甚修，居母丧毁瘠不食盐酪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214522_comment'></div>服除，有出世间意，有父命勉仕，故讫其身惟衣疏布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214522_comment'></div>进侍亲油油翼翼，寝食不敢先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214522_comment'></div>辍奉赐班宗族之贫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1214522_comment'></div>犹子天任蚤孤，抚之尽其恩，先己子而官之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1214522_comment'></div>仕遵三尺，因俗为政，虽宽猛异施，而所临称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1214522_comment'></div>先娶清河张氏，赠旌德县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1214522_comment'></div>今夫人洛阳范氏，封崇德县君，改封永福县君，皆有贤操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1214522_comment'></div>男即天辅，好学自立，试吏部第一，举进士，又举进士，皆中第，终承直郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1214522_comment'></div>孙三人：长即温彦，次清彦、冲彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1214522_comment'></div>女适武学博士李子奇，亦屡登科选庶，今为朝请大夫、提举西京嵩山崇福宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1214522_comment'></div>天任今为朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1214522_comment'></div>以其年十月癸酉葬公开封府长垣县太平乡永宁里邓冈之南原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1214522_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1214522'>陶唐之后，中绝不续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1214522_comment'></div>武王反商，国之于祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1214522_comment'></div>单父大家，再徙韦城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1214522_comment'></div>自公显考，总国详刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1214522_comment'></div>申直颇颣，为天下平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1214522_comment'></div>骞翔要涂，公实济美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1214522_comment'></div>决狱刊令，不为峻诋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1214522_comment'></div>入为台郎，出长郡治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1214522_comment'></div>以法为师，得法外意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1214522_comment'></div>在昔仁者，子孙必兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1214522_comment'></div>于门驷马，虞胄九卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1214522_comment'></div>公躬弗羸，隐德多有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1214522_comment'></div>源深流长，实寿厥后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1214522_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年9月</a>　为侍其玮作墓志。作品：朝散大夫致仕柱国赐紫金鱼袋侍其公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1214523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214523?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散大夫致仕柱国赐紫金鱼袋侍其公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁五年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214523")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214523'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214523'>公讳玮，字良器，姓侍其氏，苏州长洲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214523_comment'></div>世序自先汉广野君之裔孙赐氏食其，后有为武帝侍中者，因又合官与氏，而称今姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214523_comment'></div>曾祖仕李氏，知吉州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214523_comment'></div>归朝，任监门卫大将军，赠左神武卫上将军，讳祯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214523_comment'></div>祖右侍禁，讳宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214523_comment'></div>考赠右正议大夫，讳泳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214523_comment'></div>家世以武显，族大且贵，闻天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214523_comment'></div>公独自刻习儒学词章，从进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214523_comment'></div>皇祐二年中第，调杭州富阳、开封阳武二县主簿，掌书记阆州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214523_comment'></div>改著作佐郎，知池州建德县，遭正议忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214523_comment'></div>服除，知光州固始县，监鄂州酒，又知吉州之永丰，签书桂阳监判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214523_comment'></div>稍迁通判全州，移刺化州，又刺池州，表请致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214523_comment'></div>积官至朝散大夫，勋柱国，赐服佩视三品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214523_comment'></div>富阳故两税局，一隶主簿，公至课辄倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214523_comment'></div>他日专征者负殿且罢斥，公悉推羡数畀之，使偿逋额，课更以最上，而公以此称长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214523_comment'></div>阳武官僚继踵坐法免，公齿少，独当大邑，风政凛然殊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214523_comment'></div>府尹包孝肃公材之，檄摄右军巡判官，至则为之尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214523_comment'></div>有亡命卒坐剽金，论弃市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214523_comment'></div>狱具，公覆视文案，疑有冤，讯得其情，白尹，为平停之，囚以不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214523_comment'></div>在职满岁，申活枉桡以十数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214523_comment'></div>济办府事，隐然名动诸公，尹滋材之，欲表为真，人谓公且阶此显仕，而公方荐所知自代，尹义而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214523_comment'></div>河水怒溢，啮埽决坏，朝廷出制使驰视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214523_comment'></div>公临水冲，料丁壮蚤莫护作，遂以塞闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214523_comment'></div>任事者皆进秩，独不自言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214523_comment'></div>在固始询求遗便，尝穿永清、南津二渠，漕粟、溉田交赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214523_comment'></div>永丰大姓持吏短长，因横恣渔食闾里，又土俗以鼠芮蛊毒杀人，公禁沮立绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214523_comment'></div>全守武人，不闲吏治，公阴为处议，每条教下自幕府，不知由公出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214523_comment'></div>化州僻陋，下车筑校舍，置师生诵说，间为拥经亲授义训，人士知趋学，自公始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214523_comment'></div>有州佐自海南代还经郡，市征者故与有仇，以匿货文致其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214523_comment'></div>公廉知状，为处平之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214523_comment'></div>州佐欲挟公修恨，则疏其宿负，求穷竟之，公亦无所听，繇此两人交德公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214523_comment'></div>因有坐至重辟者，为奉谳，得减罪一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214523_comment'></div>已而录见，辄纵出之，佐吏大惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214523_comment'></div>公曰：「是羸瘦不堪杖，杖之必死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214523_comment'></div>谳之前而杀之后，其去几何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214523_comment'></div>人服其敢为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214523_comment'></div>居六年不代，化行南土，归装无岭外一物，当世清之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214523_comment'></div>在池州，籍记桀猾主名，或犯禁辄披籍与重比，以故奸不迹境，郡中翕然称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214523_comment'></div>未几召还，遂请老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214523_comment'></div>公性靖退知足，奉公孤立介特，以质谨自将，不肯挠节媚权近，仕进淹晚，一不缀怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214523_comment'></div>夙嗜学问，喜聚书，自少讫老未尝一日去篇籍不观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214523_comment'></div>工草隶，善属文，赋诗尤多，时称佳笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214523_comment'></div>制《续千文》行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1214523_comment'></div>内行孝友加人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1214523_comment'></div>始官钱塘，迎祖母贾氏夫人以养，承颜尽其欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1214523_comment'></div>是时族千指，贾方专家政，能使忘归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1214523_comment'></div>服前后丧，皆哀臞不自胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1214523_comment'></div>吴中赀业，前推以赡同产子，晚节无所于归，因徙贯宣城，招季弟共居，视遇与己无厚薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1214523_comment'></div>退居十年，论议本忠厚，专以表善赒急为心，江左衣冠仰为轨式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1214523_comment'></div>春秋虽高，精明如壮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1214523_comment'></div>俄属疾甚微，沐浴更衣，命左右掖坐，若将寐者，泊然而逝，崇宁三年十月丙辰也，寿八十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1214523_comment'></div>五年九月丙申葬于宣城县万松山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1214523_comment'></div>母夫人王氏，太原郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1214523_comment'></div>两娶施氏，封仙居、永嘉二县君，皆有贤行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1214523_comment'></div>男六人：鈜，桂州永福县令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1214523_comment'></div>锜，前卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1214523_comment'></div>锷，通州司法参军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1214523_comment'></div>鍴、钊，举进士，皆有学守，孝谨祥顺，名能世其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1214523_comment'></div>女三人，皆嫁，婿路庆隆为左班殿直，蒋忱为藤州镡津县令，王彦思为鄂州蒲圻尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1214523_comment'></div>孙男女十三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1214523_comment'></div>某，侍其自出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1214523_comment'></div>先夫人北海君于公笃友爱，平时道公事不虚口，故其不肖子得公世次行治劳烈为详，义不敢以疵贱辞毋铭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1214523_comment'></div>因泣铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_1214523'>侍其之先，高梁启封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1214523_comment'></div>以官命氏，繇汉侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1214523_comment'></div>逮公曾祖，脱迹建业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1214523_comment'></div>以武奋功，桓桓累叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1214523_comment'></div>公以学艺，收科自躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1214523_comment'></div>与道进退，不棘于逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1214523_comment'></div>龟紫朱轮，吏二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1214523_comment'></div>岂曰不逢，未配名德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1214523_comment'></div>惟德之配，天则大之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1214523_comment'></div>康宁寿耋，子孙颀颀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1214523_comment'></div>有窾新宫，兆墨云食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1214523_comment'></div>诏万斯年，篆此幽刻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1214523_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年11月</a>　葬乃父于江阴县青玚乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a><br /></div><div class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>，36岁</div><div id='349c01f45d7d4162b072c3a0c4500d24' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3fd77b0eeb4a4dc9bd70f8efb6d13805_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3fd77b0eeb4a4dc9bd70f8efb6d13805");'><span id='3fd77b0eeb4a4dc9bd70f8efb6d13805_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>，37岁</div><div id='3fd77b0eeb4a4dc9bd70f8efb6d13805' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a><br /></div><div class='label1' id='00ff8d01b9524eb38e407228a2006d3f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("00ff8d01b9524eb38e407228a2006d3f");'><span id='00ff8d01b9524eb38e407228a2006d3f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>，38岁</div><div id='00ff8d01b9524eb38e407228a2006d3f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8937a36520dc437199b0ca19b96c5c38_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8937a36520dc437199b0ca19b96c5c38");'><span id='8937a36520dc437199b0ca19b96c5c38_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1119')">1118-1119年</a>，47-48岁</div><div id='8937a36520dc437199b0ca19b96c5c38' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1119')">1118-1119年</a><div id='poem_1214363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214363?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回王状元启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214363")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214363'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214363'>胪传上第，首冠群英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214363_comment'></div>下明诏于九天，恩先桂籍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214363_comment'></div>收大名于一日，光映儒林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214363_comment'></div>凡在见闻，孰不庆羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214363_comment'></div>恭惟某官宏材耸壑，英气凌云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214363_comment'></div>卓尔异人，时推于间出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214363_comment'></div>伟然大器，不俟于晚成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214363_comment'></div>以妙龄秀发之姿，奉高诣讲闻之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214363_comment'></div>诸老谁先夫贾傅，天子亲擢于平津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214363_comment'></div>喜黉舍之有人，掩文场而得隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214363_comment'></div>惟他日公卿之路，当由此而致吾君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214363_comment'></div>凡一时父母之心，皆闻风而祝其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214363_comment'></div>华涂方践，远业难量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214363_comment'></div>某久共齑盐，更窥珠玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214363_comment'></div>知洋洋于流水，偶赞文衡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214363_comment'></div>引皓皓于明星，实由圣鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214363_comment'></div>拥长笺而肯顾，溢陋巷以生光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214363_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1214363_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_224460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/224460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西江月<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>连水东楼燕集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_224460")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224460'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224460'>艳曲醉歌金缕，朱门高耸铜环。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224460_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224460'>中天楼观共跻攀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224460_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224460'>飞絮落花春晚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224460_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224460'>低映绿阴朱户，斜拖素练沧湾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224460_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224460'>银钩华榜五云间。<div id='poem_sentence_4_224460_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_224460'>奕奕蛟龙字绾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_224460_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_224464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/224464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西江月<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>泛舟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_224464")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224464'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224464'>靺鞨斜红带柳，琉璃涨绿平桥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224464'>人间花月见新妖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224464'>不数江南苏小。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224464_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224464'>恨寄飞花蔌蔌，情随流水迢迢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224464'>鲤鱼风送木兰桡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_224464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_224464'>回棹荒鸡报晓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_224464_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题佛本行经</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年7月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214464")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214464'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214464'>元祐庚午岁，侍先君官此邑，丁内艰，尝诵《万寿经藏》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214464_comment'></div>后二十有八年，自大司成出领宫祠，寓居，再阅《大藏》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214464_comment'></div>七月二十七日终此帙，为考光禄、妣永嘉夫人追福，时先君捐馆十四年矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1214464_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州

<div class='label1' id='1d130e3877994473afcbb8fab02b0069_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1d130e3877994473afcbb8fab02b0069");'><span id='1d130e3877994473afcbb8fab02b0069_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>，28岁</div><div id='1d130e3877994473afcbb8fab02b0069' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a><br /></div>
