-----title
兖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='86b83570024d4aecb0bb361f39f2c14a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("86b83570024d4aecb0bb361f39f2c14a");'><span id='86b83570024d4aecb0bb361f39f2c14a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，30岁</div><div id='86b83570024d4aecb0bb361f39f2c14a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span><div id='poem_1214347' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214347' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214347?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兖州教授谢到任启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214347")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214347_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214347'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214347'>横经之选，猥及愚蒙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214347_comment'></div>负策之流，众为指议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214347_comment'></div>黾勉就职，凌兢戴恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214347_comment'></div>惟熙宁元圣之嗣兴，起建业真儒而光辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214347_comment'></div>辟邪说于去圣悠远之后，照微言于举世黯闇之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214347_comment'></div>博延师产于东州，乐育儒生于北面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214347_comment'></div>乔野之俗，寖成文雅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214347_comment'></div>记诵之习，变为讨论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214347_comment'></div>矧兹洙泗之滨，上直奎娄之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214347_comment'></div>泮宫芹藻，多可荐之英才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214347_comment'></div>阙里弦歌，有相承之圣化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214347_comment'></div>广德心者尚馀多士，立公门者何止一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214347_comment'></div>宜得名流，出领教法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214347_comment'></div>而某兰陵族冷，句漏绪微，性滞少通，学僻自信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214347_comment'></div>鹏翼九万，虽妄意于远图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214347_comment'></div>鸡蹠数千，每自惭于浅植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214347_comment'></div>侵寻仕路，淹没名场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214347_comment'></div>玷一第于仪曹，粗承家学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214347_comment'></div>擢两科于政府，滥厕英游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214347_comment'></div>夤缘君相之恩，冒昧师儒之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214347_comment'></div>术非博习，贵异大知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214347_comment'></div>自愧拙艰之有馀，犹喜敩学之相长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214347_comment'></div>郑生东矣，无著录之门人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214347_comment'></div>有子避之，多献嘲之弟子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214347_comment'></div>尚祈善贷，得至终更。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1214347_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214334' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214334' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214334?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答李集正书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214334")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214334_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214334'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214334'>某愚不肖，经学行诣不能超绝等类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214334_comment'></div>谬恩推泽，使授业鲁郡，惧不振职，私懔懔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214334_comment'></div>单车始至，人士见迎者有数，独足下奋然宠以书辞，猥见褒假，且望仆以尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214334_comment'></div>顾盼剪拂之重，仆虽不敏，敢不因来示所称述而广之，以晓左右者之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214334_comment'></div>昔项橐七岁，为孔子师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214334_comment'></div>颍川荀淑，高自标待，于名士少推许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214334_comment'></div>一日见黄叔度于汝南逆旅中，竦然异之，谓曰：「子吾之师表也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214334_comment'></div>王戎之于阮步兵，祢衡之于孔北海，少皆二十岁，而相与为欢友，著事者以为美称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214334_comment'></div>盖师取四术，友求三益，年龄后先，正自不校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214334_comment'></div>足下引韩退之之辞曰：「生乎吾后，闻道也先乎吾，吾从而师之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214334_comment'></div>意谓仆年虽尚弱而宜居师表之位，顾仆何足当之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214334_comment'></div>徒以黾勉禄仕，有不得已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214334_comment'></div>昔韦中立见柳子厚于南州，欲北面就弟子列，子厚逡巡逊却不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214334_comment'></div>至退之则不然，作《进学解》以诲诸生，又为《师说》以授李氏子，抗颜为师，不顾怪骂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214334_comment'></div>夫二子以文艺卓越，同为一世宗仰，顾或抗或逊，矛盾如此，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214334_comment'></div>退之任教职，子厚居散地故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214334_comment'></div>仆虽闇滞，而代匮黉宇，苟有铢发裨补，固不敢以犬马齿少为解矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214334_comment'></div>试以一事塞雅意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214334_comment'></div>足下属词虽工，而许与不自爱，恐论议士它日不以标鉴相许也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214334_comment'></div>商、周灏噩之文章，卓然杰出于千百岁之上，圣人不生，斯文未易再睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214334_comment'></div>今以牵强酬应之文轻见比拟，不太诬乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214334_comment'></div>至论宏词，舍刘、柳而独推陆贽、裴度，甚善，是欲以名义功阀见勉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214334_comment'></div>三复叹息，谨受教矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1214334_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>上书兖州太守，请兴修学校。作品：上兖州太守书。<div id='poem_1214333' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214333' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214333?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上兖州太守书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214333")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214333'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214333'>某闻：濯金浣锦，取鱼盐则贵有求贱之势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214333_comment'></div>培山益海，资尘露则大有纳小之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214333_comment'></div>商君佐秦，气燄可炙，而赵良以苦言药之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214333_comment'></div>狄梁公峻节雅望，为唐名卿，而元行冲愿备药笼中物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214333_comment'></div>夫疏贱之士，骋辞开说以干大吏，未必无一得之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214333_comment'></div>此两士者，足以观矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214333_comment'></div>愿赐须臾之间，宿留瞽言，何知无毫釐毗助万一耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214333_comment'></div>常观昔善宰郡者，布政处事，趣时循俗，而弛张无一定之论，故力寡功倍而民歌舞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214333_comment'></div>崔郾治陕，不笞一人，及涖鄂则诛罚一不贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214333_comment'></div>其说以谓：「陕土瘠民劳，吾抚循不暇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214333_comment'></div>鄂土沃民剽，非威不能治也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214333_comment'></div>柳仲郢尹京兆，政称严明，人莫敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214333_comment'></div>及镇河南，则以宽惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214333_comment'></div>其说以谓：「辇毂之下先弹压，郡县之治本惠养也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214333_comment'></div>若二子语政，庶乎不谬通方之训矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214333_comment'></div>阁下以名士典郡，所至有异等之效，涂歌邑诵，袭满人耳，果何以得此声赵魏之间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214333_comment'></div>岂非能观察风俗、随宜制变故邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214333_comment'></div>且阁下以赵之俗剽悍而嗜寇，魁桀而侮法，赭衣满道，桴鼓相闻，故痛以法绳之，铢两之奸不舍，强梁褫气，不敢迹境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214333_comment'></div>阁下之至上党，适岁荐饥，殍者塞涂，于是推行荒政，已责缓刑，俾豪右振廪，而千里皆果腹焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214333_comment'></div>惟知缓急先后之方，故宽猛异施，而两郡各治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214333_comment'></div>及乎诏书明扬，改付东鲁，车辙未至，而闾里之士偷度臆计，以为是必致隆于学校矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214333_comment'></div>今旌麾所临之地，即古泰山、鲁二郡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214333_comment'></div>宣精在上，奎娄为文宿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214333_comment'></div>画野在下，洙泗为儒乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214333_comment'></div>阙里之堂，矍相之圃，故基遗址，历历在目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214333_comment'></div>故其俗守经学，其人多秀令，号称礼义儒学之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214333_comment'></div>凡虔命而抚封者，率以文教先焉，亦犹赵之当用猛，潞之当用宽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214333_comment'></div>今视事弥数月矣，条教既修，成令既立，彫瘵者苏矣，跋扈者戢矣，下至金谷米盐、簿领期会、仓猝冗末，无不垂省，独郡学未有半辞及焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214333_comment'></div>今斋堂倾圮，芜棘不除，生师栖栖，有陈蔡绝粮之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214333_comment'></div>阁下亦有意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214333_comment'></div>傥如朱博所谓，俟尧舜出而陈说之，则无如之何矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214333_comment'></div>昔鲁僖公旂色鸾声，亲临泮水之上，饮先生君子以酒，而顺彼长道，故淮夷徐宅，莫不来同，此前事之验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214333_comment'></div>抑又闻：论事而不远嫌者，宋人有观其邻伐不祥之木从而请俟之类也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214333_comment'></div>荐言而不俟信者，妇始入门而戒其仆无笞朴之类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214333_comment'></div>某待罪教职，望履幕之日浅，而遽贡狂直，疑若自为道地，上之则失于不待信，次之则病于不远嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214333_comment'></div>惟宽明君子谅之而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1214333_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>时州学诸生绝粮，有诗纪事。作品：诸生绝粮偶作二首示勉夫。<div id='poem_523580' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523580' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523580?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诸生绝粮偶作二首示勉夫<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523580")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523580'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523580'>庖厨落寞不堪闻，弹铗无鱼甑有尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523580'>谁识箪瓢颜氏乐，可怜鲑菜庾郎贫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523580'>固穷始合称君子，临难聊须语细人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523580'>曳褷长歌商颂在，未应怼憾去来频。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523580'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523580_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523581?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523581'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523581'>饥肠愁坐耳无闻，放饭先疑甑拾尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523581'>闻说食功非食志，政宜忧道不忧贫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523581'>佐饔但有思尝者，执爨初无欲凊人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523581'>好向计台勤自列，文移见却已频频。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523581'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523581_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span><div id='poem_523557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>学正郭勉夫示诗次韵答之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523557")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_523557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523557'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523557'>有道家声远，沉机足干时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523557'>松生非培塿，檀伐待沦漪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523557'>虎脊卑凡乘，蛾眉疾众姬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523557'>一鸣惊伍举，千里器王圭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523557'>德令温温著，名香蔼蔼驰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523557'>披庄问同异，执礼判嫌疑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523557'>操尚倾涓子，才华进客儿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523557'>适齐非鼓瑟，逃楚笑吹篪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523557'>艺苑高三绝，书庠肃五仪。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523557'>涌泉推敏思，翻水播英辞。<div id='poem_sentence_9_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_523557'>计吏趋兰省，诸生偃璧池。<div id='poem_sentence_10_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_523557'>行殊师也过，论鄙释之卑。<div id='poem_sentence_11_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_523557'>默识扳安世，多方劣惠施。<div id='poem_sentence_12_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_523557'>风标寒似玉，机警利如锥。<div id='poem_sentence_13_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_523557'>高翥千龄鹤，前知五总龟。<div id='poem_sentence_14_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_523557'>碎金珍谢傅，馀锦梦丘迟。<div id='poem_sentence_15_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_523557'>谬学邯郸步，工施浑沌眉。<div id='poem_sentence_16_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_523557'>文科将赫奕，荣路即威夷。<div id='poem_sentence_17_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_523557'>器业今为重，功勋士所期。<div id='poem_sentence_18_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_523557'>他年青竹上，凛凛看名垂。<div id='poem_sentence_19_523557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_523557'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_523557_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523558?labeling=true' target='_blank'>勉夫示诗鸣其穷甚哀因次韵答之极其贫悴之态而卒勉之以科举庶广其意也</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523558")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_523558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523558'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523558'>落落超馀子，干时命未当。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523558'>摧伤窘文阵，拓落尚书庠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523558'>賨货无山积，毛群欠谷量。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523558'>蜗庐寒不展，龙具夜何长。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523558'>牍谩三千富，年侵四十彊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523558'>有车乘下泽，无梦入高唐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523558'>藜糗甘珍荐，桑枢自峻堂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523558'>书佣跧净院，舂赁寄修廊。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523558'>异鬼时相笑，邻家许借光。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523558'>低佪涸辙鲋，进退触藩羊。<div id='poem_sentence_9_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_523558'>原宪贫非病，荣期乐处常。<div id='poem_sentence_10_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_523558'>财雄劣程郑，赀钜笑秦杨。<div id='poem_sentence_11_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_523558'>甫里田多潦，浔阳径就荒。<div id='poem_sentence_12_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_523558'>白驹嗟逸豫，黄鸟怨遗忘。<div id='poem_sentence_13_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_523558'>薪乏支离束，钱空赵壹囊。<div id='poem_sentence_14_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_523558'>晨餐烦乞米，夜读待然糠。<div id='poem_sentence_15_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_523558'>词艺闻精敏，名声已激扬。<div id='poem_sentence_16_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_523558'>登荣将赫奕，处困暂徊徨。<div id='poem_sentence_17_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_523558'>志气宜轩翥，文辞忌怨伤。<div id='poem_sentence_18_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_523558'>逐贫高赋就，丰廪换龟肠。<div id='poem_sentence_19_523558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_523558'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_523558_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e6320f7cba7242e3be2d2e775714d00b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e6320f7cba7242e3be2d2e775714d00b");'><span id='e6320f7cba7242e3be2d2e775714d00b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>，31岁</div><div id='e6320f7cba7242e3be2d2e775714d00b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　兴办学校，教育甚力。作品：与曾运使书。与运使启四首。上盐职书。<div id='poem_1214336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214336' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214336?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢曾运使书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214336")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214336'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214336'>某至愚极陋，不敢自齿于搢绅诸公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214336_comment'></div>过听谬使，敩学鲁郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214336_comment'></div>视职满岁，而经以疑质者无训发之功，文以瑕求者无诋呵之效，大惧瘝旷，以羞儒林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214336_comment'></div>惟是缮完室庐，营度稍食，窃然为诸生庇身糊口之计，姑欲杜众毁而塞吏议，如是而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214336_comment'></div>间者使车按临，始获肩随掾吏，趋走幕下，幸蒙不以常辈知遇，妄以胥宇继粟为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214336_comment'></div>退念位卑而劘上，交浅而求奢，不揣其本而惟末是图，三者皆宜得诛绝之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214336_comment'></div>心口默计，不寒自慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214336_comment'></div>敢图厚德，阔略不问，又从而听许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214336_comment'></div>意无犹豫之疑，文无勘诘之扰，一日而赒三十万，观听者惊焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214336_comment'></div>方县官经用窘急之秋，领使事营辑岁计，笼络利源，毫釐纤悉，稍可纾目前有司之急者，无不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214336_comment'></div>榷酤龙断与夫州邑之赋少阙常额，则奉职之吏望风伺指，忧虞惴慄之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214336_comment'></div>今独无功而受厚赐，自非大人君子留情风教、进诱后学，讵肯瘠彼肥此耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214336_comment'></div>洙泗乡校，有几废复兴之渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214336_comment'></div>圆冠侈袂，腾颊颂誉，皆曰上之德我者如是，不激昂奋励则为匪人，鲁道庶乎兴矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214336_comment'></div>功利之博，与三十万之费，轻重小大为如何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214336_comment'></div>若夫区区嗜学之心，不为忧米盐乱，因得卒业，又不至失职而去，此义恩及于一己，而非敢私谢者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214336_comment'></div>抑又闻士伸于知己，尚敢以一事浼听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214336_comment'></div>仙源县学赐田，岁租具在，而田无所归，甚有可并之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214336_comment'></div>阁下盛名雅望，朝廷方取信诚，能书盈尺之纸，转以上闻，不伤公私，不戾文法，其势宜必得此邦受赐，又非特三十万而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214336_comment'></div>峨峨大石，深刻颂美者不在他门，而作为声诗者亦且不胜听矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214336_comment'></div>偶进记为谢，又因以请，惟执事实图之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1214336_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上监职书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214335")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214335'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214335'>某尝闻何武行部，先即学宫，延见诸生，试其诵论，课以得失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214335_comment'></div>已乃入传舍，问垦田，见二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214335_comment'></div>其恢尚儒雅有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214335_comment'></div>又闻奇章公始随计京师，声望未白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214335_comment'></div>韩退之欲与延誉，因携皇甫持正阚亡而过之，大书其门曰：「某日愈、湜同谒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214335_comment'></div>由是僧孺之名籍籍动等辈，其成就后进有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214335_comment'></div>每涉传记，究观达人胜士所为，魁然拔俗远甚，未尝不置卷遐想，以为旷数百年未易再睹，诚不自意亲于其身而见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214335_comment'></div>恭惟阁下以聪明之才，位部刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214335_comment'></div>崇儒拔士之声，嘈嘈乎列郡，私固已藏诸胸中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214335_comment'></div>今兹车辙马足始至鲁郊，戴褷垂缨之士，方且引脰拭目以观所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214335_comment'></div>然而金谷未问也，簿领未核也，囚系未处也，牒诉未阅也，道从传呼，先临泮水之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214335_comment'></div>降舆跻阶，款谒庙室，要笏沃酹，槃躄磬折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214335_comment'></div>退即学庭，延见胄子，雍容垂接，与白屋亢礼，悼稍食之觳薄，叹室庐之颓陋，慨然有意赒而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214335_comment'></div>兹非何武之用心欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214335_comment'></div>某受性方拙，既不能激昂奋迅以为身谋，又不能喔咿俯仰以追时好，韦编棐几，自守穷约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214335_comment'></div>阁下乃欲卵而翼之，屈二天之尊，礼一介之贱，使行路指目曰：「是虽无似，然钜公尝一聘矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214335_comment'></div>吴坂之鸣，安知无三倍之价，兹非韩退之好事欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214335_comment'></div>矧自近世，达官大吏类以刀笔期会为急，至于教化本原，往往漫不屑意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214335_comment'></div>视校学之庭，则曰「此虚器也」，顾师儒之职，则曰「此左局也」，轻蔑菲薄，以儒为戏，彼又乌知三纲五常所系，而荐绅大夫所从出乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214335_comment'></div>独阁下达览深识，留情艺文，施设缓急轻重，与世异趣，瞆者警焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214335_comment'></div>洙泗儒风，将配畴曩，而于乐泮水之颂，不得专美于前日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214335_comment'></div>吾道赖以掖持，后来因之竞劝，岂特某与逢掖诸生受赐而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214335_comment'></div>爵跃蹈舞，实为天下贺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214335_comment'></div>私布腹心，惟阁下察之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1214335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　兖州新任太守祝康到任，有贺启。作品：贺兖守祝刑部启。<div id='poem_1214350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺兖守祝刑部启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214350")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214350'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214350'>奉诏十行，分符千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214350_comment'></div>凡依庇赖，共集欢欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214350_comment'></div>窃以未丧斯文，洙泗有圣人之化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214350_comment'></div>大启尔宇，龟蒙为叔父之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214350_comment'></div>矧在祥符，尝迂清跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214350_comment'></div>落成琳馆，光昭受祖之休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214350_comment'></div>登祀岱宗，诞启格天之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214350_comment'></div>在今尤为雄镇，择守必付重人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214350_comment'></div>恭惟某官雅望济时，孤忠许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214350_comment'></div>遇事奋敢为之气，祥刑推钦恤之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214350_comment'></div>凛凛清规，夙著《破邪》之论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214350_comment'></div>优优美化，久传《乐职》之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214350_comment'></div>爰从潞子之邦，改涖鲁侯之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214350_comment'></div>吏民慕德，日期抗隼之来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214350_comment'></div>僚属钦风，预喜左鱼之出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214350_comment'></div>伏念某谬悠单见，委琐凡材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214350_comment'></div>由仁义行，期敩学半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214350_comment'></div>凤凰翔千仞，分隔华途；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214350_comment'></div>鹪鹩巢一枝，自安拙宦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214350_comment'></div>侧闻命牧，窃喜事贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214350_comment'></div>倒屣以迎，固非敢冀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214350_comment'></div>敛板而进，庶或有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214350_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1214350_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　送诸生赴京应举，席上有诗次祝康韵。作品：次韵祝守康鹿鸣宴赠诸先辈（二首）<div id='poem_523596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵祝守康鹿鸣宴赠诸先辈<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523596")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523596'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523596'>清香画戟燕儒流，场籍英材喜博收。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523596'>奋袖谈辞争落落，抠衣矩步更秋秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523596'>新篇奖激华如衮，公议归怀缀若旒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523596'>蕊榜登荣即从政，定知果艺过由求。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523596'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523596_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523597?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523597'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523597'>观光六十富豪英，宾送春闱属钜卿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523597'>乐采旧知多藻茆，燕敖今喜食蒿苹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523597'>糊名选艺无私见，置醴优贤有颂声。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523597'>成就旋归充贡职，鲁人歆艳始知荣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523597'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　为《策问》数篇以课诸生。作品：策问十七篇。<div id='poem_1214472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>策问一<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>治德</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214472")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214472'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214472'>问：《传》曰：「明王即位，建大中以承天心，则庶徵序于下，日月理于上」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214472_comment'></div>又曰：「天子建中和之极，兼总条贯以顺成天庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214472_comment'></div>故善治者莫大于建中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214472_comment'></div>又曰：「天下本无事，庸人扰之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214472_comment'></div>第澄其源，何忧不简邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214472_comment'></div>又曰：「窃恨国家释乐成之业，而虚为此纷纷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214472_comment'></div>故善治者莫先于靖民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214472_comment'></div>汤之执中，舜之恭己，盛帝显王之称，煌煌于天下，率循是而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214472_comment'></div>恭惟圣天子绍祚二年于兹，精神所向，天顺之，人应之，虽庶僚百执不足仰望清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214472_comment'></div>然窃意其万一，殆专以大公至正之术待天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214472_comment'></div>纪元诏书，恳到切至，士有一言及此者，不以次而官使之，此二三子所睹闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214472_comment'></div>夫居尊而制四极，正始而虑万世，非大明法度不足以藩饰，非广延贤智不足以维持也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214472_comment'></div>今朝廷既皆知，二三子其茂明之，以著于篇，毋使问以国事，千转万变而不穷，专美方册也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1214472_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214473?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>治功</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214473'>问：盖闻上古隆治之时，俊良耆杰无不登用，奸回谀媚无不放斥，四夷宾服，百吏竞奋，黎民醇厚，风俗移易，天灾时变，昆虫草木之妖无不消弭，休符嘉瑞、麟凤龟龙之属无不备至，郊天祀地，神示顾答，跂行喙息，无不得宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214473_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214473_comment'></div>何修何饰而至此欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214473_comment'></div>本朝受命百数十年，圣圣相授，润色宏业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214473_comment'></div>以今观察治效之隆，岂尽如古邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214473_comment'></div>其未至耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214473_comment'></div>兴利之要何先？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214473_comment'></div>补弊之术何贵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214473_comment'></div>守成之道何以？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214473_comment'></div>杜患之几何务？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214473_comment'></div>诸君具言之，毋有所隐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1214473_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214474?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>治效</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214474'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214474'>问：周室之兴，岐、豳、丰、镐四易都邑，修仁累义，受命配天，积十七王至于成、康，然后兵寝圄空，号称极治，何其难耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214474_comment'></div>唐文皇仗义晋阳，不三月帝天下，投戈偃革之日未久，已能使贞观之民居者外户不阖，行者旅粮不赍，何其易耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214474_comment'></div>然周道陵夷既久，诸侯强大，莫之敢倾，郏鄏之卜，卒过其历；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214474_comment'></div>唐至天宝，海内已乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214474_comment'></div>自安史首难，悍镇骄据四十八州，乍服乍叛，讫不能有，岂治效有浅深之异，故祸乱之作亦有淹速欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214474_comment'></div>公孙弘诵语汉廷，谓周公旦治天下期年而变，尚窃迟之，则图治疑若甚易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214474_comment'></div>李石抗对便坐，谓十年养德甫成尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214474_comment'></div>天下治不治，要自今观之，则图治又若甚难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214474_comment'></div>孔子曰：「善人为邦，百年可以胜残去杀矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214474_comment'></div>治果易乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214474_comment'></div>又曰：「如有用我者，期月而已可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214474_comment'></div>治果难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214474_comment'></div>历观前世通儒上品，才议时政，亦杂然不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214474_comment'></div>或曰：「日中必熭，操刀必割」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214474_comment'></div>持是说者，其言刚果而必行，若贾谊告文帝「失今不治，必为痼疾，不肯早为，岂异秦之季世」是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214474_comment'></div>或曰：「物暴长者必夭折，功卒成者必亟坏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214474_comment'></div>持是说者，其言宽缓而不迫，若朱浮告世祖「游意经年之外，望化必世之后」是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214474_comment'></div>二端异焉，将时势使之然欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214474_comment'></div>方文思天子在上，达孝绍先猷，明德临海县，励精治道，宵旰念此至熟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214474_comment'></div>将远抚长驾，井田、肉刑，比隆三代之盛，又虑未可以岁月几也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214474_comment'></div>将兴补滞弊，持守盈成，苟图目前之治而已，又虑不足以贻则万代也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214474_comment'></div>然则奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214474_comment'></div>诸君学优智明，通达国体，其尽言之于篇，以启告愚陋，亦敩学相长之义也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1214474_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214475' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214475' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214475?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214475_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214475'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214475'>问：在昔隆治之时，分职以驭群臣，因能以裁列位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214475_comment'></div>治稷者不以涖水土之功，典礼者不以居犴狱之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214475_comment'></div>下至虞人之贱，犹知守官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214475_comment'></div>典衣之微，不敢出位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214475_comment'></div>故能同德协义，共图康功，何其盛也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214475_comment'></div>去古寖远，官制紊乱，先后失当，崇卑夺伦，序爵之功，无复可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214475_comment'></div>神宗皇帝慨然念之，远稽成周之隆，近约宇文之制，肇修废典，董正治官，始以阶定品，而省台、寺监之仪，粲然一新矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214475_comment'></div>名定而实应，职分而事举，在下者思于竞劝，居上者易于循责，品式周密，济济乎乡于六服承德之时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214475_comment'></div>今朝廷绍隆前休，增光润色，约循成书，以诏万世，盖将与唐之《六典》并驱而争光也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214475_comment'></div>议者谓曹司概补则吏有冗员，文移复重则局有滞事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214475_comment'></div>官司之迁徙太数，司徒之弊蠹未清，尚有可论者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214475_comment'></div>试条陈其端以复于上，增损更化，助成不刊之典，岂不休哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1214475_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214476?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>官方</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214476'>问：读先王之诗，考其风声气俗，士大夫廉耻行义，蔼蔼穆穆，何其盛耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214476_comment'></div>仕止之义，雍容可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214476_comment'></div>羞于夸毗以倖爵宠，故其诗曰：「靖共尔位，正直是与」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214476_comment'></div>引君当道，不以拱嘿为智，故其诗曰：「来游来歌，以矢其音」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214476_comment'></div>质实忠朴，虽在隐陋无所蔽欺，故其诗曰：「肃肃兔罝，施于中林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214476_comment'></div>赳赳武夫，公侯腹心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214476_comment'></div>勤劳营职，朝夕夙夜，故其诗曰：「黾勉从事，不敢告劳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214476_comment'></div>此其所以能振夫国是而宣赞时雍者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214476_comment'></div>以今在籍考之，垂缨褷充百执事之选者，盖钜万计，不为不盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214476_comment'></div>然射进者以奔趁衒鬻为深谋，患失者以抗直敢言为无策，以至诞谩诬伪，为罔上之奸，委靡因循，为窃食之计，殆不可缕数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214476_comment'></div>其能魁然振拔流俗之外者，亦无几人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214476_comment'></div>岂干禄之路狃于故习，讫不可变欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214476_comment'></div>将播告训敕，劝诱惩艾者未至也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214476_comment'></div>昔贾生有言，人主所托材器职业者，萃于群下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214476_comment'></div>俱亡耻，俱苟安，则国家最病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214476_comment'></div>今诸生受业学庭有日矣，其宜据古验今，议所以矫革之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214476_comment'></div>若夫庸庸守常之论，非所欲观也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1214476_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214477?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>选举</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214477'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214477'>问：掌铨总者以用人为职，能官人则振职矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214477_comment'></div>若其所以振职，不必问也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214477_comment'></div>司贡举者以取士为任，能得士则胜任矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214477_comment'></div>若其所以胜任，不必问也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214477_comment'></div>昔任昉指刘之遴谓王瞻曰：「此子学优未仕，水镜所宜甄擢」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214477_comment'></div>瞻即处以要官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214477_comment'></div>是昔之能官人者，亦因众誉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214477_comment'></div>崔郾试进士，吴武陵将杜牧《阿房赋》为疾读，郾即处以异等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214477_comment'></div>是昔之能得士者，亦采素论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214477_comment'></div>今吏部之启拟，一以资格；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214477_comment'></div>礼部之考阅，一以文辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214477_comment'></div>成法定令，付在有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214477_comment'></div>尸其事者虽达官近辅，犹不得毫釐加损也，况敢开请寄之路乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214477_comment'></div>虽足以示至公，而逢掖寒素，欲人人称其才分所宜，未必尽能如古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214477_comment'></div>议者欲少宽禁防，兼采平日之众论，以为用人取士之术，庶几已仕者无淹恤之患，未仕者无遗失之嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214477_comment'></div>不识其说可听否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214477_comment'></div>试援古推今论之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1214477_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214478?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>考察</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214478'>问：《书》曰：「无旷庶官，天工人其代之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214478_comment'></div>《语》曰：「修废官，四方之政行焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214478_comment'></div>此圣人重世之格言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214478_comment'></div>后世乃有官省则事省、事省则心清之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214478_comment'></div>盖搜罗之不精，课覈之无法，人人偷合保置而漫不营职，则虽多无益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214478_comment'></div>若夫百执事之选，皆得真才而官使之，咸修智能，效见于事，则岂以多为忧哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214478_comment'></div>仰惟主上焦劳万务，慎择庶明，不爱爵宠以示延纳，虽文王之能官，未有以过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214478_comment'></div>异时要官显级虚位弗置，与夫閒曹复员一官兼领者，今皆推择布满而联事合治矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214478_comment'></div>又增六察以纠愆违，置六尚以司服御，鹾茗有使，均输有官，建内外学校而联师儒至于数百，修山泽政令而命丞佐至于数千，皆前日所未及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214478_comment'></div>尚虑百司庶尹不孚上意，自奋于功名之涂，而奉职因循，姑为游食养望之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214478_comment'></div>不识选除之方、考课之令何修而可比于先王之盛，二三子能知之乎？</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1214478_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214479?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>取士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214479'>问：自乡举里选之法废，而以词艺取士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214479_comment'></div>略其平时而论其一日，凡流倖进，望士閒黜，非徒朝廷之深患，待举者亦病之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214479_comment'></div>裕陵稽古，欲覈实于庠序，而渐革科举沿习之弊，于是成均政令一新，广轮奂之居，丰饩廪之秩，慎师儒之选，增弟子之员，优迁补之条，重请寄之罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214479_comment'></div>以至于今，人材之成，比隆于多士济济之世，德至厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214479_comment'></div>今朝廷欲推广美意，增建州县学，择其秀出于等类者升之辟雍，论材而官之，议固已定而法则未下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214479_comment'></div>诸生试论其详，以待讲议局之采择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1214479_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214480?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span>士习</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214480'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214480'>问：古之儒者，用于君则忧君之忧，食于民则患民之患，在下而不用，则积学修身而已，固未有救乡邻之斗而代大匠之斲者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214480_comment'></div>今之儒服者，往往不能以分义自安，投罅伺隙，干时射进，追逐时好，章交公车，甚者饰游辞以诬善类，倡邪说以渎先烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214480_comment'></div>彼其居心积虑，岂真有意于整纷救弊哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214480_comment'></div>不过侥倖爵赏，偷取少顷之荣而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214480_comment'></div>迨夫时论载新，国是既定，则又尽变前日之说，而更为趋附之计，隐慝呈露，上烦司败之刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214480_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214480_comment'></div>古之所谓恒心持操者固如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214480_comment'></div>昔战国之际，处士横议，朝从暮横；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214480_comment'></div>而东京之衰，太学诸生品覈公卿，裁量执政，以成党锢之祸，皆前世弊事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214480_comment'></div>以今文明之时，教养之盛，而士无纯一之操若此，不识何以救之？</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1214480_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214481?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span>劝学</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214481'>问：通经好学，天下以邹鲁为称首，今列学士之版者殆以千计，可谓盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214481_comment'></div>郡学新书，蔽自上意，加惠学者，恩意甚宠，遵行寖久，虽十室之聚，无不揭墙壁而昭示之，业进士者皆所睹闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214481_comment'></div>是宜归心慕义，云合雾集，使泮林之上，俎豆之容，訚訚可观，弦歌之声，亹亹相属，追昔洙泗之盛，顾不韪欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214481_comment'></div>今则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214481_comment'></div>狃于宴安，志在琐屑，甘为自贼自暴之士，而恬然无不若人之耻者，尚多有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214481_comment'></div>甚者掉臂于改筑之宫，其视黉宇废兴，不啻如秦人视越人肥瘠，岂能副明天子乐育之意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214481_comment'></div>《语》曰：「学如不及，犹恐失之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214481_comment'></div>《传》曰：「怀与安，实败名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214481_comment'></div>昔人盖有轻千里而迎师、走百舍而问道者，今不出父母之邦，而得自进之学，诚非旦暮遇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214481_comment'></div>顾左计若此，独何欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214481_comment'></div>议者谓攻异端、辟邪说，徐以圣人之精义诱掖而开达，使道德性命之固有者瞭然神受，然后能乐道德而趋向之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214481_comment'></div>劝学之序当如此，诸生以为何如？</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1214481_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214482?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span>试士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214482'>问：国家三岁一下明诏，猎取天下俊杰，考其经以观其学，考其论以观其识，策之世务以观其才，其轩然秀出者，不旋踵而畀以爵位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214482_comment'></div>招延之路甚广，眷礼之意甚隆，而禁防之术似未尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214482_comment'></div>论者谓近岁场屋有四弊：不书行实，一也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214482_comment'></div>限以定数，二也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214482_comment'></div>冒名代试，三也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214482_comment'></div>挟书求售，四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214482_comment'></div>昔贾至议贡士，欲使保桑梓者乡里举，在流寓者庠序推，庶几兼得士之行实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214482_comment'></div>今徒责一日之文，而略平日之行，则可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214482_comment'></div>丁鸿议孝廉，使郡国率户二十万岁荐一人，不满则二岁一人，故能革前日不均之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214482_comment'></div>今诸郡取士，宽狭至相倍蓰，初不顾应试之数，而一切限以定额，则可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214482_comment'></div>假手旁坐，借人外助，此唐弊法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214482_comment'></div>今欲得真才，如之何不峻其防？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214482_comment'></div>陈书庭中，不肯露索，此唐异事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214482_comment'></div>今欲观记问，如之何不覈其实？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214482_comment'></div>考言选士，近在数月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214482_comment'></div>诸君智策甚高，通达国体，科选利害，讲之尤宜详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214482_comment'></div>愿悉意陈之，将以告于春官氏焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1214482_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214483?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十二 </span>富强</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214483'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214483'>问：懋化居者，理财之义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214483_comment'></div>训游惰者，强兵之术，语政者莫先焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214483_comment'></div>元丰真人修明宪法，加惠天下，凡邦邑皆置平准局，以权万货低昂，使重装富贾不得擅豪夺之柄，利源之入归于公上，此泉府治市之馀意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214483_comment'></div>或曰：设官笼货，与细民争铢两之得，似非王人布利之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214483_comment'></div>其说信乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214483_comment'></div>陪京诸道，籍剽勇之民，保伍联结，教以技击蒐阅，渐可革冗兵待哺之费，此乡遂寓军之遗法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214483_comment'></div>或曰：聚不逞之人，授之凶器，非惟妨农堕业，且虞其啸集生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214483_comment'></div>其说信乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214483_comment'></div>恭惟主上缉熙功绪，纤巨毕举，惟兹二者或置之不论，或复之未尽，其故何邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214483_comment'></div>岂时异事变，终不可恢复欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214483_comment'></div>议论之士不深覈其实，而姑为是𠴲𠴲也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214483_comment'></div>诸君通知世务，行作吏矣，利害之实其详著之，有补于今日绍隆之政，岂不休哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1214483_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214484?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十三 </span>食货</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214484_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214484'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214484'>问：生人之本，食与货而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214484_comment'></div>农能修水土之功则食足，商能兴刀布之利则货通，然后国富民实而服教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214484_comment'></div>故箕子陈《洪范》，推为八政之首，而史家亦曰道御之而王，权用之而霸，古今一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214484_comment'></div>方成周时，天子自治者止于寰内千里，而懋迁治穑之官，至不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214484_comment'></div>后世以海宇之大，生聚之富，而曾无官师及于食货之务，此民力所以多瘠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214484_comment'></div>主上以孝友之德，绍休两朝，以神明之资，励精庶政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214484_comment'></div>比诏郡邑，皆置农田市易之官，盖将挈提生灵，纳之富寿，凛凛三王之举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214484_comment'></div>今欲地无遗力，而年谷常丰，亡者使有，利者使阜，而民财不乏，不识尚有以裨朝廷之宪令者乎？</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1214484_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214485?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十四 </span>藩镇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214485'>问：唐自天宝失御，寇盗内讧，桀黠为乱，方镇割裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214485_comment'></div>史家虽具著于篇，而制御得失之方，论述犹未备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214485_comment'></div>魏博七州，传袭六姓，不沾王化者，一失于仆固怀恩，再失于马希倩，三失于李怀光，四失于马燧，五失于田布，六失于李听，其说信乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214485_comment'></div>章武以元和九年秋讨蔡，至十有二年冬十月，然后元济授首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214485_comment'></div>尝怪其以英锐绝人之资，团天下之兵，据人主之势，与三州之孺子敌，顾乃老师旷日，仅能克之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214485_comment'></div>杜牧谓由五败不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214485_comment'></div>详考事实，殆真有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214485_comment'></div>至讨成德，出入十年，叛涣之臣，讫不能羁致阙下，或谓丁未诏书赦承宗而班师者，谋失于白居易，庚辰诏承宗受地者，谋失于田弘正，其是非又何如也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214485_comment'></div>卢龙之地已复旋失，议者皆归咎崔植、杜元颖不知制将，萧俛、段文昌不知制兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214485_comment'></div>或又曰始不用裴度而用张弘靖，燕蓟所以亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214485_comment'></div>终不用裴度而视贼弗讨，蓟所以不能复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214485_comment'></div>矛盾之说，又将安据也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214485_comment'></div>会昌泽、潞之功，李德裕一人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214485_comment'></div>观其抵排浮议，要结外援，训师使整而壮，御将使专而勇，谋猷有足称者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214485_comment'></div>愿并论之，以观诸君博古之蕴焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1214485_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214486?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span>远识</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214486'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214486'>问：奸臣窃命，谀媚成俗，金匮大诰之书藏于海内，西汉所以亡也，而论者归罪张禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214486_comment'></div>阉尹擅朝，击断无讳，回天独坐之谣哗于民间，东汉所以亡也，而论者归罪胡广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214486_comment'></div>岂其偏见异说，苟欲惑众欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214486_comment'></div>将独览深识，灼见基祸之自，故探端揣本而诛之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214486_comment'></div>齐、晋之季也，晏子、叔向能预言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214486_comment'></div>吴、虢之亡也，子胥、卜偃能先见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214486_comment'></div>隋文帝靖三方之难，破五王之谋，混一南北，天下仰治，而嫡庶殽乱，房玄龄独深忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214486_comment'></div>晋武帝用张、羊之谋，仗王、杜之决，役不二时，扬、越归附，而无经国远图，何颖考独深忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214486_comment'></div>已而陵土未乾，板荡同辙，一何标鉴之明邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214486_comment'></div>且天下，大物也，基广根深，故无倾拔之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214486_comment'></div>苟且目前之安，而不思长久之计，则祸隙虽未露，而识者寒心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214486_comment'></div>方策所载，诸生讲求孰矣，悉条举以告愚陋者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1214486_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214487' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214487' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214487?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十六 </span>靖民</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214487_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214487'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214487'>问：盘瓠遗育，介恃险绝，敢以乌合之众，骚绎吾圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214487_comment'></div>虽蚍蜉蚁子，不足污刀几，然边氓一有不被浸润之泽者，上圣所戚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214487_comment'></div>于是起沈英于久废，而属以干城之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214487_comment'></div>僇任职之不虔，而诘其讳盗之因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214487_comment'></div>赫然兴师，洗涤区落，诏使节方及境，而两路之捷至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214487_comment'></div>归我旧境，锡之新名，而慎简守将以绥抚之，甚盛举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214487_comment'></div>尚虑远人归附之始，所以招怀安辑之方，备豫长久之计，有当议者，幸详著之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1214487_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214488?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十七 </span>律令</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214488'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214488'>问：律令之学，号为较易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214488_comment'></div>然区别纲条，贯通伦类，意论轻重，慎测浅深，使纤微曲折无不与邮罚相当，非积日究习者往往不能通其旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214488_comment'></div>神宗皇帝睿虑及此，始建东学以处士，张法科以取人，又命业进士者皆试律义，庶家修人习，知奉三尺以从事，且涖官弊讼之际，无致纷纭枉挠之失，而惠泽延及于齐民，虑至远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214488_comment'></div>后之议者，以谓经术儒雅自足饰吏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214488_comment'></div>隽不疑，北海一文学，而能决疑狱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214488_comment'></div>徐有功，东郡一明经，而用法无冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214488_comment'></div>至杜周、张汤辈，号明知宪令，而弄文骫法，至使人重足而立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214488_comment'></div>且吏道自有资材，何至使待举之士敝精神于末学？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214488_comment'></div>由是附律之议，废格不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214488_comment'></div>今欲取元丰之美意，附益于取士法中，二三子以为可否？</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1214488_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　与同僚子充游尧祠。作品：同子充游尧祠见交代李行正诗追李太白旧韵因亦次韵呈子充。次韵子充九日建天宁道场罢遂游尧祠。<div id='poem_523449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同子充游尧祠见交代李行正诗追用李太白旧韵因亦次韵呈子充</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523449")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523449'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523449'>俗物败人意，作吏七不堪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523449'>朅来东蒙遇欢友，角立杰出推江南。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523449'>英材百汰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>挥利刃，夷量万顷澄寒潭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523449'>弱龄文采照金殿，荏苒立境衣犹蓝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523449'>铜章来踏瑕丘鼓，邑屋欢康无疾苦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523449'>春风郊外正酣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>酣，笑指丛祠两骖舞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523449'>猛抛簿领乱回回<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作追芳哲，据《永乐大典》改）</span>，戏看油碧声如雷。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523449'>不遣韶光浪湮灭<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上两句原倒，据《永乐大典》改）</span>，桃已蒸霞柳飞雪。<div id='poem_sentence_11_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_523449'>荒郊遗趾望中来，遐想千古令人哀。<div id='poem_sentence_12_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_523449'>五斗不归俱委琐，邂逅为僚天赞我。<div id='poem_sentence_19_523449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_523449'>金兰缟纻未足誇，嵇吕命驾何其赊。<div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>，31岁</div><div id='9595721b0eb3483a93e6e25ec73b5b2a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>外舅张磐病故有祭文。作品：祭外舅张朝散文。再祭外舅文。<div id='poem_1214545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭外舅张朝散文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214545")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214545_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214545'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214545'>元丰季年，公墨谏纸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214545_comment'></div>摅忠论事，慷慨奇伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214545_comment'></div>可罢可行，曰此曰彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214545_comment'></div>逆鳞敢婴，懦者兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214545_comment'></div>流离十霜，以困自喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214545_comment'></div>绍圣简求，擢官大理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214545_comment'></div>迩臣飏言，秩中御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214545_comment'></div>帝曰汝俞，召升轩陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214545_comment'></div>开陈纚纚，朝纲国是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214545_comment'></div>帝用嘉之，言倾其耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214545_comment'></div>谓当施行，径跻华仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214545_comment'></div>如何南箕，寝成哆侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214545_comment'></div>佐郡饶阳，进尺退咫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214545_comment'></div>天不憖遗，乃终于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214545_comment'></div>惟公少时，越尚洵美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214545_comment'></div>浮念杂好，如弃尘滓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214545_comment'></div>沈涵群经，该总百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214545_comment'></div>阴阳星历，医卜方伎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214545_comment'></div>一物不知，为身之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214545_comment'></div>蓄藏既多，奋发无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214545_comment'></div>间关没身，命也天只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214545_comment'></div>昔我弱龄，从亲涟水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214545_comment'></div>公实奇之，有誉无訾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214545_comment'></div>谓器万乘，谓驹千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214545_comment'></div>恩勤绸缪，乃妻以子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214545_comment'></div>出入门墙，且踰一纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214545_comment'></div>不我鄙愚，数载抚视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214545_comment'></div>孰谓半涂，遽失凭恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214545_comment'></div>公之介妇，又实女弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214545_comment'></div>贽币未行，已隔生死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214545_comment'></div>丹旐有翻，言旋归止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214545_comment'></div>遣辞寄哀，涖濡脯几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214545_comment'></div>尚想平生，歆此嘉旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214545_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1214545_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再祭外舅文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214546")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214546_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214546'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214546'>呜呼我公，才非命值。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214546_comment'></div>襟量宏远如此，而所享止于中寿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214546_comment'></div>器业浩博如此，而所涖止于半刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214546_comment'></div>位稍进矣，而或困于左迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214546_comment'></div>上欲用矣，而中辍于浮议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214546_comment'></div>盖事之不如意者，常十之七八；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214546_comment'></div>而学之稍得施者，无百之三四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214546_comment'></div>岂志大者终落落以难合，而才高者亦峣峣而多忌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214546_comment'></div>不然，何为进方寸而退已尺，前既跋而后亦疐也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214546_comment'></div>虽然，万有俱空，百年如寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214546_comment'></div>善取名者必图不腐之传，能徼福者必计不赀之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214546_comment'></div>公之名节方光于时论，而子之仕进且都于显位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214546_comment'></div>以彼此而乘除，逮短长之不异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214546_comment'></div>然而感今悼往，不能不嘐嘐以长号者，徒以扳县联于亲懿而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214546_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214546_comment'></div>昔合好于二姓，逮濡留于三岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214546_comment'></div>荷爱育之绸缪，服胸怀之乐易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214546_comment'></div>悼从禄之崎岖，遽兴嗟于殄瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214546_comment'></div>携孥奠觞，涕盈两眦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214546_comment'></div>仰惟平生，庶其歆醉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1214546_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>送友赴试钜野。作品：送友赴试钜野送之西门时方有外舅之戚极目无聊归不得卧作诗五首却寄以风云入壮怀为韵。<div id='poem_523362' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523362' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523362?labeling=true' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523362")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523362_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523362'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523362'>三吴炊未熟，祗命挈挈东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523362'>铅刀一何补，粮食赋頖宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523362'>寥寥坐空庐，寂寞如扬雄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523362'>引脰望南境，不及马牛风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523362'>何如广文饭，终岁与子同。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523362'>年颜吾老矣，痴愚心尚童。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523362'>子虽齿发少，操行一老翁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523362'>岂独友于厚，政赖博我功。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523362'>儒玄各精诣，衮衮倾谈丛。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523362'>欲知不常处，乃在阿堵中。<div id='poem_sentence_9_523362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_523362'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_523362_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523363?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523363'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523363'>此子早树立，抗志高浮云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523363'>委蛇处州巷，颇以隽秀闻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523363'>挟书从我游，追琢益自勤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523363'>便便经与史，用志初不分。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523363'>疑篇了咄嗟，确论摧纷纭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523363'>文辞近道要，见者笔为焚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523363'>差肩鲁诸儒，蔼蔼扬清芬。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523363'>秋风济阳战，足扫千人军。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523363'>只今呼贺酒，伫子归策勋。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523363'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_523363_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523364?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523364'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523364'>寒斋篁竹间，墙屋久不葺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523364'>旁穿及上漏，雨过满床湿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523364'>忍饥哦诗书，亭午或未粒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523364'>先生自不饱，濡沫岂能及。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523364'>出门有纷奢，囊空自羞涩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523364'>世事不如意，八九更论十。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523364'>问君胡不归，肄业乃其急。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523364'>自言苦心志，更觉聪明入。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523364'>谁能学仲卿，夜抱牛衣泣。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523364'>说经已铿铿，青紫真可拾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_523364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_523364'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_523364_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_523365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523365'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523365'>寥寥里选空，龊龊士风丧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523365'>狂澜欲东之，汎滥不可障。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523365'>词场自衒鬻，相与计留放。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523365'>夸毗徒一名，倾排至千状。<div 青州

开封

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　奏赋数千言，列为第一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年11月29日</a>　父卒，丁外艰。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d968ac9d21644b46ab278c3fd8035769_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d968ac9d21644b46ab278c3fd8035769");'><span id='d968ac9d21644b46ab278c3fd8035769_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>，36岁</div><div id='d968ac9d21644b46ab278c3fd8035769' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　以拒郭天信，罢议历所提举官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='554dad3be1974aa2bddfa6812a0ad03c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("554dad3be1974aa2bddfa6812a0ad03c");'><span id='554dad3be1974aa2bddfa6812a0ad03c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>，37岁</div><div id='554dad3be1974aa2bddfa6812a0ad03c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a><div id='poem_1214357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除馆职启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214357")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214357'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214357'>芝检诞颁，猥倚褒迁之宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214357_comment'></div>兰台入直，获从英隽之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214357_comment'></div>退揣冥顽，仰惭推择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214357_comment'></div>窃以登延册府，号第一官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214357_comment'></div>䌷绎秘文，非具员吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214357_comment'></div>历观前日，率付可人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214357_comment'></div>为名流待用之途，亦华姓起家之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214357_comment'></div>故凡青钱学士，不愧赤衣诸贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214357_comment'></div>或由少讫老，而手不置书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214357_comment'></div>或自甲至丁，而卷能谈事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214357_comment'></div>或聚七千帙而考练，或课五十纸而校求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214357_comment'></div>衒瑰奇者旬日而了秘阁奥篇，自标置者三年而隔同舍共语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214357_comment'></div>图形东观，蔚为经术之宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214357_comment'></div>奏赋南郊，焕若辞华之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214357_comment'></div>以岑文本之材，而始愿止此；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214357_comment'></div>如张伯绪之望，而固求不迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214357_comment'></div>矧昭代之恢儒，幸圣皇之崇学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214357_comment'></div>显帝尧文章，而饰万物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214357_comment'></div>体周王寿考，而蒸众材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214357_comment'></div>槐市交兴，蓬山尤重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214357_comment'></div>肇新宝宇，申揭云章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214357_comment'></div>老人出授于神书，童子不忧于朋字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214357_comment'></div>荀《录》、虞《志》，拥签带之纷纭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214357_comment'></div>任笔沈诗，萃绅緌而商略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214357_comment'></div>间犹讹谬，特重校雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214357_comment'></div>言豕渡河者三，实资是正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214357_comment'></div>书马并尾而五，更在研穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214357_comment'></div>岂容素飧，以累清议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214357_comment'></div>伏念某人门具下，年位并轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214357_comment'></div>虽问学勉企于前修，而声望不高于时辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214357_comment'></div>规规求志，踽踽固穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214357_comment'></div>偶屡窃于词科，因数移于宦牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214357_comment'></div>主青衿之学校，久困齑盐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214357_comment'></div>对黄卷之圣贤，益勤铅椠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214357_comment'></div>俄婴艰棘，深自屏藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214357_comment'></div>摧伤甫逮于丧除，收召俾承于官乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214357_comment'></div>预清台之较历，佐戚邸之司宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214357_comment'></div>坐縻饩粮，毫无功阀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214357_comment'></div>何言此段，稍躐稠人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214357_comment'></div>秋熭简编，觉芸香之消蠹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214357_comment'></div>夜窥坟籍，惊藜杖之分光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214357_comment'></div>顾惟久衰多难之姿，岂图偶得傥来之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214357_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官朝廷元老，学者宗师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1214357_comment'></div>以献可替否赞时雍，以激浊扬清昭人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1214357_comment'></div>显致抡材之助，仰裨序爵之公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1214357_comment'></div>谓牛鼎烹鸡，用器固难于适称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1214357_comment'></div>然蚁封试马，历久始见于非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1214357_comment'></div>当求未见之书，更辅多闻之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1214357_comment'></div>措诸事业，庶能酬覆载之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1214357_comment'></div>作为文词，或可颂泰平之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1214357_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1214357_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='48b917f3cc0e43bc9915ee4c2e7c0b39_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("48b917f3cc0e43bc9915ee4c2e7c0b39");'><span id='48b917f3cc0e43bc9915ee4c2e7c0b39_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>，38岁</div><div id='48b917f3cc0e43bc9915ee4c2e7c0b39' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年6月</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年8月</a>　以议事不合，责知歙州休宁县，有谢表。作品：休宁知县谢上表。<div id='poem_1214296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>休宁知县谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214296")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214296'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214296'>躐厕仪曹，愧匪小材之累日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214296_comment'></div>除还铨部，犹叨大邑以庇身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214296_comment'></div>荷恩难名，报德无所<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214296_comment'></div>伏念臣人门俱下，仕学并轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214296_comment'></div>虽偶窃于科名，本自甘于州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214296_comment'></div>识拔误除于师席，编摩进直于书林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214296_comment'></div>佐贰宗英，预掌银潢之津派；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214296_comment'></div>登延册府，获窥金匮之图书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214296_comment'></div>每自疚于超踰，岂复希于擢序？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214296_comment'></div>久尸官于省户，曾乏建明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214296_comment'></div>属议礼于宗祊，遂成瘝旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214296_comment'></div>蠡何施于测海，蚊果困于负山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214296_comment'></div>特烦简礼之严，上渎冕旒之邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214296_comment'></div>止从澄汰，实戴矜容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214296_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下尧釐百工，舜明庶物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214296_comment'></div>黜陟必先于考绩，贤愚咸使之遂情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214296_comment'></div>若此无能，尚有攸处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214296_comment'></div>臣敢不承流宣化，勉报政于三年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214296_comment'></div>念咎省愆，誓输忠于九死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214296_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1214296_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d03fa0a5362742e3802c62a8ca125dfb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d03fa0a5362742e3802c62a8ca125dfb");'><span id='d03fa0a5362742e3802c62a8ca125dfb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1118')">1113-1118年</a>，42-47岁</div><div id='d03fa0a5362742e3802c62a8ca125dfb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1114')">1113-1114年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年9月</a>　纂《太常因革礼》三百卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1118')">1114-1118年</a><div id='poem_1214520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝奉大夫吴公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214520")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214520'>崇宁三年十月某甲子，天子临幸太学，既奠谒先圣，退即论堂延见师生，正坐听讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214520_comment'></div>时钱塘吴公为国子司业，被召讲《易·大有》，析理入微，音吐鸿畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214520_comment'></div>上咨异之，顾辅臣称其邃于学术，就锡金紫服，且进官一列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214520_comment'></div>不旬日，召试制诰，奏篇合旨，躐拜中书舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214520_comment'></div>公入谢，上曰：「佐教府而除书命，前此未有也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214520_comment'></div>方是时，庠序之教外薄海县，贤能宾贡云集京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214520_comment'></div>车驾大昕视学，官上舍生十六人，馀推恩有差，以风四方，而公师儒，首被奖擢，寘身严近，名誉尊显，一时衣冠歆艳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214520_comment'></div>公讳絪，字子进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214520_comment'></div>少委节学问，强记该览，本丰源衍，文辞立就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214520_comment'></div>熙宁九年擢第，调滁州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214520_comment'></div>公以业进士而得学究出身，非其志也，去之，再试有司，两居第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214520_comment'></div>复预廷试，神宗嘉其志，因诏下第并赐同进士，著为令，自公始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214520_comment'></div>调应天府户曹，朔部漕臣辟管勾纲运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214520_comment'></div>时常平书始颁，郡邑吏若民率未晓科旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214520_comment'></div>公著为论说，明示天子德意，识者韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214520_comment'></div>元丰初遴简中外校官，始为试法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214520_comment'></div>公献所为文，得召试；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214520_comment'></div>坐试席者百数，廑以四人名闻，公为选首，学者讲诵其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214520_comment'></div>除太学正，迁博士，改宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214520_comment'></div>丁外艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214520_comment'></div>服除，元祐初出教授齐州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214520_comment'></div>未几，遭母夫人忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214520_comment'></div>服除，又教授苏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214520_comment'></div>颛以经术诱接人士，每曰：「圣人微言具六籍，岂宜猥徇时俗而辍，自为废堕」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214520_comment'></div>追时好者皆笑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214520_comment'></div>逮绍圣初，再以博士召，岁馀迁太常博士，序迁丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214520_comment'></div>建议天子事七世宗无常数，仁宗、神宗功德盛大，宜为帝者百世不毁之庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214520_comment'></div>言当上意，下有司施行，特降玺书奖谕。<div class='inline'
