id='poem_sentence_27_1214520_comment'></div>后还复顺祖增置九庙，议实自公发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214520_comment'></div>哲宗、钦慈二后复主祔庙，屡抗大议，虽咈众逆指，弗顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214520_comment'></div>入尚书省，为屯田员外郎，俄易主客，遂迁司业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214520_comment'></div>学术行谊为诸生横表，著录者数千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214520_comment'></div>其为训词，深厚绵密，称进贬退，白黑分明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214520_comment'></div>未几，以显谟阁待制知湖州，纲纪张设如世吏师，讼銗益简，庭无逋事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214520_comment'></div>老吏骇伏曰：「尝未治郡，所为乃若此耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214520_comment'></div>俄属疾，召诸子曰：「四体不支，大期迫矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214520_comment'></div>为我求谢事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214520_comment'></div>语竟，奄然而逝，大观三年三月某日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214520_comment'></div>公夙与学佛者游，领悟密谛，故属纩神宇不乱，年五十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214520_comment'></div>官五迁为朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214520_comment'></div>讣闻，上为悯恻，特赠官五等，优以赙赠，敕有司护办丧事，以官舍处其孥，且特官其子若干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214520_comment'></div>惟吴氏世序有讳公约者仕唐僖宗，为台、信二州刺史，晚家杭之硖石，于公为五世祖，故公为硖石人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214520_comment'></div>曾大父廷赟、大父熙之，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1214520_comment'></div>父戣，以进士推恩调江宁府溧水簿，以公恩赠朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1214520_comment'></div>初，硖石未有学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1214520_comment'></div>朝散始择里之秀良，励使为学，一方趋从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1214520_comment'></div>后不数年，文学之士继出，而公独先贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1214520_comment'></div>公性湛静，不汲汲显仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1214520_comment'></div>分教太学生，出入十五年，官奉常积七岁不迁，未尝有坎𡒄滞淹之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1214520_comment'></div>已而进位显剧，每入对，辄逡巡求去，当世以是高之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1214520_comment'></div>娶太原王氏，封某县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1214520_comment'></div>男长曰序宾，某官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1214520_comment'></div>次曰次宾，擢进士第，皆有学守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1214520_comment'></div>女长适某官王涛，次适某官惠柔民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1214520_comment'></div>诸孤以某年某月葬公于某县某乡之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1214520_comment'></div>以予雅素且职太史，见诿以铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1214520_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1214520'>朅朅吴公，道贯六学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1214520_comment'></div>纂辞射科，屡见头角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1214520_comment'></div>说经雍泮，铿铿岳岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1214520_comment'></div>遂司胄子，斯文所托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1214520_comment'></div>乘舆来临，劝讲帏幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1214520_comment'></div>帝曰惟尔，多闻守约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1214520_comment'></div>其代予言，往持从橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1214520_comment'></div>殒于一麾，恤典优渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1214520_comment'></div>铭以昭之，死者可作。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1214520_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免太子右谕德劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214255")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214255'>臣伏睹御笔，特除臣兼太子右谕德者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214255_comment'></div>蝼蚁疏贱之臣，滥膺圣擢，循省恐悸，不知所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214255_comment'></div>窃以有周盛时，妙简贤智之臣，以陪辅世子，使日闻正言，躬履正道，如召公、史佚之伦，乃得为之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214255_comment'></div>下至导谕之官，盖亦未尝不艰其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214255_comment'></div>恭惟陛下盛德大业，卓冠古初，浚发明断，肇建储位，将以中春令日，发册路寝，亲御燕閒，推择僚寀，而臣闇劣，亦叩头中选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214255_comment'></div>惟谕德之官，委属攸重，非天下端士博闻有道术者，岂称拔举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214255_comment'></div>伏念臣学识行诣无以加人，虽屡尘科选，荐被使令，而琐琐碌碌，讫无铢发之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214255_comment'></div>今又超躐，使赞德春闱，虽仰戴君父生成之恩，而退自省量，大惧上玷明公登选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214255_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特寝成命，改授隽杰，使朝廷无虚授之嫌，微臣免倖进之诮，岂胜大愿！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214255_comment'></div>重念臣官卑，在法不当辞宠，迫于私义，不敢辄贪非据，谨冒昧自列，干渎天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214255_comment'></div>臣无任陨越俟命之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1214255_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孝论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214491")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214491'>分之所赋有贵贱，而孝亦有等差；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214491_comment'></div>性之所造有浅深，而孝亦有大小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214491_comment'></div>孔子以天子、诸侯、卿大夫、士、庶人之孝，列为五等，著之于经，此所谓分有贵贱而孝亦有等差也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214491_comment'></div>若夫性之所造有浅深，而孝亦有大小，自《论语》观之，可得而言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214491_comment'></div>夫孝，天之经，地之义，在人虽为不学之良能，不虑之良知，然扩充于心，效见于事，岂能无辨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214491_comment'></div>是故贤人之孝则异众人矣，圣人之孝则异贤人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214491_comment'></div>承颜顺志而礼无违于事死，孟懿子未必能知此也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214491_comment'></div>举足不敢忘父母，故非礼勿动，出言不敢忘父母，故非礼勿言，疾病之外不当贻亲之忧，孟武伯未必能知此也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214491_comment'></div>尽孝敬之道而不以养口体为贵，子游未必能知此也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214491_comment'></div>尽孝爱之道而不以有酒食为先，子夏未必能知此也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214491_comment'></div>有父兄在，闻不可遽行，子路未必能知此也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214491_comment'></div>一朝之忿，忘其身以及其亲，樊迟未必能戒此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214491_comment'></div>是数子者性之所造尚浅，故犹待圣人谆谆以诲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214491_comment'></div>若夫贤人之孝，则进乎此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214491_comment'></div>德行素修，名誉素著，交游称之，朋友信之，人虽欲间于父母昆弟之言而不得也，若闵子骞者能之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214491_comment'></div>父母全而生之，子全而归之，身体发肤不敢毁伤，不以且死为忧，而以得免手足之伤为幸，若曾子者能之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214491_comment'></div>是二子所谓贤人之孝者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214491_comment'></div>若夫圣人之孝，则大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214491_comment'></div>达而在上者莫如禹，穷而在下者莫如孔子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214491_comment'></div>有四海之奉而礼自贬于一身，以一身之微而化可孚于四海，是二人者岂贤人所能及哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214491_comment'></div>人之情，饮食欲厚也，禹则菲饮食以自奉而致孝乎鬼神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214491_comment'></div>衣服欲美也，禹则恶衣服而致美乎黻冕，谓不如是则不足为民主也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214491_comment'></div>此所谓有四海之奉而礼自贬于一身者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214491_comment'></div>入则事父兄，而孝弟之化移于阙里，其自处则曰：「孝乎惟孝，友于兄弟，施于有政，是亦为政，奚其为为政」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214491_comment'></div>可谓以一身之微而化孚于四海者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214491_comment'></div>《记》曰：「小孝用力，中孝用劳，大孝不匮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214491_comment'></div>其是之谓与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214491_comment'></div>《语》载孔子论孝凡十有四，因论其小大浅深之序如此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1214491_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>学论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214492")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214492'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214492'>孔子以天纵之圣，兆于变化，而木铎一世，凡道之妙，皆不勉而中，岂待学哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214492_comment'></div>其自称盖尝曰「默而识之」，则道不待于言传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214492_comment'></div>「一以贯之」，则道不涉于多见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214492_comment'></div>然《论语》之书载其好学特详者，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214492_comment'></div>盖圣人之言所以为中人法，圣人恐天下后世以己为将圣不可跂及而遂惰于学也，故为说曰：「我非生而知之者，好古敏以求之者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214492_comment'></div>盖学而加以敏求，则就效速矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214492_comment'></div>又曰：「若圣与仁，则吾岂敢？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214492_comment'></div>抑为之不厌，可谓云尔已矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214492_comment'></div>盖学而抑之以不厌，则用心刚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214492_comment'></div>以世之学常失于躐等，故为之说曰：「吾十有五而志于学，三十而立」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214492_comment'></div>示进道当渐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214492_comment'></div>以人之患每失于自惰，故又为之说曰：「吾尝终日不食，终夜不寝，以思，无益，不如学也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214492_comment'></div>示入道当以诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214492_comment'></div>文武之道，贤者识其大，则固可宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214492_comment'></div>不贤者识其小，则亦未易弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214492_comment'></div>故子贡曰：「夫子焉不学，而亦何尝师之有」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214492_comment'></div>示求道当以广也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214492_comment'></div>所造者深，则不可以一指名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214492_comment'></div>所成者大，则不可以一言蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214492_comment'></div>故达巷乡党人曰：「大哉孔子！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214492_comment'></div>博学而无所成名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214492_comment'></div>示体道当以全也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214492_comment'></div>以生知之圣，犹强学如此，况中人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214492_comment'></div>圣人所以为天下后世计者深矣，故劝学者之说，载于《语》者凡三十六，而不为复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214492_comment'></div>其曰「学而时习之」，则亦贵渐之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214492_comment'></div>其曰「学如不及，犹恐失之」，则亦贵诚之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214492_comment'></div>其曰「就有道而正焉，可谓好学」，则亦贵广之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214492_comment'></div>其曰「三年学不至于谷，不易得也」，则亦贵全之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214492_comment'></div>是故于颜渊、孔文子好学则称而美之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214492_comment'></div>于子路之六蔽、伯鱼之《诗》、《礼》则诱而进之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214492_comment'></div>宰我昼寝、冉有自画则辞而辟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214492_comment'></div>其大要欲学者日趋圣域而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214492_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214492_comment'></div>后之学者可不勉与！</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1214492_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214493' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214493' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214493?labeling=true' target='_blank'>齐论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214493")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214493_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214493'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214493'>昔太公望钓海滨而夹辅周室，武王国之强齐，使表东海，其丰功盛德，必有大过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214493_comment'></div>而司马迁为《齐世家》，言文王拘羑里，太公求美女奇物献之于纣以赎西伯，西伯归而与吕尚阴谋修德以倾商政，其事多兵权与奇计焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214493_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214493_comment'></div>审如此，则《诗》、《书》所载反妄耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214493_comment'></div>且太公之嫉纣而欲亡之者，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214493_comment'></div>为其侈丽淫湎而毒天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214493_comment'></div>使其一旦幡然悔悟，咎前之为，更为善政，以幸天下，则岂不偃兵息谋，恬然臣服之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214493_comment'></div>讵肯以尤物蛊其心而稔其恶乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214493_comment'></div>且太公之过纣也，曰收天下美女、金宝、缯帛也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214493_comment'></div>武王之过纣也，曰作奇技淫巧以说妇人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214493_comment'></div>如是而以货色惑之，是助其亡道，抱薪救火也，其贤于纣几何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214493_comment'></div>又况陷君于恶，而己则图利，太公讵忍为之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214493_comment'></div>藉使太公为之，文王其安受之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214493_comment'></div>尝闻秦以女乐间戎矣，又闻吴以珍货惑魏矣，未闻圣贤亦为是诡谲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214493_comment'></div>此迁之缪一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214493_comment'></div>夫纣之积恶久矣，文王积善亦久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214493_comment'></div>上帝下民，去彼而就此，非一日也，孰谓阴谋修德以倾商政哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214493_comment'></div>《诗》言「周世世修德，莫若文王」，则是周之德不待商而修也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214493_comment'></div>《书》曰：「独夫纣，洪惟作威，乃汝世仇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214493_comment'></div>则是商之政不待周而倾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214493_comment'></div>今奈何曰「阴谋修德以倾商政」耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214493_comment'></div>夫在己之德则修之而使人附，在人之政则倾之而使众离，是乃田常、王莽篡齐盗汉之术尔，太公岂肯以是导文王乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214493_comment'></div>此迁之缪二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214493_comment'></div>且纣有臣亿万，武王乱臣十人而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214493_comment'></div>纣兵七十万，武王虎贲三千而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214493_comment'></div>然而牧野之战，前徒倒戈而势若拉朽者，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214493_comment'></div>逆顺之势异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214493_comment'></div>太公虽有兵权何所施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214493_comment'></div>虽有奇计安所用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214493_comment'></div>尝观《六韬》万有馀言，祗皆修仁、行义、听谏、用贤之说尔，虽有《阴谋》之篇，而惟以戒惧谦下为言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214493_comment'></div>今奈何曰「多兵权与奇计」乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214493_comment'></div>此迁之缪三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214493_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214493_comment'></div>迁之言必有稽證，然百子虚滥之说，不能力断而力排之，猥存诸书以传疑于后，亦迁之过也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1214493_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南齐论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214494")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214494'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214494'>人君恢廓大度以御臣下，示以赤心，无或疑间，则人人感说，争为报效，虽有奸邪，化为忠顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214494_comment'></div>苟或猜忌刻薄，不情多诈，横诛滥罚，逆防祸患，则人人惴慄，怀不自安，虽有忠顺，化为奸邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214494_comment'></div>此理之必至，事之固然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214494_comment'></div>昔者齐明帝以宗属辅政，首废二帝，攘神器而有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214494_comment'></div>鳃鳃然畏异世之后，旁枝疏派袭己之迹而帝天下者，非其子孙也，于是包藏祸心，剿灭同姓，违显达之忠谋，而入遥光之伪策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214494_comment'></div>凡意所忌，不戮不已，使高、武诸孙，无复遗育，连颈受戮无虑六十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214494_comment'></div>煮椒之酷，燔香之伪，有出于委巷小人所不为者，而偃然为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214494_comment'></div>其心遂以为基业之固，晏然如日在天，不足经虑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214494_comment'></div>不知身死肉未及寒，而建业以墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214494_comment'></div>其首兵倡乱者，不在他姓，而乃在宗藩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214494_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214494_comment'></div>猜虐之虑果有益，而未然之变果可曲防乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214494_comment'></div>昔我先王，并建宗英，贵以爵位，使之犬牙相制，以捍王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214494_comment'></div>居无事之时，国邑茅社错峙环列，不失亲亲之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214494_comment'></div>假设不幸一国弄兵，则纠合众援，环而攻之，鲜不胜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214494_comment'></div>观萧衍之起也，下郢、鲁如摧枯，定浔阳如沃雪，桴旝所临，莫不褫溃，东墉新垒，以次归降，则以无所畏惮而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214494_comment'></div>乡使江夏不诛，衡阳犹在，河东之属噍类或存，则缓急之际，岂无义勇奋发、以身许国者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214494_comment'></div>精兵毅卒循江而守，长棘劲铩望焱而奋，则萧衍虽善兵，齐犹未亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214494_comment'></div>又况梁武之兴，虽曰仗义，然本以复前世之仇而澡私户之耻耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214494_comment'></div>则夫明帝之猜虑果利乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214494_comment'></div>果害乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214494_comment'></div>昔宋欲去群公子，乐豫以为不可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214494_comment'></div>晋大灭宗室，叔向知公室之将卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214494_comment'></div>盖枝叶既落，则本根无所庇覆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214494_comment'></div>股肱既刈，则胸臆不能独存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214494_comment'></div>是以君子知王族之重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214494_comment'></div>有齐之亡，非东昏之罪，实明帝取之尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1214494_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梁论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214495")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214495'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214495'>古之兴王既定天下，莫不创立典宪，维持后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214495_comment'></div>迨其末涂，子孙骄傲，忘其先祖艰难，然后残命亡世，殆其国家，盖自三代以下皆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214495_comment'></div>至躬创大业而昧于持守，祸乱四作，亲于其身者，一梁武帝耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214495_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214495_comment'></div>武帝起襄阳，褰裳奋袂，矜夸前功，心侈意广，经略注措，颠倒谬戾，凡季世昏主之迹，皆取而践之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214495_comment'></div>则国之颠覆，不俟异世宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214495_comment'></div>寻其弃违嘉谋，妖梦是践，弗戒洛口之奔，弗监冯亭之祸，而招纳河南之叛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214495_comment'></div>既已王之矣，而携贰于心，衰其礼遇，结好齐国，欲止而归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214495_comment'></div>彼非偶人，能无愤怨于心乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214495_comment'></div>已而封豕长蛇，突我黄屋，又不能破以奇谋而羁以胜算，徒拱手端然以待覆灭，低回纡郁，竟瘐死于台城，其干略安在哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214495_comment'></div>且武帝享御四十八载矣，械用犀利，宜倍于檀溪，武旅精强，宜加于全雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214495_comment'></div>往以人臣弄兵，以逆攻顺而有济；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214495_comment'></div>今以人君问罪，以顺讨逆而无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214495_comment'></div>往以一镇之弱而取天下，今以天下之强而不能平一镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214495_comment'></div>是岂取之易而守之难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214495_comment'></div>特始勤终怠故耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214495_comment'></div>且其平日信仗者，朱异也，而缓急非可用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214495_comment'></div>平日依凭者，柳仲礼也，而将略非所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214495_comment'></div>异时耽味于内典，而无益于攻战之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214495_comment'></div>异时信向于桑门，而难驱于兵刃之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214495_comment'></div>则太清之祸，其谁御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214495_comment'></div>乡使移三蠹之宠以礼谋臣，回同泰之费以结士卒，沈约辈不以才诛，刘显等不以能黜，则虽百侯景亦可谈笑而臣之，何至仓皇失图而身以僇没也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214495_comment'></div>其后简文幽于永福，元帝覆于江陵，方智迫于陈氏，三世皆不得其死，祀亦不传，则以创业之不善耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214495_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214495_comment'></div>创业以治，犹惧其乱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214495_comment'></div>创业以乱，则再传而遂亡，犹为幸也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1214495_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214496")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214496'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214496'>兵无常机，亦有成算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214496_comment'></div>审乎此者，善用兵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214496_comment'></div>凡伐国之兵利速战，速战则主必摧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214496_comment'></div>凡却敌之兵利持久，持久则客必溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214496_comment'></div>比在兵法，必胜计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214496_comment'></div>昔崔乾祐之攻潼关，哥舒翰曰：「贼远来，思亟战，王师必坚守」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214496_comment'></div>不幸牵制于权臣，遽与之战，哥舒果败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214496_comment'></div>仆固怀恩之寇奉天也，郭尚父曰：「彼深入，思亟战；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214496_comment'></div>吾缓之，当自携贰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214496_comment'></div>于是坚壁待之，尚父果胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214496_comment'></div>观二子之事，则陈、隋之计可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214496_comment'></div>开皇之伐陈也，扫境即戎兵五十万，是谓动众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214496_comment'></div>八道并进，浮江千里，是谓深入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214496_comment'></div>势如风霆，飘忽振荡，所向辄下，遂逼都境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214496_comment'></div>为隋计者，固宜因利乘便而扫平之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214496_comment'></div>陈人诚能出轻锐之兵，北据蒋山，南断淮水，闭关坚垒，案甲养威，为持久之计以挫之，则江左之地，庶几保有，宗庙之祀，未当绝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214496_comment'></div>盖方是时，资储尚富，义勇尚强，台城坚完，未易可破。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214496_comment'></div>彼以孤军深践吾境，相持既久，势必困敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214496_comment'></div>馈饷之费能无乏绝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214496_comment'></div>精锐之气能不沮伤乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214496_comment'></div>根本隔远，能无内顾之忧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214496_comment'></div>师老兵疲，能无弃甲之念乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214496_comment'></div>吾之镇戍岂无入援之人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214496_comment'></div>俟其引归，徐以奇兵邀击归路，彼前不得斗，退不得还，不败何待？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214496_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214496_comment'></div>食肉满朝，而皆昧于良画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214496_comment'></div>任忠、司马消难皆进是谋矣，惜乎弃不可弃之忠言，听不可听之谬算，付文庆以经略，仗孔范以机要，骤举轻发，争锋于一日之间，阵未及整而师已北矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214496_comment'></div>使高祖艰难之业，剪焉倾坠，壤地数千里入之长安，为天下笑，宁不痛哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214496_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214496_comment'></div>以叔宝之愚，畏懦退缩，奇娆淫昏，介恃天堑以傲大国，则压境之祸固有以召之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214496_comment'></div>一旦临大利害，方且效儿女曹，昼夜涕泣，为坠井自全之计，又乌足责望以经国长算哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214496_comment'></div>然愚深恨当时之失谋，在兵法可不败，故慷慨而论之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1214496_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论彰义</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214498")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214498'>宪宗以元和九年秋讨，至十有二年冬十一月然后元济就独柳之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214498_comment'></div>尝私怪宪宗以英锐之资而制一孺子，据上人之势而讨一叛臣，圜天下之兵而搏蚍蜉蚁子之聚，将李愬、光颜之朋而与赵玉、仁清为敌，当吴、蜀、江东、泽潞、易定、魏博厎平之后，破竹迎刃之势，而致讨于蕞尔之三州，碫石投卵，未足为易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214498_comment'></div>宜其咄嗟谈笑之间，摧灭破荡，顾乃涉四年而后定，尝窃迟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214498_comment'></div>论者曰自希烈盗蔡而少诚踵之，弥四十年，民不知天子之恩泽，习暴掠，嗜搏斗，宛然有夷貊风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214498_comment'></div>又赵翼其北，承宗为之援，齐隐其东，师道为之谋，内恃陂浸以为阻，是以拿兵累年，官军仅克其一县，厎定若此艰难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214498_comment'></div>尝窃迹其事，政以当时庙堂有二失五败而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214498_comment'></div>讨蔡之役未竟，而堂堂之师又出于镇、冀之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214498_comment'></div>于时李绛谓蔡镇不可并取，韦贯之请释镇州专力淮西，张弘靖谓戎事并兴，鲜克有济，请俟淮西平乃治承宗，而谋适不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214498_comment'></div>方且命刘总兴武强之役，诿郗士美举柏乡之战，是以势分力屈，兵不坚决，其失一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214498_comment'></div>李逢吉险谲，王涯暗沓，非惟才识不足属大事，且忌裴度有功，阴图阻止，排抵中伤，訾訾百绪，而帝不之察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214498_comment'></div>顾使与度并肩当国，由是二子得与钱徽、萧俛辈共为首鼠，而屡有休师之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214498_comment'></div>逮至十二年，逢吉始罢，十三年涯始出，不既晚耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214498_comment'></div>其失二矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214498_comment'></div>杜牧论兵，谓元和诛蔡，天下乾耗，四岁不能取，由五败不去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214498_comment'></div>寻牧之言，诚中时病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214498_comment'></div>当是时，调兵诸道，名为客军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214498_comment'></div>每战，客军居前，主人在后，志羸力弱，多致败衄，此董重质所深恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214498_comment'></div>则牧以不蒐练为一败，信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214498_comment'></div>韩愈请四道置兵，道率三万，乘时逐利，一日俱纵，则蔡首尾不救，可以责功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214498_comment'></div>吴武陵欲分三大将环贼而屯，以实期授濒蔡诸将，而以三期绐贼，皆指日破贼计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214498_comment'></div>而不议出此，是以师老兵屈，饷亿不继，天子至出禁钱以赡军，程异讽诸路输货，李鄘先诸道籍府库，皇甫镈且因是得宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214498_comment'></div>则牧以不责实料食为二败，信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214498_comment'></div>韩弘为都统，以官齐王锷为耻，陈书自列，遽授司徒，班锷上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214498_comment'></div>他时诸将告捷，辄累日不怡，逗挠若此，而受赏每与诸将埒，虽裴度犹畏之，至避「更张琴瑟」之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214498_comment'></div>则牧以赏重为三败，信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214498_comment'></div>袁滋去斥堠，与贼通好，六月无功，而止贬为刺史；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214498_comment'></div>高霞寓轻悍寡谋，统制不善，败于铁城，而旋召为将军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214498_comment'></div>严绶有磁丘之衄，令狐通有马塘之败，而未闻斥责以励将卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214498_comment'></div>则牧以轻罚为四败，信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214498_comment'></div>崔峻为监军，李义成为制将，谋画不同，进退掣肘，一曰为偃月，一曰为鱼丽，三军万夫，目翔惝恍之间，贼骑之来，每至折北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214498_comment'></div>则牧以不专任责成为五败，信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214498_comment'></div>乡使二失五败无可议之迹，则缓不过岁月无蔡州矣，何至旷日持久而后胜，相府有横尸之祸，陵戟有燔毁之辱乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214498_comment'></div>议者徒见德宗合十六道兵以讨少诚，溵河、广利、五楼之役相次而败，尺地一级无得焉，未几怵韦皋之说，听贾耽之计，而复其官封，终其身不能臣也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214498_comment'></div>宪宗由裴度而得李愬，由愬而得王士良，而得吴秀琳，由秀琳而得李祐，遂定袭蔡之谋而赤叛者之族，遂以德宗为稔寇，宪宗为成功，殊不知宪宗特贤于德宗耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1214498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1214498'><span class='label'>《兵法》：</span>「有役不再籍。」宪宗何预也？《丹阳集》卷七。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1214498_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1214500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论卢龙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214500")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214500'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214500'>丰爵秩以塞其侥觊之心，峻绳检以抑其豪锐之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214500_comment'></div>知是说者，知御将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214500_comment'></div>无事而蒐练，则警急有备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214500_comment'></div>平居而抚养，则仓猝可使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214500_comment'></div>知是说者，知制兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214500_comment'></div>今夫载笔之士，追咎长庆之失，皆曰崔植、杜元颖不知御将，萧俛、段文昌不知制兵，由是燕蓟之地已得而更失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214500_comment'></div>刘总挈八州效顺，惧部将溃乱，先籍朱克融辈送京师，欲朝廷划疆土处之，使北方歆艳其宠，不复甘乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214500_comment'></div>当时柄庙算者虑不经远，徒知五两半通之命为可爱，而不知慰其羁踬之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214500_comment'></div>既又弛槛緤而纵豺虎，由是克融披撅不可制，实崔、杜二子之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214500_comment'></div>穆宗初，两河无虞，遽议偃革，建请天下镇兵，岁俾十之一为逃死不补，谓之销兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214500_comment'></div>既而籍卒逋散，啸聚为盗，克融一日收用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214500_comment'></div>朝廷募乌合充战，疲琐不能支敌，遂失河朔，实萧、段二子之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214500_comment'></div>愚以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214500_comment'></div>盖始不用裴度而用张弘靖，卢龙所以亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214500_comment'></div>终不用裴度而视贼不讨，卢龙所以不能复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214500_comment'></div>就使当时无御将处兵之失，碣石之野亦未必不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214500_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214500_comment'></div>张弘靖傲虐自肆，燕人苦之，于是囚之蓟门而挟众乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214500_comment'></div>彼所欲逐者，弘靖耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214500_comment'></div>克融虽不北还，彼谓军中不可一日无帅，将不取豪健得众者擅立乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214500_comment'></div>又况弘靖之囚也，众请朱洄为帅，谢老疾而后以其子克融领军务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214500_comment'></div>使朝廷徇总之请，而以钜封剧镇付之克融，则洄且自为之矣，父子影会，举兵连衡，祸未必不更大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214500_comment'></div>故愚以为崔植、杜元颖之失，未必能致乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214500_comment'></div>元和十五年正月，俛、文昌始当国，明年七月克融已叛，销兵之议甫一岁耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214500_comment'></div>十分天下之镇兵而不补其一，又始二岁，失职者未甚夥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214500_comment'></div>王廷凑同时反赵，亦收用之，则克融所得又其半耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214500_comment'></div>克融有畔涣之志，虽无失职之兵，岂不啸引凶党用之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214500_comment'></div>李怀仙、朱滔犯顺，亦岂因朝廷所销之兵耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214500_comment'></div>又况克融拱手安步，坐享旄节，朝廷未尝致讨，而克融初不用兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214500_comment'></div>故愚以为萧俛、段文昌之失，未必能致乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214500_comment'></div>然则一日而亡地数千里，由不用裴度，而刘总入朝，请折八州为三道以弱燕蓟之势，其策固善，至请以弘靖、卢士玫、薛平分治之，则用人固已疏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214500_comment'></div>奈何弃度不用，又全以总地宠之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214500_comment'></div>弘靖之帅幽州也，不能因俗制变，遂致军乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214500_comment'></div>彼魏始降而度往宣慰也，遍至属部，扬天子恩泽，魏人欢服，使之代总，必不肯如弘靖朘削军费，取缗钱二十万供私费矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214500_comment'></div>蔡始平而度往视也，以蔡牙卒侍帐下，使之代总，必不肯如弘靖肩舆障盖，与士卒殊劳逸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214500_comment'></div>度尝建请私第见士，延俊英，访筹策，必不肯委成参佐，旬一决事，罕见将吏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214500_comment'></div>度之入蔡，悉除元济偶语馈遗之禁，必不肯专以刑法根治吏士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214500_comment'></div>总之降也，诚能起度于河东而付之弘靖之重寄，彼将恤乏吊灾，丰犒而勤恤之，则卢龙何自叛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214500_comment'></div>此策之失一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214500_comment'></div>夫既不能用度而产患若此矣，克融拒刘悟，使不得入，旋以易定为寇，于是时诚能合集锐师，北首燕路而以授钺之寄属度，则已失之燕，谈笑可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214500_comment'></div>观夫克融之援廷凑也，度移书开说，遂请罢兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214500_comment'></div>其执杨文端也，度画二策，即日听命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214500_comment'></div>韦处厚曰：「使度位廊庙，则幽镇自臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1214500_comment'></div>使二镇还者，皆曰裴度居东，人情失望，奈何帝冲逸而弗知用也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1214500_comment'></div>且在先帝时戮师道而平齐，诛元济而平蔡，承宗献地，程权入朝，皆自度谋画之致，岂独幽州而无功乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1214500_comment'></div>此策之失二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1214500_comment'></div>穆宗席前世之烈，不驰一戈，不亡一镞，而坐享幽、燕之地，未及转盼而复陷于贼，议者谓幽州幽阴惨毒，其民刚强，厥田沃壤，远慕田光、荆卿之义，近染思明、禄山之风，忘忠嗜乱，殆非人力所能为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1214500_comment'></div>愚独以为皆不用裴度之过。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1214500_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论泽潞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214501")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214501'>用兵有六要，而敌之坚脆不论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214501_comment'></div>抵排浮议则计不摇，要结外援则力不困，师整而壮则有剽疾之功，将专而勇则无折北之虑，孤其势则我益强，捣其虚则我滋实，六者兼备而敌已困于冥冥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214501_comment'></div>尝观会昌泽潞之役，刘稹有可诛之形，武宗有决诛之志，而丞相德裕有能诛之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214501_comment'></div>指踪受胜，六要且举，兹所以堂堂潞子之邦，讫不沦于篡逆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214501_comment'></div>迹夫刘悟死而从谏欲主留务，宝历之君违李绛之计而徇王守澄之请，于是举五州而弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214501_comment'></div>已而擅兵长子，阴连训、注，致论二萧欲清君侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214501_comment'></div>迨至从谏，因崔士康而以符节自擅，谢医拒使，检商阁货，胁其君而剿其民，上愤下怨，所谓可诛之形也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214501_comment'></div>武宗以内地叛涣，锐意征讨，使者不入则谪隶恭陵，贼使远来则杖死京兆，彼能缓茂卿之赏而不疑，禽太原之兵而不赦，李悟乞降而不从，崔碣请纳而远逐，群臣议罢兵者誓戮之于境上，兹所谓决诛之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214501_comment'></div>至于巨谋纤计，算不失一而六要具举，则又出于德裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214501_comment'></div>何谓抵排浮议则计不摇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214501_comment'></div>始议用兵，沮梗百绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214501_comment'></div>或曰刘悟挈十二州还天子，当使遗育；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214501_comment'></div>或曰从谏兵强食足，未易可破。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214501_comment'></div>廷臣皆媕娿趣和，并为一谈，独德裕以赢缩胜负为兵家之常，而慨然以身任责，故谢却陈夷让易置李宗闵，而贼已丧胆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214501_comment'></div>何谓要结外援则力不困？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214501_comment'></div>上党之地，前触魏，侧肘赵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214501_comment'></div>魏人驰劲骑不三四日，兵交于漳水西矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214501_comment'></div>赵人出坚甲不五六日，兵合于泜水东矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214501_comment'></div>形利势便，封略相错也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214501_comment'></div>德裕因敕李回谕旨，使二镇出兵，于是王元逵次临洺，何弘敬栅肥乡，左排右掖，而贼无炊火焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214501_comment'></div>何谓师整而壮则有剽疾之功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214501_comment'></div>异时团诸道兵，有所讨伐，尺布斗粟仰给公上，多迁延以耗供亿，甚者约贼令解守备，得一屯一县，则献公要赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214501_comment'></div>德裕因敕诸将直取州勿攻县，故邢、洺继降，而刘稹气索矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214501_comment'></div>何谓将专而勇则无折北之虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214501_comment'></div>异时阍寺掌兵，进退掣肘，监军取精剽士以自随，而以疲琐者备行阵，师小不利，则卷旂自遁，大兵辄随以北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214501_comment'></div>德裕建请诏本道付宰司，乃下监军不得干凡事，百人取一为卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214501_comment'></div>又王宰观望而薄责，由是石卫以胜闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214501_comment'></div>李产佐逗遛而遣代，由是乌岭以捷奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214501_comment'></div>何谓孤其势则我益强？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214501_comment'></div>李丕善长短术，军中雅疾之，脱族自归，议者疑为贼遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214501_comment'></div>德裕建议讨贼，半载始有降者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214501_comment'></div>廪赐不厚，何以劝馀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214501_comment'></div>于是擢刺忻州，而贼妪恸泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214501_comment'></div>未几，裴问以邢归赵，王钊以洺款魏，高玉、魏元谈辈以次降附，而贼无与战矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214501_comment'></div>何谓捣其虚则我滋实？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214501_comment'></div>先是，河朔诸将死，即如吊祀，申以册赠之使，重以宣慰之人，度军中便宜，乃与节，军中不许，始用兵，大抵不半岁不能定，故謷将逆子因得固巢穴，积叛谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214501_comment'></div>德裕请乘其未备讨之，于是仓皇号恸，而二十六载之逋寇平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214501_comment'></div>或曰刘悟以此始，则郭谊以此终，殆天道好还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214501_comment'></div>愚独以为一出德裕之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214501_comment'></div>至贼平之后，以郭谊衅斧而不赦，畏诸将请地，以卢弘正团结其州，又见其谋画之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214501_comment'></div>《诗》云：「式固尔犹，淮夷卒获」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214501_comment'></div>德裕有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214501_comment'></div>史臣谓武宗用一德裕，遂成其功，谅哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1214501_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>外戚论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214502")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214502'>人君有天下而未知治乱得失之机，胡不取前世之已事观焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214502_comment'></div>某事果利乎，循而行之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214502_comment'></div>某事果害乎，矫而变之，庶几可以远祸乱，基太平也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214502_comment'></div>今夫天子以一身而制天下者，以有权利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214502_comment'></div>惟利可以役人，惟权可以制人，是以不出殿陛而天下惟吾之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214502_comment'></div>苟不能慎惜名器而轻以假人，倒持太阿，授人魁柄，则晚节末路，抱持虚器而威势下移矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214502_comment'></div>况外戚之伦，少不知学，狃富贵之居则志易以僭，挟禁掖之势则权易以专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214502_comment'></div>其始盗天子之威福为予夺，以劫持天下，天下既侧目而畏之，则还以恐喝于上而邀望大利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214502_comment'></div>君人者奈何不加抑远而使之立朝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214502_comment'></div>西汉之业以外戚亡，愚尝惜成、哀之君纵不能远取前世事以为龟鉴，胡不以祖宗之得失耳目未远者观之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214502_comment'></div>始文帝以后弟窦广国贤有行，欲相之，既而曰「恐天下以吾私广国」，卒拜申屠嘉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214502_comment'></div>元帝以冯野王行能第一，欲用为御史大夫，既而曰「后世必谓我私后宫」，卒用张谭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214502_comment'></div>是二帝者矫私徇公若此其蚤也，遏绝外戚之乱若此其甚也，继其后者若之何不循而行乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214502_comment'></div>异时吕氏盗朝，产、禄肆乱，不有太尉主兵而北军助顺，则海内危矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214502_comment'></div>霍氏继起，禹山专制，肆行非度，阴有异谋，非宣皇帝毅然加兵，则宗庙恐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214502_comment'></div>彼二氏者柄朝未几而产害已若此，继其后者若之何不矫而变乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214502_comment'></div>悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214502_comment'></div>建始以后政柄旁落，归于王氏，五侯群弟更迭弄权，威势翕习，青紫充满，排摈宗室，孤弱公族，诛戮亡忌，击断不清，而当时之君琐琐碌碌，曾不敢举手开喙以预天下事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214502_comment'></div>自王章以直言诛，刘向以正谏黜，而忠谠之士卷舌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214502_comment'></div>杜钦、谷永之朋方且逆望风旨，揄扬赞颂，而张禹、孔光共为持禄计，不肯吐忠实于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214502_comment'></div>由是汉室彫弱不振，至于贼莽，则大事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214502_comment'></div>彼且文饰休符，招致琛赆，作为石匮、大诰之书以愚弄天下，则汉欲不亡，得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214502_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214502_comment'></div>自古天下败于外家者惟汉与周，然隋文帝东平全齐而西破巴蜀，五王奸谋同日摘发，则于宇文氏不为无功，方之安汉，可异日谈也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1214502_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>卫青论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214503")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214503'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214503'>卫青起于奴隶，显于戚里，而终以阃外之功，封侯裂土，延及襁褓，三子同日受封，而裨校皆得爵土，虽曰知兵胜敌，然其德度亦自有以致之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214503_comment'></div>方是时，武帝在上，大臣少丽罪则诛戮随之，青独能保身以没，可谓贤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214503_comment'></div>且天子之大柄二：一曰爵赏，二曰诛戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214503_comment'></div>而青于此皆逡巡退避而不敢专，此其所以能保身者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214503_comment'></div>尝曰自魏其、武安厚宾客，天子常切齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214503_comment'></div>彼亲待士大夫、招贤黜不肖者，人主之柄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214503_comment'></div>人臣奉法遵职而已，何与招士？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214503_comment'></div>此不肯侵天子爵赏之柄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214503_comment'></div>苏建尽亡其军，周霸之属皆请斩以立威，青曰：「青幸得以肺腑待罪行间，不患无威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214503_comment'></div>傥归天子，使天子自裁之，示不敢擅专诛于境外，以风人臣不敢专权，不亦可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214503_comment'></div>遂囚建行在，此不敢侵人主之诛罚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214503_comment'></div>以此令终，不亦宜乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1214503_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214362' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214362' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214362?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答何状元启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214362")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214362_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214362'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214362'>冠名英俊之躔，升华图籍之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214362_comment'></div>仲舒之为举首，启发道真；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214362_comment'></div>子政之校中经，夙昭人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214362_comment'></div>朝廷得士，寰海趋风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214362_comment'></div>恭惟某官学奥离伦，材高周用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214362_comment'></div>元元本本，博穷载籍之传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214362_comment'></div>济济洋洋，蚤预宾兴之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214362_comment'></div>果缘健笔，力取巍科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214362_comment'></div>上兴见晚之嗟，人以睹先为快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214362_comment'></div>名惊学子，笔稿至于欲烧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214362_comment'></div>文播都城，纸价几于骤贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214362_comment'></div>敢图谦谢，亦附冗僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214362_comment'></div>退揆菲材，固难当于溢美；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214362_comment'></div>仰窥佳藻，亦窃幸于珍藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214362_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1214362_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>枢密吴公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214519")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214519'>政和三年正月，光禄大夫、知枢密院事武昌公抗疏言：「臣老被病，自度不能复任陛下政事，愿赐骸骨归故里」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214519_comment'></div>降御笔诏弗许，戒毋得重陈，且命有司，章上勿复纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214519_comment'></div>时朝廷尊荣，边鄙不耸，上方倚眷旧德，而公求去甚力，入对恳切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214519_comment'></div>上不得已，拜武康军节度使，知洪州，凡礼秩悉视见执政，许其子接领祠宫自随，除直秘阁以宠之，数遣近侍访所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214519_comment'></div>及陛辞日，慰劳周渥，令月上一疏奏事，赆有饫赐，宴有腆乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214519_comment'></div>出都门，复遣近侍抚问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214519_comment'></div>大丞相太师鲁公帅二府，即寓馆访别，且谓大臣进退之美，近世鲜俪，中朝缙绅，杂然誉叹之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214519_comment'></div>公涖镇踰年，条教既孚，兵民豫附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214519_comment'></div>移知庐州，会继四上章祈罢节钺，三上章祈谢事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214519_comment'></div>御笔诏有曰：「耆龄微恙，理或有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214519_comment'></div>卿素怀忠义，神明监相，药石旋效，何感而上书归印」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214519_comment'></div>七月辛巳，以公薨闻，上为一日不视朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214519_comment'></div>赠开府仪同三司，录所当任者特以文资官之，敕本路计臣护办丧事，听其家常上其子若孙一人任本部官，亲篆墓隧之碑首曰「旧德褒贤之碑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214519_comment'></div>复命史臣某志其墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214519_comment'></div>臣某承诏退伏，考公以宏才伟望受知三朝，自承辖历东西侍郎，遂长枢筦，履正秉义，劢相国家，出处始终，不见玷毁，克保富贵寿考，屹然为当代重臣，而勋名恩礼之盛，在法宜纪，以劝后世，其敢以固陋辞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214519_comment'></div>谨按武昌公讳某，字某，姓吴氏，豫章人，神烈真人汉吴猛之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214519_comment'></div>上世尝徙籍临川，自公复家豫章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214519_comment'></div>曾大父某赠太师、昌国公，配曰韩国夫人傅氏、益国夫人杜氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214519_comment'></div>大父某赠太师、庆国公，配曰越国夫人晏氏、魏国夫人葛氏，晏即丞相元宪公女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214519_comment'></div>父某，池州录事参军，赠太师、秦国公，配曰燕国夫人饶氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214519_comment'></div>公幼孤，克己自立，博涉载籍，尤精先、后《汉书》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214519_comment'></div>入太学，众儒推重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214519_comment'></div>嘉祐八年第进士，调潭州攸县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214519_comment'></div>见谓习事，守燕度器之，表置幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214519_comment'></div>推行常平新书，有精识，课最卓异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214519_comment'></div>会开梅山，均给蛮人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214519_comment'></div>方是时，天子修举先朝故事略尽，大兴礼乐学校，以文太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214519_comment'></div>公调御将顺与有功，禁田招集新附有劳，叠二赏，改大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214519_comment'></div>论者犹以不侔功，遂迁殿中丞，知安州景陵、开封咸平二县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214519_comment'></div>熙宁八年东南饥，选公计置六路，振济米斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214519_comment'></div>时州县定簿法、均役钱，守长率未烛法意，科指舛逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214519_comment'></div>大司农上公咸平政绩，乞就除本路勾当公事官措置，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214519_comment'></div>奉使还，擢司农寺主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214519_comment'></div>俄迁丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214519_comment'></div>召对，神宗奇其材，除河北西路常平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214519_comment'></div>顷之入觐，奏事殿中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214519_comment'></div>神宗面谕，以究心职事、不孤寄属，赐朱衣、银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214519_comment'></div>移京东转运判官，就升副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214519_comment'></div>朝廷更制盐荚之初，公在东土累年，处画精审，豪商右姓不得扰开阖之柄，而利归公上，坐收缗钱数百万赡一路，且输其赢以实中都，策功增秩一等，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214519_comment'></div>神宗使河北路取以为法，诏遣周辅、李南公与公会议境上，数降玺书褒奖，最后御批以谓：「内外财计之臣，政绩著验，未有加吴某者，其议所以褒显之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214519_comment'></div>遂除天章阁待制、京东都转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214519_comment'></div>诏以本路盐息钱百七十万市绢给河东马直，不两月又以办闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214519_comment'></div>诏复奖谕，知密州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1214519_comment'></div>范锷建言板桥榷易之利，神宗独委公筹之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1214519_comment'></div>公又建请利国监岁铸大铁钱二百万以佐关陕兵食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1214519_comment'></div>神宗阅奏，大嘉曰：「居京东而恤他路，干国器也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1214519_comment'></div>悉可其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1214519_comment'></div>元祐中，公摈不用且十年，荣悴一不婴意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1214519_comment'></div>绍圣初，哲宗躬断以前所坐非罪，亟召用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1214519_comment'></div>起知鄂州，未赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1214519_comment'></div>改苏州，复集贤殿修撰，为江淮荆浙等路发运使，俄复天章阁待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1214519_comment'></div>涟水支家渠岁久倾塞，漕引留碍，累议疏浚，迄无坚决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1214519_comment'></div>公起徒役治之，上功，进一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1214519_comment'></div>汴口流胔，旧有收瘗之令，然暮夜多顺流入淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1214519_comment'></div>公命设网索于圯下，自是岁瘗倍前，人以为有阴赐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1214519_comment'></div>召拜户部侍郎，哲宗命以元祐责告悉纳尚书省燔弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1214519_comment'></div>进户部尚书，除龙图阁学士，知开封府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1214519_comment'></div>以严绳下，豪猾慑服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1214519_comment'></div>请置四厢捕卒营房摄录盗贼，使都人夜户不闭，长老言前治京师者莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1214519_comment'></div>上即位，以为永泰陵桥道顿递使，旋改真定府、永兴军安抚使，未赴，改复土桥道事，出知和州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1214519_comment'></div>以医药济病者，所全活甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1214519_comment'></div>除龙图阁待制、陕西都转运使，寻兼制置解盐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1214519_comment'></div>崇宁元年召还，再尹开封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1214519_comment'></div>奏对剀切，上竦听，再除户部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1214519_comment'></div>旧以三司、开封为省府，号难治，公皆再践其职，拨繁整棼，魁然有异等之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1214519_comment'></div>上以为可大用，拜尚书右丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1214519_comment'></div>以收复抚定湟、鄯、廓州，数迁秩，拜中书侍郎，迁门下侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1214519_comment'></div>大观初以年臻七十，累求致仕，除资政殿学士、东太一宫使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1214519_comment'></div>故事，罢执金带，换御仙花，恩特许服毬纹，遂著为令，自公始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1214519_comment'></div>坐法左迁端明殿学士，知亳州，言者谓不当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1214519_comment'></div>会藩东南，改提举鸿庆宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1214519_comment'></div>居期年，复资政殿学士，知徐州，言者复伸前论，罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1214519_comment'></div>大观三年，上以元丰侍臣不当久置閒左，起知洪州，移太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1214519_comment'></div>将及国门，遣使者郊劳，赉锡加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1214519_comment'></div>及对，遂以佑神观使留京师，再除门下侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1214519_comment'></div>岁中，遂除知枢密院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1214519_comment'></div>尝从容奏请遹追先烈，在坚其志，且以见尧舜羹墙等事，广引详说，及献备边选将要议，上皆嘉纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1214519_comment'></div>每定大政，辄遣中人就第咨访，事多施用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1214519_comment'></div>上以诸路漕臣失职，赏赐御批曰：「漕臣不营职业，惟以干叩朝廷为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1214519_comment'></div>曩者卿任京东，未尝告乏，盖材与不材所致也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1214519_comment'></div>预议元圭，进一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1214519_comment'></div>公典枢机，以周慎自著，忠言鲠议，多造膝启沃，退未尝语人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1214519_comment'></div>然论者见其君臣相得，礼意笃备，而一时疆埸无虞，兵革偃戢，河西、朔北争效职贡，则知帷幄运筹之功为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1214519_comment'></div>公仕五十馀年，积官光禄大夫，勋上柱国，爵武昌郡开国公，虚邑五千户，实食邑一千二百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1214519_comment'></div>夙被简注，前后所得上真迹甚富，建阁袭藏于豫章里第，御篆「褒贤之阁」宠之，饬尚方勒金字榜驰赐，公刻石叙荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1214519_comment'></div>每遇天宁节及上本命壬戌日，必斋戒，召方士启醮阁下，祝千万岁寿，费出廪禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1214519_comment'></div>及为先令，又戒子孙毋辄废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1214519_comment'></div>公机鉴通悟，而质厚谨，自少讫老，无一日置书不读，晨兴奉朝请亦视书待旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1214519_comment'></div>手钞历代史记百馀帙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1214519_comment'></div>文词典雅，尤工诗，慕杜甫氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1214519_comment'></div>上览之，常激赏，或俯同其韵，且命以平日所为录进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1214519_comment'></div>公进数百篇，优制称述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1214519_comment'></div>有文集一百二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1214519_comment'></div>少贫，依中表杨南仲学，其妻李贤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1214519_comment'></div>及后贵，李犹无恙，以母事之，移世赏官其二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1214519_comment'></div>公笃于节谊，多此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1214519_comment'></div>属纩，神明不乱，享年七十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1214519_comment'></div>娶刘氏，封豫章郡夫人，某官冯京女甥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1214519_comment'></div>子四人：接，今为朝请郎、直秘阁、提点洪州玉隆观，学行孝谨，名能守家法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1214519_comment'></div>择，故通直郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1214519_comment'></div>括、授，皆承奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1214519_comment'></div>女：长适朝奉大夫李禔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1214519_comment'></div>次适宣义郎、无为军录事刘蒙之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1214519_comment'></div>次适朝奉郎、知池州吕漴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1214519_comment'></div>幼封孺人，未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1214519_comment'></div>孙男五：兴祖，承务郎、江南西路转运司管勾帐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1214519_comment'></div>寿祖，将仕郎、监兖州东岳庙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1214519_comment'></div>庆祖，登仕郎、监衡州南岳庙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1214519_comment'></div>荣祖，承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1214519_comment'></div>孙女一人，封孺人，未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1214519_comment'></div>曾孙男成杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1214519_comment'></div>政和五年某月某日，葬进贤县麻仙山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1214519_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_112_1214519'>惟吴之先，肇自太伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1214519_comment'></div>神烈真人，名垂仙籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1214519_comment'></div>福祚后昆，源源其泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1214519_comment'></div>是生开府，资适逢时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1214519_comment'></div>奋取侍从，神宗所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1214519_comment'></div>崇宁之初，天子颛柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1214519_comment'></div>遹图康功，拔举众正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1214519_comment'></div>公来自西，陛对崇政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1214519_comment'></div>开陈大谋，动寤万乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1214519_comment'></div>乃尹三辅，乃跻六卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1214519_comment'></div>帝顾在位，敷求辅臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1214519_comment'></div>曰惟汝贤，国之元老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1214519_comment'></div>谁其绥予，自我圣考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1214519_comment'></div>俾贰政机，进长枢幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1214519_comment'></div>密勿十年，文谋武略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1214519_comment'></div>端委廊庙，精神折冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1214519_comment'></div>三陲不警，卧鼓櫜弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1214519_comment'></div>公拜稽首，抗章乞身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1214519_comment'></div>帝曰昼绣，归荣里门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1214519_comment'></div>南昌之封，武康之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1214519_comment'></div>暨暨戎容，建旄授钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1214519_comment'></div>公以讣闻，燕朝辍视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1214519_comment'></div>一品正司，衮衣以襚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1214519_comment'></div>公功在史，亦纪旂常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1214519_comment'></div>勒铭幽宫，公则不亡<span class='inlineComment2'>（《丹阳集》卷一二。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1214519_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_137_1214519'>周辅：据《宋史》卷一八一《食货志》所记，此人当为「蹇周辅」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_137_1214519_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214256' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214256' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214256?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免大司成劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214256")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214256_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214256'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214256'>臣准东上閤门告报，已降告命，除臣试大司成者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214256_comment'></div>卑贱之臣，骤膺亲擢，闻命震怖，不知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214256_comment'></div>恭惟陛下大兴庠序，以兴斯文，声教之远，外薄海表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214256_comment'></div>而成均辟雍之长，实总中外学政，非宿德名儒，岂称任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214256_comment'></div>伏念臣孤愚一介，经学浅薄，徒知安分守义，而行能器识，无以逾人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214256_comment'></div>昨被选除，再贰国子，夙夜黾勉，觊有毫发之效，而讫未有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214256_comment'></div>方惧旷官，以干罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214256_comment'></div>敢谓天慈不遗微品，特加因任，就进从班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214256_comment'></div>虽曲泽所加，在臣至为荣幸，而公议可畏，不敢辄冒非据之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214256_comment'></div>伏望睿明将行迁令，追寝误恩，岂惟示名器之公，亦以增学校之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214256_comment'></div>所有告命，臣未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214256_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任屏营俟命之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1214256_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大司成谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214297")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214297'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214297'>入持禁橐，已愧超迁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214297_comment'></div>进长经黉，更叨因任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214297_comment'></div>循涯虚受，程奏恳辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214297_comment'></div>膺诏旨之弗俞，锡服章而加贲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214297_comment'></div>亦既就职，深虞累恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214297_comment'></div>伏以兼三代之学，以明人伦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214297_comment'></div>同四海之风，而暨声教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214297_comment'></div>大申孝弟之义，交献贤能之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214297_comment'></div>历年滋多，明效灼见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214297_comment'></div>小子有造，预鼓箧者千人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214297_comment'></div>海邦率从，来执经者万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214297_comment'></div>惟时教法，特轸渊衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214297_comment'></div>责古人大全，则荐降德音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214297_comment'></div>示圣经奥旨，则亲为训传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214297_comment'></div>盖躬教立道之君处上，则育材首善之臣至难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214297_comment'></div>方广询求，以专属任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214297_comment'></div>而臣学非得己，才不加人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214297_comment'></div>行谊不足为世之范模，文藻不能作经之鼓吹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214297_comment'></div>偶自朝廷兴学之始，首叨方郡分教之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214297_comment'></div>玷礼曹郎属者四年，预胄席师儒者三等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214297_comment'></div>所能何有，每迁益高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214297_comment'></div>虽宾贤养士之规模，粗知本末；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214297_comment'></div>顾成德达材之绩效，蔑有毫釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214297_comment'></div>不悟异恩，就跻迩列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214297_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下诞敷文德，遹图康功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214297_comment'></div>久于道而化成，不忘乐育；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214297_comment'></div>主其心而慎治，更务能官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214297_comment'></div>察臣所守之靡他，贷臣已试之无验，猥加曲泽，使勉后图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214297_comment'></div>誓毕微生，仰酬洪造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1214297_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵宏道游三官院园时余往辟廱不果往</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523649")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523649'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523649'>晚携胜友共扬镳，应厌家鬟捻紫箫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523649'>逮得暇时能有几，每逢佳处且相邀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523649'>大夫高挹髯龙操，公子閒窥白雁标。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523649'>独恨抗尘乖寄赏，偶飞轻盖四门桥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523649'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523649_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元巳日王循德<span class='inlineComment2'>（孝迪）</span>招饮方池宏道兄有诗奉和以纪一时之事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523612")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523612'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523612'>浮爽清波正日迟，出郊修禊属芳时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523612'>幸陪飞观朋簪盍，未睹华堂舞袖僛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523612'>命中已于三耦见，争雄仍向一枰知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523612'>爱君多艺能倾坐，岂但流觞记逸诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523612'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_523612'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_523612_0'>⑴ 自注：宏道兄有舞者甚丽，未之见也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_523612_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_523368' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523368' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523368?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵张宏道劝释奠致斋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523368")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523368_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523368'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523368'>斋居屏尘务，况复儒宫清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523368'>木落必粪本，祭菜敢不诚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523368'>瑚簋见三代，错落罗两楹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523368'>骨冷破梦境，虚窗坐黎明。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523368'>祠官趣盥颒，珊然环佩声。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523368'>巍巍素王像，视若四海营。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523368'>当时杏坛士，与享彯华缨。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523368'>乐教属昭代，弟子陈歌笙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523368'>端如从陈蔡，琴舞纷纵横。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523368'>元功流万祀，德大遍诸生。<div id='poem_sentence_9_523368_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_523368'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_523368_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214508?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宗正寺少卿壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214508")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214508'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214508'>昔周之盛时，封同姓五十三国，而公族之居王朝者尚众，始置宗正以纠正之，所谓「彤伯为宗」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214508_comment'></div>后世因袭不改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214508_comment'></div>先汉位九列，后汉秩中二千石，率用宗姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214508_comment'></div>唐制：卿一人，从三品；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214508_comment'></div>少卿二人，从四品，杂以同姓、异姓充选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214508_comment'></div>天祚宋德，宗庶繁衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214508_comment'></div>景祐中，始诏推择属近望高者二人判大宗正事，至纂修玉牒属籍，则用他官兼领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214508_comment'></div>神宗皇帝董正治官，肇置九寺，深惟庆系之重，圣神在天，实鉴临之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214508_comment'></div>且奕世帝籍若谱牒昭穆之序，皆隶宗正，不可与他寺等，故班秩特高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214508_comment'></div>然卿少虚位弗置，专以丞董寺事者，以有太宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214508_comment'></div>上嗣位，广延众正，大修废官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214508_comment'></div>崇宁某年始命邓祐甫为少卿，以后复三代宾兴法，念宗子之俊秀奇异者亦宜教养而官使之，诏即广亲诸第建六学，凡三舍，校试升迁法悉视廱泮，而以寺长贰总之，宗正选益重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214508_comment'></div>逮今十馀年间，所阅二十馀人，类能以勋绩自见，为时名臣，可谓盛哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214508_comment'></div>寺故有玉牒殿、籍属堂，面势褊曲，室宇湫陋，不称天子尊祖睦族之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214508_comment'></div>岁在丁酉，诏彻太医学以广寺治，发德音，委大匠护役，不数日而屋若干区为之一新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214508_comment'></div>既落成，因集前人名氏，且叙建寺首末并刻之，使后来得以考观焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1214508_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214538' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214538' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214538?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徐太令人葛氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214538")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214538'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214538'>太令人常州江阴葛氏，赠吏部尚书讳某之孙，承议郎、赠太中大夫讳某之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214538_comment'></div>葛氏族大且显，凡女子许字必求天下名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214538_comment'></div>令人年既笄，辩慧婉嫕，太中与其兄工部尚书某皆爱奇之，为访佳对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214538_comment'></div>而金陵徐君安道受经舒王，以才识为高第，中治平某年进士甲第，隐然有俊杰之称，遂以归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214538_comment'></div>其后入御史府为监察，入中台为郎，奉使诸道，风节端亮，名誉尊显，卒官中大夫、京西转运副使，令人阃助为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214538_comment'></div>中大夫求所生戴氏，十年始得，既归，性高严，令人奉养如嫡，刺测微旨，无铢发忤戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214538_comment'></div>抚姒妇之孤踰己子，单复之服制必先之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214538_comment'></div>逮其长，为谋家室，垂橐不吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214538_comment'></div>岁时享徐氏祖考，不以馔羞委僮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214538_comment'></div>侍遇父母尊亲之党，恩义均一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214538_comment'></div>从夫若子官四方，中外宗姻靡日不婴念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214538_comment'></div>服衰至小功、缌，闻讣皆摧恸，以丧礼自律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214538_comment'></div>逢讳日，蔬食阅经，以资其福，尽齿不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214538_comment'></div>太中所嗜蓣栗之属，辄不忍食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214538_comment'></div>宦游旧境，复经历，未尝不涕泗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214538_comment'></div>性淑灵，而笃孝尤加人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214538_comment'></div>以夫恩封永昌县君，以子恩封普宁县太君，再封太令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214538_comment'></div>政和七年八月壬申终于京师，寿七十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214538_comment'></div>崇信释氏，日课其书，且奉其斋戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214538_comment'></div>属纩不乱，呼子与妇执其手曰：「吾诀矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214538_comment'></div>泊然而瞑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214538_comment'></div>子六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214538_comment'></div>男永，朝请郎、行太常寺主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214538_comment'></div>奕，通仕郎、知卫州新乡县，前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214538_comment'></div>女长适承事郎、知常州江阴县李孝远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214538_comment'></div>次早卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214538_comment'></div>次适通直郎、武学博士朱天锡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214538_comment'></div>次适宣教郎、知平江府长洲县陆棠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214538_comment'></div>孙男二人，女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214538_comment'></div>永以学行知名，荐践师儒之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214538_comment'></div>自中大夫即世，令人食其禄者十九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214538_comment'></div>晚节寝病绵剧，视絮糜药，至夜不解带，人士称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214538_comment'></div>卜葬，得令人卒之年某月甲子，祔中大夫之封，在江宁府上元县莫府山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214538_comment'></div>以某于令人为兄子，且先君通奉与之相友爱，见属以铭，因泣铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1214538'>性笃孝，士所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214538_comment'></div>乾其身，行之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214538_comment'></div>媲其良，训厥嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214538_comment'></div>诏三封，寿六纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214538_comment'></div>源有衍，报必丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214538_comment'></div>在后人，不于躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214538_comment'></div>莫府原，龟墨食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214538_comment'></div>千万年，安且吉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1214538_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢江州太平观表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年1月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214298")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214298_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214298'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214298'>跻荣命教，滥居学省之华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214298_comment'></div>负罪投閒，尚窃祠宫之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214298_comment'></div>宽恩下逮，感涕横流<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214298_comment'></div>伏念臣学术空疏，性资愚拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214298_comment'></div>本为贫而干泽，寖席宠以逢时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214298_comment'></div>俾游英俊之躔，尽出圣神之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214298_comment'></div>班陪从橐，秩冠儒官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214298_comment'></div>顾惟何人，辄膺是选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214298_comment'></div>果缘冒处，遂致疾颠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214298_comment'></div>仰繄亭毒之私，犹颁饩廪之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214298_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下德俾天大，恩均父慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214298_comment'></div>扩仁恕以并容，亶聪明而临照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214298_comment'></div>深闵向隅之戚，特从祝网之宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214298_comment'></div>退居寂寞之滨，得从优逸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214298_comment'></div>上答生成之赐，更誓糜捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214298_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1214298_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
黄山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='80600a64e3b941f68c2d486dca15688e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("80600a64e3b941f68c2d486dca15688e");'><span id='80600a64e3b941f68c2d486dca15688e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>，38岁</div><div id='80600a64e3b941f68c2d486dca15688e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年8月</a>　到任三日，作祀神文四篇以明心迹。作品：初莅任祀神文四首。<div id='poem_1214553' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214553' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214553?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初莅任祀神文<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214553")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214553_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214553'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214553'>某罪大贬轻，犹得为令，实与有神，均莅此邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214553_comment'></div>凡力所及者，既自黾勉矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214553_comment'></div>非力所及者，惟神相之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214553_comment'></div>傥不瘝厥官，其敢乏神之命祀？</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1214553_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214554' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214554' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214554?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214554_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214554'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214554'>州县之吏，以事神保民为职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214554_comment'></div>然民之庶富，必赖有神之阴骘，则事神之谨，尤所宜先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214554_comment'></div>某视职三日，并走群祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214554_comment'></div>四郊不警，五稼普收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214554_comment'></div>繄神相之，使安厥位。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1214554_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214555' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214555?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214555'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214555'>祗奉恩纶，叨膺郡绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214555_comment'></div>不学而入政，未信而临民，大惧旷瘝，以孤任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214555_comment'></div>顾惟阴相，实赖有神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214555_comment'></div>恪职之初，承祭敢怠？</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1214555_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214556?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214556_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214556'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214556'>此邦之人，肖神之像而祠事之者，以神有功德于己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214556_comment'></div>天子不爱爵宠以发扬潜懿，复以徽称荣其庙者，以神有功德于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214556_comment'></div>长吏以尊君爱民为职，不敢慢于神者，以君之所尊崇，民之所祈向也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214556_comment'></div>某于视事之始，顿颡祠下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214556_comment'></div>唯是三者，神其图有以称之<span class='inlineComment2'>（《丹阳集》卷一一。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214556_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1214556'>此篇原与上篇连为一文，今据孔抄本析之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1214556_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　虽遭贬而不改其节操。作品：上前宰相书。<div id='poem_1214339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上前宰相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214339")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214339'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214339'>某七品冗吏，抵罪窜逐，得邑岩壑间，自安贫贱之分，悤悤校吏，不敢数以竹牍尘记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214339_comment'></div>退念幸蒙相公不以常辈知遇，曩虽得罪于朝廷，未得罪于名义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214339_comment'></div>今隶迹丹书，低簪把板为折腰吏，相公岂以屯厄遽移眄接之恩哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214339_comment'></div>因饰固陋之辞，叙悃诚自通，愿垂须臾之听，使毕其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214339_comment'></div>某窃惟在昔名节之士，操守素定，事至物来，以其素定者处之，不计祸福利害而叛其所学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214339_comment'></div>轻于蹈患害，而重于随时改度，喔咿俯仰，故能风节峣然，与霜日争光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214339_comment'></div>伏读旧史，竦然慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214339_comment'></div>曩者误沐过听，得备官使，贵戚有沮挠教法者抗章绳之，近习有猥见辟置者洁身去之，此分义之常，而相公广坐谭赏，此其意岂以碌碌凡流见望哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214339_comment'></div>提挽不已，遂得厕列文昌显曹，常欲激昂奋拔，稍自效见，以报奖知，而未有路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214339_comment'></div>会相公暂解钧轴，遂邪说丛兴，中执法建议纷更，上及僖祖殿室，表里影响，合为一辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214339_comment'></div>某非不知脂韦享厚福，婞直贾奇祸，独念名教至重，期待甚深，不当选软瘝厥官，因援引古义，谓不当罢奉常，诸僚是之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214339_comment'></div>继为奏议以上，风宪不容，相次斥逐，直注丑地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214339_comment'></div>某得邑黟、歙，有汤镬最沸之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214339_comment'></div>投身于兵戈杀越之乡，斗智于牒诉纷纭之地，心疲神极，与九死为邻，而处之甘如饴蜜者，趋操定也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214339_comment'></div>意相公未详首末，故详布腹心，此言朝闻，夕填沟壑无复遗恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214339_comment'></div>恭惟相公光辅圣政八年，勋名德泽旁照华裔，极天下金石竹帛，不足铭功而颂美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214339_comment'></div>拔士数千百人，寘之显列，山陬水滨，惟恐鉴采未至，可谓无负于人士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214339_comment'></div>今兹恳谢机政，颐神燕处，簿海内外，黄童白叟犹知歌《狼跋》、《九罭》之诗，引领以望，而况门下士哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214339_comment'></div>虽然，名士之用舍，世运系之，非人力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214339_comment'></div>孔子曰：「天之未丧斯文也，匡人其如予何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214339_comment'></div>孟子曰：「天欲平治天下，当今之世，舍我其谁哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214339_comment'></div>伏冀珍练眠食，为天下自重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1214339_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　勤于吏事，尤善断狱。作品：阅讼诉忽疲起卧少顷复视事。次韵德林新亭诗韵。圄空讼息复遇视眚庭事萧然蒙良器解元宠诗辄以二章为谢。<div id='poem_523353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523353' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523353?labeling=true' target='_blank'>阅讼诉忽疲起卧少顷复视事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523353")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523353_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523353'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523353'>平明坐早衙，投缿来相踵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
