id='poem_sentence_1_523353'>讼牍鼠雀暗，吏行凫鹜拥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523353'>外台竦风棱，檄至亟须捧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523353'>以身为形役，劾去顾未勇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523353'>病骨瘦栾栾，衰发希种种。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523353'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_523353_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523575' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523575' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523575?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次德林新亭诗韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523575")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523575_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523575'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523575'>缿讼无多得暂閒，结亭聊就碧鲜间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523575'>胡床寄目中宵月，手板支颐四面山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523575'>楂带水禽流浅濑，帆随烟艇转前湾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523575'>登临似与尘寰隔，况复朋从接笋班。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523575'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523575_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523573?labeling=true' target='_blank'>圄空讼息复遇肆眚庭事萧然蒙良器解元宠诗辄以二章为谢<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523573")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523573'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523573'>一官铜墨付疏顽，岁好人和偶未瘝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523573'>东亩黄云穈芑卧，北扉青草纆徽閒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523573'>鹄亭夜觉冤氛静，蝇笔晨惊霈泽颁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523573'>倪耄欢谣归帝力，风人溢美但赪颜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523573'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523573_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523574' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523574' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523574?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523574_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523574'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523574'>编户相安易得情，年来狴犴每刑清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523574'>庭閒不复施梧象，俗朴聊同示草缨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523574'>牍背仅能平枉桡，需头那复觊褒荣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523574'>人言官事无由了，暂得居官事了名。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523574'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523574_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_523574'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_523574_0'>⑴ 自注：来诗有“皇皇绣斧几时来，愿采民谣献天子”之句。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_523574_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　当地士人慕名求见者甚夥，有愿执师礼者。作品：答王斋长书。答李解元书。与程嘉量秀才书。<div id='poem_1214340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答王斋长书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214340")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214340'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214340'>某才知学问无足算录，又方窜逐于朝，宜人士摈而弗顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214340_comment'></div>吾子独惠然见存，抵以书幅，且引李白「不愿万户侯，愿识韩荆州」之语，何嗜好趋尚与俗背也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214340_comment'></div>韩朝宗行事，虽史篇漏逸，而白推以为人物之权衡，且踵门求见贤者，以收名定价，其非碌碌凡士审矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214340_comment'></div>顾仆何足以拟之，然有以知吾子好学求益之意深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214340_comment'></div>昔之名儒钜公，闻某所有贤士，则汲汲求见，未必不甚于士之求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214340_comment'></div>故皇甫规喜见王符，则曰「徒见二千石，不如一逢掖」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214340_comment'></div>桓大司马喜习凿齿，则曰「三十年读儒书，不如一诣习主簿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214340_comment'></div>以吾子齿壮气锐，敏于文词，稍自奋激，则《潜夫》之篇，魏晋之论，不难及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214340_comment'></div>此政鄙心所愿交，况逃空谷而喜足音之时乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214340_comment'></div>承暂留县学，仆以职事，当日夕继见，承音旨之日未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214340_comment'></div>深窃自幸，因叙以为谢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1214340_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214341?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答李解元书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214341")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214341_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214341'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214341'>某自入境，蒙人士以书见及者十数，遣辞立意，褒与过甚，皆非仆所敢当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214341_comment'></div>至吾子书辞比拟，大非其类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214341_comment'></div>周公、孔子大圣人也，如仆辈未免为乡人，岂可同年共世而语哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214341_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「儗人必于其伦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214341_comment'></div>昔柳子厚牧柳州，有杜温甫者以书为贽，亦有「周公」之说，子厚皇遽逊避，至累数百言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214341_comment'></div>夫子厚虽有附丽匪人之过，然文章妙一世，学问亦不碌碌，且犹云然，况仆辈又远子厚数千丈乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214341_comment'></div>虽佩厚意，然不敢领纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214341_comment'></div>吾子文辞婉缛，固自瘉人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214341_comment'></div>惟太不慎品藻，此亦夏璜之微瑕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214341_comment'></div>因载书为谢，并以相晓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1214341_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与程嘉量秀才书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214342")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214342'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214342'>数辱见临，猥示造述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214342_comment'></div>昨日复拜雅贶，开编疾读，如游玉圃于蓝田之郊，如闻《咸池》于洞庭之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214342_comment'></div>𢥠耳惊目，方咨美不暇，乃有师资之说，何撝挹过甚乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214342_comment'></div>柳子厚于韦中立犹逊避不敢当，况吾子学识加中立数等，而仆望子厚万里乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214342_comment'></div>虽然，语有之矣：「学所入者浅，体所安者深」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214342_comment'></div>闲习礼容，不如式瞻仪度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214342_comment'></div>讽诵遗言，不若亲承音旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214342_comment'></div>又曰：「望之俨然，乃不言之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214342_comment'></div>与田苏游，忘其鄙心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214342_comment'></div>则夫求当世望士，与之周旋，乃吾子之善学，第仆非其人尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214342_comment'></div>必欲规模，则书辞论子厚似太过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214342_comment'></div>子厚节操视退之虽父子，然文章兄弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214342_comment'></div>子厚不敢以师表自处，退之独抗颜为人师，既作《师说》以著传道解惑之益，又为《进学解》以诲诸生，非其不同意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214342_comment'></div>退之分教四门馆，则授业乃其职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214342_comment'></div>子厚方锢散地，不呶呶召闹取怒尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214342_comment'></div>古贤胜人处事自有次第，吾子以为何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214342_comment'></div>披读有暇，时过县斋，以既所欲言者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1214342_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年11月</a>　冬夜，感怀作《江神子》词。作品：江神子（初至休宁冬夜作）<div id='poem_224454' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224454' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/224454?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江神子/江城子 初至休宁冬夜作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_224454")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224454_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224454'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224454'>昏昏雪意惨云容。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224454'>猎霜风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224454'>岁将穷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224454'>流落天涯，憔悴一衰翁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224454'>清夜小窗围兽火，倾酒绿，借颜红。<div id='poem_sentence_4_224454_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_224454'>官梅疏艳小壶中。<div id='poem_sentence_5_224454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_224454'>暗香浓。<div id='poem_sentence_6_224454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_224454'>玉玲珑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_224454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_224454'>对景忽惊，身在大江东。<div id='poem_sentence_8_224454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_224454'>上国故人谁念我，晴嶂远，暮云重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_224454_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3b7f5ddb051044048e314f98c599b9c3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3b7f5ddb051044048e314f98c599b9c3");'><span id='3b7f5ddb051044048e314f98c599b9c3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1113')">1110-1113年</a>，39-42岁</div><div id='3b7f5ddb051044048e314f98c599b9c3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　创真意亭于南溪，时啸咏其上。作品：次韵良器真意亭探韵并序。游真意亭得二绝句示良器。程良器嘉量解元许为写照作诗求之。<div id='poem_523355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵良器真意亭探韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523355")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523355'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523355'>我爱陶渊明，脱颖深天机。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523355'>丛菊绕荒径，五柳摇幽扉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523355'>生逢卯金兴，典午势已非。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523355'>著书但甲子，岁晚频歔欷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523355'>仕宦聊复尔，樽酒真焉依。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523355'>南亩犹种秫，西山同采薇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523355'>浩歌归去来，熹微恨晨晖。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523355'>迷途往莫谏，今是庶可几。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523355'>蓄琴但取意，不施弦与徽。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523355'>观其四八目，贤哲在所希。<div id='poem_sentence_9_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_523355'>出处固有意，夫岂轻行违。<div id='poem_sentence_10_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_523355'>谁云惮束带，辞荣俄拂衣。<div id='poem_sentence_11_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_523355'>念彼同产人，抚视因遄归。<div id='poem_sentence_12_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_523355'>平生共志趣，但有一翟妃。<div id='poem_sentence_13_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_523355'>少陵罪责子，颇谓达道非。<div id='poem_sentence_14_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_523355'>右丞鄙乞食，更以人我讥。<div id='poem_sentence_15_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_523355'>乃知第一流，尚此知音稀。<div id='poem_sentence_16_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_523355'>妙诗发天奥，流转同衡玑。<div id='poem_sentence_17_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_523355'>自谓处人境，喧无车马騑。<div id='poem_sentence_18_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_523355'>心与尘事远，地偏堪遁肥。<div id='poem_sentence_19_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_523355'>东篱秋色晚，悠然望翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_20_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_523355'>真意不可辨，佳气随鸟飞。<div id='poem_sentence_21_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_523355'>诗辞向千载，凛凛犹光辉。<div id='poem_sentence_22_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_523355'>我生但睎骥，望之有等威。<div id='poem_sentence_23_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_523355'>行怀斜川游，坐想栗里矶。<div id='poem_sentence_24_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_523355'>九原不可作，筑亭傍崔嵬。<div id='poem_sentence_25_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_523355'>独取诗句名，櫩宇殊飞翚。<div id='poem_sentence_26_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_523355'>岩谷有杳霭，花卉无纷菲。<div id='poem_sentence_27_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_523355'>修篁寒逼人，坐如霜雪飞。<div id='poem_sentence_28_523355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_523355'>诸公赏清致，野服驰鞯鞿。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　真意亭初成，有《渔家傲》词二首。作品：渔家傲（初创真意亭于南溪游陟晚归作）二首。<div id='poem_224500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224500' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　泛舟南溪。作品：西江月（次韵林茂南博士杞泛溪）三月初六日席上代监酒和。<div id='poem_224462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_224462'>万顷溪连罨画。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224462_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224462'>柳恽风流旧国，鹤龄潇洒人家。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年8月</a>　秋，与程嘉量泛舟南溪，往返次韵，有《水调歌头》三首。作品：水调歌头（程良器嘉良别赋一阕纪泛舟之会往返次韵）三首。<div id='poem_224450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224450' id='poem_sentence_0_224450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224450'>棹飞穿碎金电，翻动水精宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224450'>横管何妨三弄，重醑仍须一斗，知费几青铜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224450'>坐久桂花落，襟袖觉香浓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_224450'>从来好景良夜，我辈敢情钟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_224450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_224450'>但恐仙娥川后，嫌我尘容俗状，清境不相容。<div id='poem_title_523451_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523451'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523451'>元丰功成身退閒，钟山小筑掩松关。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523451'>配食孔庙时烝祠，子生其后不识之。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523451'>纳鉴唾口难细论，谓言不信有如日。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/523452?labeling=true' target='_blank'>补之见和复次韵二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年11月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523452")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523452_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523452'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523452'>仙曹无事身得閒，午睡绝恶呼当关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523452'>榻施籧篨独展转，梦觉不离周孔间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523452'>官出砚州初乏砚，过眼罗纹如过电。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523452'>半生用一即墨侯，颇欲易之贫不办。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523452'>旧闻梦砚湘君祠，乃今神异真类之。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523452'>秣陵真儒岂虚授，文字之祥昌不衰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523452'>擘笺亹亹称名笔，正始微言欲俦匹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523452'>终当辞藻瑞朝廷，更请焚膏勤继日<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523452'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_523452_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_523452'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_523452_0'>⑴ 自注：蒋道支蓄鱼砚二十年，忽失之，见梦曰：游湘水，为二妃所留。后于湘君祠获焉。出《异苑》。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_523452_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_523453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523453' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523453?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年11月20日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523453'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523453'>逸骥未遇虚王闲，盐车垂耳犹间关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523453'>梦中一眄逢伯乐，遗以旧物惝恍间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523453'>斧柯山神护珍砚，采琢往往兴雷电。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523453'>欲求潜璞满书簏，顾岂咄嗟便能办。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523453'>祷求苦用中牢祠，何如假卧辄得之。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523453'>池塘句好有神助，文字格力何因衰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523453'>莫嗟筮仕困刀笔，聘材行即肩群匹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523453'>速将妙语醉衰翁，鸂鶒飞滩知不日<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523453'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_523453_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_523453'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_523453_0'>⑴ 自注：兴雷电，祭以中牢，皆出柳公权论砚。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_523453_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年12月30日</a>　除夕独坐县斋，有诗次乃兄和仲韵。作品：次韵工部兄除夕见寄三首。<div id='poem_523642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵工部兄除夕见寄三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年12月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523642")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523642'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523642'>异县飘流十载穷，年华又见转和风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523642'>春游已陡惊梅白，夜集犹疑共烛红。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523642'>蓝尾方嗟形影隔，苍头俄喜信音通。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523642'>麦秋时节摇归掉，禅榻相从话苦空<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_523642'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_523642_0'>⑴ 自注：除夕独坐县斋，偶记香山居士《隐几诗》云：行年三十九，岁莫日斜时。方寸如死灰，寂然无所知。老杜《守岁诗》云：四十明朝过，飞腾暮景斜。谁能更拘束，烂醉是生涯。因成长句二首，呈衣器。是岁予年数三十九，是日持六斋。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_523642_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_523643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523643?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年12月30日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523643'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523643'>霜毛垂领病摧颓，岁晚流年四秩催。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523643'>一自贬官瞻日远，两经除夕叹星回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523643'>梅吹画角馀寒尽，柏欲飞觞暖律来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523643'>岁莫日斜还隐几，心同白傅守寒灰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523643'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523643_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523644?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年12月30日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523644'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523644'>江城流落岁还新，懒作雕虫问大钧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523644'>月尽嘉平馀景刻，年侵彊仕尚沉沦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523644'>晚持禅悦惟三白，晓簇春盘又五辛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523644'>肯把生涯供烂醉，黎明学不动心人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523644'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523644_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年1月17日</a>　与李文中遍游歙、黟、祁门山水，有《西江月》词二首。作品：西江月（正月十七日与文中自邑境遍游歙黟祁门山水十九日在黟邑同灵观夜作二首）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a><div id='poem_523635' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523635' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523635?labeling=true' target='_blank'>婺源祁门二令母年八十求为保官注家便阙慨然慕之作诗二首自悼<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523635")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523635_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523635'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523635'>庭闱无复荐芳膻，乌鸟哀情每泫然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523635'>游子但吟春草句，门人欲废蓼莪篇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523635'>风枝数效皋鱼泣，水菽难攀子路贤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523635'>空羡邻封二佳令，儿啼八十寿亲前。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523635'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523635_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523636?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523636'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523636'>迎养京都突未黔，苍黄荼毒血沾襟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523636'>百年过隙知难复，三釜缠哀政自深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523636'>不为鲈莼归亦好，独甘羊枣果何心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523636'>寄言世上斑衣子，温凊应须竞寸阴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523636'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523636_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年2月</a>　应请求为陶直夫作墓志铭。作品：著作佐郎陶公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1214531' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214531?labeling=true' target='_blank'>著作佐郎陶公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214531")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214531_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214531'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214531'>晋著作佐郎陶渊明之后十六世，有孙曰直夫，字次，仍居浔阳，仕宋亦佐著作，大观三年年四十七，二月庚寅以疾卒官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214531_comment'></div>陶氏本鄱阳人，吴平，徙庐江之浔阳，有名丹者为吴扬武将军，是生晋荆州刺史长安郡公侃，于渊明为曾祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214531_comment'></div>而公之曾祖鉴，为左监门卫大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214531_comment'></div>祖稷，大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214531_comment'></div>父舜咨，第进士，终宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214531_comment'></div>公嗣举进士中第，调建昌军司户参军，官有殊政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214531_comment'></div>会诏诿诸道察良吏，江西使者以公应令，迁雄州防御推官，知亳州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214531_comment'></div>改教授怀州，谈经受业，切磋恳至，自远著录者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214531_comment'></div>遭外艰去职，学徒恨不得卒所闻，泣饯者踵相逮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214531_comment'></div>服除，又教授徐州，时三舍宾兴法兴，法始颁，方郡众未晓，能推广德意，区别科指，行之不少盭，傍郡取则焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214531_comment'></div>明年，集贡士试京师，徐土人士卒占异等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214531_comment'></div>迁大学正，改宣德郎，提举梓州路学事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214531_comment'></div>召对，询劳移晷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214531_comment'></div>先是，蜀部学廪不继，公至则披图考籍，录乾没吏一人寘之理，笼利源以丰岁入，窒奸隙以裁日用，养士之费始羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214531_comment'></div>迁监察御史，入秘书省为著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214531_comment'></div>逢受宝恩，转奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214531_comment'></div>公生质秀颖不凡，综练经学，广窥众善，专精或积岁不踰阈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214531_comment'></div>元丰中补太学弟子员，年少耳，然志尚风旨，魁然出老先生右，一时贤隽皆慕与之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214531_comment'></div>七年秋充贡赋，居第一，海内诵其文辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214531_comment'></div>及为吏，砥节首公，敕身自约，惴惴惟恐过差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214531_comment'></div>气貌严正，虽燕不堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214531_comment'></div>处交朋间，无择言之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214531_comment'></div>居丧举动遵礼纪，而毁戚独过制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214531_comment'></div>事寡嫂甚于兄之存，字其孤不啻己子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214531_comment'></div>有文数百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214531_comment'></div>初，宣德府君不喜吏职，浮沈筦库数年，亟谢事归家巷，故公亦濡迹埋光，不及擢序，而族昆节夫以儒学将略致位侍从，屡殿大邦，终龙图阁学士、正奉大夫，胄阀益显矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214531_comment'></div>公娶张氏，亦同志趣，后公二年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214531_comment'></div>男曰忻，女一人，皆幼，能举公及公妻之丧，以政和元年二月壬寅合葬于江州德化县先生乡之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214531_comment'></div>且求予铭以谢葬者，尚书司封员外郎悦，龙图阁公子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214531_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1214531'>浔阳之城，柴桑之里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214531_comment'></div>靖节之家，有贤孙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214531_comment'></div>不慕荣利，閒静少言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214531_comment'></div>官止著作，以屈为伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214531_comment'></div>其尚类也，视此刻文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1214531_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年4月8日</a>　有诗赠县丞曹文中。作品：四月八日蒙文中饷黑饭作诗二首纪谢。<div id='poem_523837' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523837' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523837?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四月八日蒙文中饷黑饭作诗二首纪谢<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年4月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523837")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523837_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523837'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523837'>热际初经四月八，磨香灌佛晓泉寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523837_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523837'>丞公忽致槃游饭，儿辈惊看欢喜丸。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523838?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年4月8日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523838'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年4月</a><div id='poem_523839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>比作黑饭新茶二首未蒙文中县丞宠和走笔再赋以助一笑<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_523839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523839'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523839'>点漆饭蒙清净供，翻匙那敢配羊寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523839'>独欣法味盈斋钵，尚欲诗辞看弹丸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523839'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523839_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年5月16日</a>　会食普满院，有诗。作品：五月望日会食普满院夜归作诗二首呈文中县丞玉老禅师江【左边“学”字，右边“攵”】王彧。<div id='poem_523627' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>五月望日会食普满院夜归作诗二首呈文中县丞玉老禅师江敩王彧<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年5月</a>　盆池放鱼。作品：盆池放鱼送曹文中。<div id='poem_523380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>盆池放鱼呈曹文中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523380")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523380'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523380'>小鱼如针锋，大鱼如柳叶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523380'>舍之石斛中，泼泼逝鳞鬣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523380'>秋毫麸与籺，腹果意各惬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523380'>渺如在湖海，不叹杯水狭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523380'>笑之复自笑，邑小大邦摄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523380'>摇足已恐堕，一动不敢辄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523380'>廪人给五斗，饘粥周儿妾。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523380'>虽然颇自适，携杖园日涉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523380'>岂羡蝉冕窟，迁擢等常猎。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523380'>漆园信知鱼，非惟常梦蝶。<div id='poem_sentence_9_523380_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_523380'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_523380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年7月</a>　为祁门县作辟支佛舍利铭。作品：歙州祁门县青罗山辟支佛舍利铭并序。<div id='poem_1214512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>歙州祁门县青萝山辟支佛舍利铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214512")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214512'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214512'>辟支佛一名独觉，于无佛世出现，调伏有情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214512_comment'></div>然其始皆生人中，婴受众苦，起厌离相，霍然解悟，遂證果位，如《契经》所载苏摩大帝月爱月出之流，皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214512_comment'></div>自如来示灭，凡夫异生不知背尘合觉，观本性空，方迷谬颠，流浪苦海，而所谓独觉者亦隐弗现。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214512_comment'></div>则夫悲济利生之士，求其戒体之所自出者，崇建塔庙，使上智触境而悟苦谛，中人修供而植福田，其饶益方便，岂细也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214512_comment'></div>青萝山在祁门东五里，岩壑深复，有瑰奇卓绝之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214512_comment'></div>自唐永泰中始建寺，而湫陋褊迫，不与山相称，来者以为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214512_comment'></div>元祐二年，今住持道清师始嗣禅席，惟行与解二俱超然，道俗信乡之，未尝求而人自施，未尝劳而事自集，改营旧宇百五十区，卑隘者斥大之，漫漶者丹垩之，栌栱相辉，像设俱严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214512_comment'></div>意犹怀不满也，将建浮屠七宝岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214512_comment'></div>会山郡通守李侯景渊施所宝辟支舍利二十，而邑民张洪首开檀施，远近附和，委货利若材木者相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214512_comment'></div>遂以政和元年正月告成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214512_comment'></div>支撑巧奇，规模宏丽，露盘宝铎皆应经式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214512_comment'></div>今昭庆军节度使、开府仪同三司莆阳蔡公嘉其勤，为书六大字榜之塔，虽托于幽遐之境，而显名四方者，繄公书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214512_comment'></div>是岁七月十日夜毫光出，轮杪亘数十丈，色若火聚，申旦不灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214512_comment'></div>按《阿含经》云：「应起塔人，一如来，二辟支佛」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214512_comment'></div>《造塔功德经》云：「未有塔处，于中建立，乃至小如庵萝果，福胜梵天」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214512_comment'></div>然则光景出现，殆建造翘勤之应也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214512_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1214512'>犀角喻觉第二乘，见无佛世乃出兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214512_comment'></div>如日西入续膏灯，五滓昏暗聊依凭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214512_comment'></div>寂不说法閒莫应，神足变现时飞升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214512_comment'></div>遗骨戒定相薰蒸，驮都千亿数莫能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214512_comment'></div>偶得少分严缄縢，覆以斗薮波七层。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214512_comment'></div>夜出光相辉玉绳，赤髭白足见未曾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214512_comment'></div>岌岌榜字蛟龙腾，永镇江左高崚嶒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1214512_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年9月25日</a>　游凤凰山、筑亭榭、疏泉甃池。作品：凤凰山泉石胜绝去城无几里而前此未有者偶因休吏与文中良器二士访寻得瑰奇卓绝之观于荆棘草莽间相顾大笑因崇基址筑亭榭疏泉甃池为登临啸咏之地九月二十五日游陟归夜作小诗十首。<div id='poem_523858' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523858' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523858?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523879'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523879'>不甘蒿藋蔽流溪，混沌何妨一画眉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523879'>若遣周回插杨柳，醴泉便是陆家池。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523879'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523879_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523880?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523880'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523880'>隐吏皆非谩诲潜，夜灯花落广文檐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523880'>招寻月月携连璧，不用船中觅孝廉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523880'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523880_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523881?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523881'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523881'>屈曲云根屋旋移，下窥鸳瓦碧参差。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523881_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523881'>不须欲速求儳路，自地升天理合迟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523881_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523881'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523881_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523882' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523882' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523882?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523882_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523882'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523882'>云巘回环出远青，千层万叠莫知名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523882'>白茅峰独如黄宪，不见须臾鄙吝生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523882'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523882_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523883' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523883' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523883?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523883'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523883'>催功下下与高高，束火人归闹小桥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523883'>莫向九岩生妄见，须知采柏望中遥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523883'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523883_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523884?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523884_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523884'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523884'>滩声留客不容归，更尽西山一寸晖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523884_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523884'>要看冰轮升紫磨，绕枝寒鹊自惊飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523884_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523884'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523884_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523885' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523885' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523885?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523885_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523885'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523885'>秋残景物更萧疏，愁寄忧埋尽破除。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523885'>埃壒是中无少分，昼尘终恐误君书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523885'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523885_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523886?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523886_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523886'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523886'>闻有山房隐茂林，高人不与世相寻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523886_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523886'>屋虚但有荒基在，恐是宜僚遁陆沈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523886_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523886'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523886_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523887?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_523887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523887'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523887'>结友忘怀契道真，水云情话似亲亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523887'>爱君叶落云飞句，知是才高压众人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523887'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_523887_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214530?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文林郎姜公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214530")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214530_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214530'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214530'>姜姓本出天水，太公望封营丘，后世为田和所灭，子孙散徙，而天水之姜曰肱、曰维，显名史氏，至恪公辅相唐高宗、德宗，益号冠姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214530_comment'></div>君其裔也，讳周臣，字仁辅，世居睦州建德，莫知其始徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214530_comment'></div>曾祖考及祖考延德、考逸，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214530_comment'></div>君少孤，母李夫人训使学，专精自厉，已而文词经术隐然称诸儒中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214530_comment'></div>元丰八年进士第，调温州永嘉、江宁德化二县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214530_comment'></div>部索夙盗，囊橐过抵悉知之，相戒毋得觇君境，人赖以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214530_comment'></div>迁衢州录事参军，听狱明审，每甲乙参准，以钩取事情，不强以楚掠文致其罪，故狱无颇颣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214530_comment'></div>竟案，有可矜辄为奏谳，所全宥甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214530_comment'></div>任势者之辟，监洪州丰城市易务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214530_comment'></div>满岁，会省官，罢，改明州象山县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214530_comment'></div>逢受宝恩，迁文林郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214530_comment'></div>数行令事，为政简易，人便安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214530_comment'></div>未满秩，复会省官，罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214530_comment'></div>君性温良谦退，居官不以武健干名，所至称长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214530_comment'></div>隐约自守，禄赐缘手匮竭，不营归赀，鬻旧业几尽，识者清之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214530_comment'></div>暇日以所谓梵书者自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214530_comment'></div>进官淹晚，聊不婴意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214530_comment'></div>校吏考十一，不絓铢发过差，竟以州县职没其身，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214530_comment'></div>配南郡张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214530_comment'></div>子六人：男师孟，尝贡礼部；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214530_comment'></div>师仲，第进士，将仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214530_comment'></div>师季，举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214530_comment'></div>女长归同郡陈夷简；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214530_comment'></div>次归开封府何至德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214530_comment'></div>一尚处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214530_comment'></div>孙男一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214530_comment'></div>某令休宁，与师仲为僚，喜其齿少自立，于载籍博涉精说，诵说数千百载事如目击；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214530_comment'></div>既又闻两昆弟皆崭然见头角，意其门户且兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214530_comment'></div>亡几何，君来过师仲，见君以德善自晦，粥粥若不能言，固知流泽有在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214530_comment'></div>政和元年二月壬戌终于休宁子舍，寿五十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214530_comment'></div>诸孤奉丧归，卜十月己酉窆建德平碧乡之原，走书泣请曰：「先人行治，微夫子铭，且湮没」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214530_comment'></div>义不得辞，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1214530'>有所激以昌其气，惟学之嗜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214530_comment'></div>故壮而仕无所丽，以直其躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214530_comment'></div>惟义之从，故老而穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214530_comment'></div>祚德自天，嶷嶷三子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214530_comment'></div>庆充门闾，君其不死。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1214530_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　次韵韩景贤承议自金陵沿檄宣歙道中见贻二首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　周文之彦质运使巡按海宁追忆曩岁与伯仲同奉版舆之乐感慨赋诗……次韵和二首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
临汝
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ab063b2238c1481fb7fc5da68f7b1520_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ab063b2238c1481fb7fc5da68f7b1520");'><span id='ab063b2238c1481fb7fc5da68f7b1520_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1122')">1119-1122年</a>，48-51岁</div><div id='ab063b2238c1481fb7fc5da68f7b1520' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年12月</a><div id='poem_1214299' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214299' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214299?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢复右文殿修撰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214299")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214299_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214299'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214299'>殊庭游食，深幸安全；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214299_comment'></div>秘府疏荣，特从甄序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214299_comment'></div>隆恩下逮，感涕横流<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214299_comment'></div>伏念臣学不造于道真，材不周于世用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214299_comment'></div>自奋寒苦，三收词艺之科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214299_comment'></div>寖冒宠嘉，四躐师儒之等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214299_comment'></div>钦承纶綍，俾长胶庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214299_comment'></div>退量羊质而虎皮，何补鸢飞而鱼跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214299_comment'></div>肮脏但期于报国，颛愚实昧于周身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214299_comment'></div>惟行法已咈于人情，而处事每违于时论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214299_comment'></div>怨仇交积，衅咎易乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214299_comment'></div>猥自劾归，亲承训奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214299_comment'></div>慰留之诏始下，搏击之疏继闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214299_comment'></div>凡可排诋而中伤，无不崇饰而诬蔑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214299_comment'></div>莠言甚巧，惑投杼于三人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214299_comment'></div>幽结莫申，类降霜于五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214299_comment'></div>赖乾坤亭毒之施，察风波险陷之危，曲示优容，止投閒左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214299_comment'></div>微生易殒，圣造难酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214299_comment'></div>旋闻邦诬，靡逃天鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214299_comment'></div>阿比附会，著在德音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214299_comment'></div>放逐流离，屏之荒服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214299_comment'></div>臣之所坐，岂假自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214299_comment'></div>遂令流落之馀，曲被便蕃之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214299_comment'></div>稍贲集贤之职，渐刊司败之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214299_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下覆露万邦，帡幪庶尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214299_comment'></div>风挥日舒而专断，云行雨施以均慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214299_comment'></div>蹈舜之文哲而审官，体汤之宽仁而宥过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214299_comment'></div>肆令浮贱，不遂弃捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214299_comment'></div>恩已重于邱山，实踰始望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214299_comment'></div>身未填于沟壑，誓竭孤忠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1214299_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214373' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214373' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214373?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复修撰谢两府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214373")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214373_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214373'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214373'>殊廷氾扫，幸簉迹于臞仙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214373_comment'></div>秘殿疏荣，或厕名于墨客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214373_comment'></div>稍从抆拭，曲荷生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214373_comment'></div>伏念某者奋自羁单，进蒙简擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214373_comment'></div>逶迤持禄，深戒鄙夫之事君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214373_comment'></div>肮脏徇公，妄期君子之谋道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214373_comment'></div>一昨超登侍从，进长胶庠，虽无成德达材之功，粗有畏法绳愆之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214373_comment'></div>钦惟寄属，每自激昂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214373_comment'></div>杜请托则深咈于人情，多建明则显违于时论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214373_comment'></div>虽学子粗安其朴拙，而憸人潜议于中伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214373_comment'></div>孤根易摇，小器先溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214373_comment'></div>青蝇交集，白简厚诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214373_comment'></div>凡可排根而倾挤，无不诞谩而崇饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214373_comment'></div>彼正异放麑之惠，固优为掇蜂之谗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214373_comment'></div>上赖照临，止投閒左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214373_comment'></div>莠言甚巧，类成叶于三年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214373_comment'></div>幽愤莫申，将降霜于五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214373_comment'></div>惟神听之难罔，而天道之好还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214373_comment'></div>旋闻邦诬，莫逃圣鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214373_comment'></div>畀虎豺而不食，御魑魅以远行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214373_comment'></div>四门穆清，百揆时叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214373_comment'></div>惟兹枉挠，屡乞辨明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214373_comment'></div>敢期旷荡之恩，稍加丽正之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214373_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官心存体国，道广济时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214373_comment'></div>惠顾穷人，起伊尹纳沟之念；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214373_comment'></div>磨砻治具，肩傅说作砺之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214373_comment'></div>致脱丹书，渐还清贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214373_comment'></div>傥未填于沟壑，誓仰报于陶镕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1214373_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214300' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214300' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214300?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汝州到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214300")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214300_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214300'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214300'>序道山之秘职，已荷疏荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214300_comment'></div>殿陆海之名邦，更蒙起废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214300_comment'></div>苦心易感，危涕自零<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214300_comment'></div>伏念臣器识无以加人，学问本期治己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214300_comment'></div>会睿神之博采，旅俊哲以同升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214300_comment'></div>遍历清涂，皆非素望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214300_comment'></div>直栈传厩，虽知戒于回邪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214300_comment'></div>方穿运车，顾每难于谐合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214300_comment'></div>昨承人乏，进长国庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214300_comment'></div>云汉为章于天，何裨化养；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214300_comment'></div>日月有明必照，独荷矜全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214300_comment'></div>数侍清閒，荐膺训奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214300_comment'></div>维时邦汋，方擅台评。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214300_comment'></div>凡可倾挤而中伤，无不诞慢而崇饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214300_comment'></div>傥非洪造，岂有馀年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214300_comment'></div>矧退黜仅及再周，而恩渥已更三至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214300_comment'></div>既察采苓之罔，遂叨剖竹之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214300_comment'></div>滨九死而复生，殒百身而曷报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214300_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下宏规吁俊，大德容愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214300_comment'></div>旷然兼覆之恩，仁为己任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214300_comment'></div>展也大成之业，善与人同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214300_comment'></div>故虽无庸，不使终否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214300_comment'></div>臣敢不益殚夙夜之力，少纾宵旰之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214300_comment'></div>惩沸羹而吹齑，更防后患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214300_comment'></div>羡渊鱼而结网，勉企前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214300_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1214300_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汝州到任谢两府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214374")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214374'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214374'>起于宫祠，付之民社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214374_comment'></div>自顾散儒之陋，谬当良吏之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214374_comment'></div>亦既抚封，莫知报德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214374_comment'></div>窃以鲁山沃壤，汝水名邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214374_comment'></div>密拱两都，新被节旄之渥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214374_comment'></div>旁连四辅，旧称屏翰之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214374_comment'></div>当承流宰牧之权，必赴功肤敏之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214374_comment'></div>而某生姿迟钝，涉世阔疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214374_comment'></div>途如阮籍之穷，性有汲黯之戆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214374_comment'></div>学初为己，妄期造道以逢原；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214374_comment'></div>仕则慕君，性有汲官而徇义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214374_comment'></div>顾多取于公器，复显忤于要权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214374_comment'></div>致俎豆楚者几稀，而鱼肉涉者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214374_comment'></div>骇机一发，溢恶交兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214374_comment'></div>惟锐进之邦朋，方上摇于国是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214374_comment'></div>从而下石，易若吹毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214374_comment'></div>独赖睿明，烛知诬罔，虽褫职于辇毂之下，独赋禄于湖海之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214374_comment'></div>方齐得丧于环中，而置恩怨于度外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214374_comment'></div>以退缩为安身之计，以静默为进德之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214374_comment'></div>敢觊矜怜，稍加收用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214374_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官膺天大任，佐时有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214374_comment'></div>积累治功，若农夫之望岁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214374_comment'></div>铨量人品，如匠者之度材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214374_comment'></div>袁安不忍于锢人，傅说但期于迪后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214374_comment'></div>肆令衰懦，复与简求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214374_comment'></div>某敢不防患周身，指覆车而自戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214374_comment'></div>牧民涖政，忧制锦之或伤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1214374_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　谒颜真卿庙。作品：颜鲁公祝文二首。<div id='poem_1214581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颜鲁公祝文<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214581")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214581'>惟公以身徇义，视死如归，英风峻节，映照万古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214581_comment'></div>初，希烈矫据此邦，虽忠逆殊途，决不肯生公，然穴地而不敢坑公于坎，积薪而不敢投公于火，养子拔刃争进，而顾以身麾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214581_comment'></div>逡巡濡留，至祸且及己，始使人肆毒，则仰公名德之重而钦重之，为何如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214581_comment'></div>希烈豺狼蛇豕之性，不利于公，乃其判然犹知钦畏如此，况士之生于数百岁之后者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214581_comment'></div>况士之有知识而忠槩者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214581_comment'></div>某视职之初，首修视谒，以公行事告于邦人，岁时其敢乏神之祀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1214581_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214582?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214582'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214582'>公以危言峻节违忤柄臣，国忠、辅国、元载、杨炎、卢杞之徒交相媢嫉，相继贬逐，虽不能一日安于朝廷之上，而生平名德晖映，盖亘万古而不泯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214582_comment'></div>某待罪二邦，皆公庙食之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214582_comment'></div>祗见貌像，踧然改容，其畏祗之诚，何减公之于李憕、卢奕哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1214582_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_4_523743_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年11月</a>　贺宰相王黼。作品：贺太宰启。<div id='poem_1214396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺太宰启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214396")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214396'>光膺涣号，册拜冢司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214396_comment'></div>周公之觏绣裳，爰是皇于四国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214396_comment'></div>仲山之补衮职，盖以事于一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214396_comment'></div>夷夏共瞻，宗祊蒙福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214396_comment'></div>窃以盛世以置辅为重，志士以得时为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214396_comment'></div>抱经纶之业者，或困迹于草莱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214396_comment'></div>都廊庙之位者，或贻羞于竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214396_comment'></div>由才位龃龉而难合，故勋业寂寥而无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214396_comment'></div>天将福于斯民，世特生于良弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214396_comment'></div>恭惟某官斯文木铎，王国元龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214396_comment'></div>学贯天人，而博穷载籍以来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214396_comment'></div>辞该象数，而尽屈能言之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214396_comment'></div>英声茂实，夙推先觉之贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214396_comment'></div>峻节忠规，笃守后凋之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214396_comment'></div>自预闻于大政，益眷注于渊衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214396_comment'></div>遵制扬功，中辖著弥缝之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214396_comment'></div>奉公履正，东台存绳纠之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214396_comment'></div>果符梦卜之求，遂冠钧衡之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214396_comment'></div>赞又新之政，已寅亮于天工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214396_comment'></div>开众正之门，行共熙于帝载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214396_comment'></div>伏念某小器窘用，孤根易摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214396_comment'></div>又困风波，幸托帡幪之芘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214396_comment'></div>未填沟壑，悉归播植之公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214396_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1214396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年1月</a>　伯兄次仲卒。作品：太中大夫大司成葛公行状。祭亡兄司成文。<div id='poem_1214517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太中大夫大司成葛公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214517")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214517'>宣和三年正月庚子，大司成葛公寝疾革，诏饬太医诊治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214517_comment'></div>越翌日燕紫宸殿，上小语左右，访安否，以不禄闻，上惊曰：「当是为庸医所误」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214517_comment'></div>嗟悼久之，特赠正奉大夫，赙恤加常数，敕本属供葬费，置官济办，员外置州通判一员董之，上其子若干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214517_comment'></div>惟葛氏世序，自昔稚川为散骑常侍居丹阳，至公之六世祖自广陵徙贯江阴，故今为常州江阴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214517_comment'></div>公讳次仲，字亚卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214517_comment'></div>曾大父惟甫，赠吏部尚书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214517_comment'></div>大父密，中庆历进士第，以承议郎得谢，赠官至通议大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214517_comment'></div>父书思，中熙宁进士第，以朝奉郎得谢，赠官今至开府仪同三司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214517_comment'></div>公父子以清德纯孝显名，虽仕不遇合，遗泽馀庆，实焘厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214517_comment'></div>公与季弟举进士联中，调泰州海陵县尉，移常州宜兴丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214517_comment'></div>未行，除吉州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214517_comment'></div>遭父丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214517_comment'></div>服除，为国信条理例所检阅官，进《北道刊误志》，会当改秩，并迁奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214517_comment'></div>逢受宝恩，迎北使，汎例迁承议、朝奉郎，除太府寺丞，迁朝散郎，提举京西南路常平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214517_comment'></div>召见谈治道，纚纚可听，上品之，谓曰：「使事不足以属卿，行召用矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214517_comment'></div>至部未阅月，果拜度支员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214517_comment'></div>踰年，迁户部，逢幸省恩，迁朝请郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214517_comment'></div>公佐邦计，遍历左右曹，周知经用出入盈缩之数，及常平开阖敛散之本，橐弊根冗悉窒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214517_comment'></div>预修《续免役书》百馀帙，除辟雍司业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214517_comment'></div>是时朝廷尊荣，中外无事，上方乡儒术，而诸皇子齿寝长，英敏绝异之姿闻天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214517_comment'></div>既以次行冠礼，出就外傅，妙简僚寀以调护之，首以公兼嘉王侍讲，授经资善堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214517_comment'></div>未几，建安、文安二郡王出閤，又兼讲官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214517_comment'></div>转朝奉大夫，迁宗正少卿，赐紫衣金鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214517_comment'></div>进《宗藩庆系录》、《仙源积庆图》及预修《玉牒》，转朝请、朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214517_comment'></div>其后安康、济阳、广平三王及镇国公出閤，皆以公为讲官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214517_comment'></div>于是并领七府训授矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214517_comment'></div>政和八年春，嘉王与天下贡士群试集英，文词学识翘然出寒俊右，唱名第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214517_comment'></div>公入谢，胪传趣使前，谕以教导有劳，宜褒赏，俄被批旨，特转行一官，遂为朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214517_comment'></div>上愈益欲诸王笃学问，诏讲官毋得兼他职，除公直龙图阁、提点东太一宫，专讲事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214517_comment'></div>已而朝论谓不可妨公涂辙，岁中除中书舍人，迁给事中，直讲如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214517_comment'></div>先是，有旨下中书，后来皇子就学，更不除他吏，止以兼领，公意殊不敢当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214517_comment'></div>会嘉王进封郓，建安、文安开国，景、肃相继出居蕃衍宅，因抗疏自列，曰：「陛下过私小臣，使待罪劝讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214517_comment'></div>今三王既即外第，而安康诸王尚宅中禁，非惟臣学浅薄，困于好问，且相距远，穷日之力不能周，愿专直蕃衍讲席，其他分命贤俊，且使臣逃尸禄讥，不胜大愿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214517_comment'></div>上不能已，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214517_comment'></div>转中奉大夫，同修国史，升翊善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214517_comment'></div>进《哲宗宝训》，迁中大夫，加食邑三百户，爵丹阳县男，除大司成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214517_comment'></div>致仕，迁太中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214517_comment'></div>公侍王府阅七年，说经无虑数十万言，凡典籍所载嘉言善行，日陈数千条，捃摭殆尽，至古人忠孝大节，辄反覆言之，间诵说诗文政事以资闻见之益，诸王每质疑问事、撰述，辄就商搉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214517_comment'></div>求跋法书、名画甚众，府第章表并时亟索，操笔立就，各极其工，宫中传诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214517_comment'></div>公每进对，上未尝不称赞谕之善，与辅臣语亦谓公靖共持重，得学官体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214517_comment'></div>一日在前，上从容曰：「郓王学甚进，作大字尤佳，《乞就外第劄子》乃亲制，可取视之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214517_comment'></div>因誉公，公顿首逊谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214517_comment'></div>在王府三被锡服，两推畀其弟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1214517_comment'></div>驾幸蕃衍，赉金帛甚腆，诸王各屡挥翰宠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1214517_comment'></div>呜呼，盛矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1214517_comment'></div>惟天祚神圣，并生天材以侈神明之胄，而公以孤臣蒙擢序，居职累年，出入禁闼，遍游邸第，谨孚周慎，不挂过差，遂结圣知，入侍帷幄，可谓儒者之荣遇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1214517_comment'></div>庐陵多士，隶弟子籍常三千人，公分教当兴学之始，以善诱著于人听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1214517_comment'></div>既董宗子六学及贰璧水，皆以德义师表人士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1214517_comment'></div>每较试，无不厌众心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1214517_comment'></div>外制特不试，而用在琐闼，论事鲠亮，凡出命未允，若除授不谐众望，皆封还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1214517_comment'></div>数相大礼，若夏祭、冬祀、明堂、耕藉、受宝，皆预执事，至考廷试贡士、奏告诸陵，率皆在选中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1214517_comment'></div>公操尚刚方，议论慷慨，常以输忠报国为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1214517_comment'></div>处家庭笃孝友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1214517_comment'></div>执二亲之丧，毁瘠踰制，日诵藏经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1214517_comment'></div>雍穆群弟，无间言，自开府即世今十七年不异爨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1214517_comment'></div>于经术汎滥疏达，非疾病未尝一日去书不观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1214517_comment'></div>晚节尤信内典，日课般若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1214517_comment'></div>洎属纩，神爽不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1214517_comment'></div>讣闻，士大夫下至闾巷，莫不痛惜之，而诸王尤极叹悼，各致赙送，以将其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1214517_comment'></div>文章典雅清丽，成一家言，遗藁三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1214517_comment'></div>少喜为诗，自晋、宋以来骚人所赋，靡不记诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1214517_comment'></div>尝为《集句诗》三卷，盛行于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1214517_comment'></div>年五十九薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1214517_comment'></div>母侍其氏，温国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1214517_comment'></div>妻先令人富春孙氏，今令人范阳卢氏，皆有贤操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1214517_comment'></div>子六人：立隆，国子监书库官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1214517_comment'></div>立悌，太常寺奉礼郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1214517_comment'></div>立廉，承务郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1214517_comment'></div>立象，通仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1214517_comment'></div>立会，承事郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1214517_comment'></div>立民，通仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1214517_comment'></div>女一人，适宣教郎、提举京东路盐香冯晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1214517_comment'></div>孙男女各一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1214517_comment'></div>诸孤卜某年月日，葬公江阴县屠墓村之原，敢乞铭以传不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1214517_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1214517_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭亡兄司成文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214548")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214548'>我辜于天，天不我丧，罚其元昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214548_comment'></div>阖门百口，有如水木，拔本塞源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214548_comment'></div>来谂迁陟，书墨尚湿，讣音在门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214548_comment'></div>变庆为吊，心摧肝裂，哀号叫阍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214548_comment'></div>忆赴临汝，兄出郊寺，数载抚循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214548_comment'></div>宁知三日，从容宴笑，永隔九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214548_comment'></div>人琴俱亡，风流顿尽，兹尚忍言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214548_comment'></div>先公盛德，理宜有后，烜赫衍繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214548_comment'></div>兄实济美，修仁行义，所闻必尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214548_comment'></div>靖共厥位，不肯噂沓，树党怀谖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214548_comment'></div>帝用嘉之，擢䌷史牒，琐闼词垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214548_comment'></div>诜诜天才，付以调护，听其讲论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214548_comment'></div>文陛进对，三接奖词，玉色康温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214548_comment'></div>谓当大用，而踬中道，敦究本元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214548_comment'></div>河通道达，今启藁殡，归驾輀轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214548_comment'></div>追惟官学，我鞠我诲，友爱特敦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214548_comment'></div>坐系微禄，小殓弗与，初丧弗奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214548_comment'></div>负衅至重，遣辞寄哀，聊侑一尊！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1214548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　伯兄次仲丧归故里江阴，遣儿子葛立方祭奠。作品：伯氏丧归有日遣立方祭奠。<div id='poem_523683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伯氏丧归有日遣立方祭奠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523683")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523683'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523683'>灵轜东下启铭旌，羁宦茕茕逗楚城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523683'>遣奠聊凭贻厥力，衔哀遥致友于情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523683'>虎闱典教曾同遇，雁塔书名亦并荣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523683'>齿脱发稀吾老矣，可堪回首望前楹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523683_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523683'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523683_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a><div id='poem_1214395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除显谟阁待制谢两府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214395")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214395'>白简骤攻，久投冗散；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214395_comment'></div>丹书一洗，复玷高华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214395_comment'></div>恩与为新，德何以报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214395_comment'></div>伏念某文质无所底，材能不及中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214395_comment'></div>会初载之博延，繇常途而躐进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214395_comment'></div>冒庠序师儒之长，参言语侍从之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214395_comment'></div>峣峣固人道之难全，碌碌实鄙心之不肯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214395_comment'></div>鼠衔窭薮，知非容穴之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214395_comment'></div>蜩决榆枋，不羡图南之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214395_comment'></div>果罹谤铄，旋辱辨明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214395_comment'></div>起于置散之真祠，付以承流之乐土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214395_comment'></div>图回百绪，黾勉二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214395_comment'></div>朝廷不忆一州，虽惭前咎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214395_comment'></div>民庶借留满岁，粗有公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214395_comment'></div>属积厉于衰门，遽缠哀于伯氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214395_comment'></div>念藐诸孤，方赖同爨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214395_comment'></div>故蕞尔邑，未可轻归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214395_comment'></div>不悟衷言，俾跻迩列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214395_comment'></div>既忝辅郡二千石之印绶，又直文考十九载之图书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214395_comment'></div>静惟所蒙，端有攸自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214395_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官股肱元圣，屏翰万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214395_comment'></div>以佑贤辅德为经济之谋，以遵制扬功为寅亮之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214395_comment'></div>用人心而引类，动义槩以恤淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214395_comment'></div>赞翊事机，独提纲而顿领；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214395_comment'></div>吹嘘时彦，讵拔本而塞源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214395_comment'></div>乃因肆眚之恩，上广隆宽之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214395_comment'></div>西厢寓直，虽叨序爵之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214395_comment'></div>东阁曳裾，尚恨趋风之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214395_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1214395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　陈与能将葛胜仲诗编成小集，葛胜仲赠诗请为作序。作品：迩日诗卷承若拙编为小集见示且有诗因次韵。<div id='poem_523693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523693?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迩日诗卷承若拙编为小集见示且有诗因次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523693")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523693'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523693'>骊珠鱼目两无遗，卷帙深烦为析釐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523693'>赋咏粗疏惭短笔<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：自谓。）</span>，赓酬刻画赖连枝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523693'>似闻警策眈佳句，何用编摩载恶诗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523693'>敢请冠篇重作序，二难文采胜延之。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523693'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523693_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a><div id='poem_523710' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_4_523398'>青嵩正北踊，紫逻复西峙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523398_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523398'>两岸千万峰，落影照清泚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523398'>周南滞留恨，此假聊一洗。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523398_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523398'>怅无周旋人，同载如郭李。<div
