id='poem_sentence_5_523459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523459'>请加什袭传后昆，阿买不独书八分。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523459'>纱帷昼静棐几滑，克肖鼻祖能缀文。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523459'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_523459_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523490?labeling=true' "poem_title_523490")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523490'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523490'>马鞭虽长不及腹，山林朝市两角逐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523490'>华堂谁挂元吉獐，坐使朱门变林谷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523490'>龙章凤姿自有种，山野头颅未为辱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523490'>长沙写真得天趣，下视冯尹皆奴仆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523490'>君不见青州刘幡得异草，能遣死麇骨再肉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523490'>又不见广平射麇变浮屠，因罢校猎投金镞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523490'>两幅陵陂槲叶香，俦侣共乐春草长。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523490'>昂头妥尾无所畏，窘拘知胜触藩羊<span id='poem_sentence_8_523490_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523461' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523461' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523461?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_523461'>造化小儿心恋嫪，偏向冰花施巧妙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523461'>冷禁霜带晓寒飘，清宜月缀微云照。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523461'>已与鸣鸠传酒信，更乞游蜂供蜜料。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523461'>交情万里寄春色，度曲五更吹怨调。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523461'>半树临溪抵死香，一枝倚竹嫣然笑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523461'>寒姿疏影太幽独，静女贫姝真窈窕。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523461'>世言嘉卉出灵山，我疑异种来圆峤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523461'>肯挑俗子炫秾丽，只约骚人伴吟啸。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523461'>少陵牵兴催衰白，广平被恼回刚峭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523461'>径须相过寿此花，市远无肴只藜藋。<div id='poem_sentence_9_523461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_523461'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_523461_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523634?labeling=true' "poem_title_523634")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523634'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523634'>嗣宗旷达早相逢，更喜林间识仲容。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523634'>林萼集中陪唱和，幽栖谷畔许过从。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523634'>云飞陇首高情远，枫落吴江好句重。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523634'>梁栋他年知有用，斋前楚楚一株松。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523634'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523634_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四桂坊<span class='inlineComment2'>（并引）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523670")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523670'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523670'>蕊榜连年诏墨黄，联翩恩绶月中香。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523670'>家声旧踵三槐位，儒学今标四桂坊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523670'>酬唱共传花萼集，笑谈应聚德星堂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523670'>门同列戟知非晚，更遣乡评服义方。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523670'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523670_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和送张元方南京掾</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523511")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523511'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523511'>下位沉英俊，青编乐自多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523511'>官曹依绿水，词笔注黄河。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523511'>初日嗟贪鼠，今年未饮鹅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523511'>陪京资禄养，何计免奔波。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523511'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523511_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拟明节皇后奉上册宝前一日奉告太庙别庙德隆殿明节皇后本陵祝文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214552")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214552'>维宣和三年岁次辛丑某月朔，孝曾孙嗣皇帝臣某，伏维明节皇后奉上册宝，谨遣某官，敢昭告于翼祖简恭睿德皇帝：伏以金台想像，玉册图徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214552_comment'></div>昭懿范于中宸，燕殊休于亿载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214552_comment'></div>涓辰蒇事，洁荐告虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214552_comment'></div>尚系孚祐之纯，永胙鉴临之赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1214552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　上疏乞免赋敛。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　举荐陈与义、富直柔、段拂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a><div id='poem_1214504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214504?labeling=true' target='_blank'>段拂教授字序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214504")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214504'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214504'>武威段拂，字去尘，金陵学士大夫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214504_comment'></div>余为汝州始识之，周旋既习，因告之曰：尘固当去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214504_comment'></div>昔楚三闾大夫曰：「安能以皓皓之白，蒙世俗尘埃乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214504_comment'></div>谢幼度之亲讥其学识不进，曰：「为尘雾经心，为天分有限」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214504_comment'></div>又六入之尘，实与觉背；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214504_comment'></div>背尘始能合觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214504_comment'></div>凡此皆尘之宜去者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214504_comment'></div>王导举扇障西风，曰：「元规尘污人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214504_comment'></div>王戎谓夷甫：「自是风尘表物」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214504_comment'></div>夫元规虽有当国召苏峻之失，终不失为名士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214504_comment'></div>而夷甫作三窟以自固，季年谄石勒以祈免死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214504_comment'></div>虽「尘污人」与「风尘表物」皆未必信，要之论人物者，以濯濯绝尘为贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214504_comment'></div>今吾子气调迈往，辅以学问，为文词卓然绝去翰墨常径，分教三郡，所至人士皆喜之，慈祥粹和，与物无忤，不必矫揉，自与道合，岂复有尘可去哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214504_comment'></div>荀卿子曰：「谏争辅拂之人，社稷之臣，国君之宝也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214504_comment'></div>国有大议，奋然撄鳞逆耳，规欲排难解纷，而宁以身为僇辱，百世之下，犹凛凛有生气，此岂患失鄙夫所能为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214504_comment'></div>吾闻士不自轻，然后能任天下之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214504_comment'></div>吾子敛然靖退，自遇若九鼎，他日进未易量也，愿以宝辅若宝臣为字。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1214504_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_523609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>段去尘教授示书以茶菊自况作诗谢之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523609")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_523609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523609'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523609'>高标落落敢评题，托物铨量庶似之。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523609'>娱客精神真北苑，可人风味剧东篱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523609'>云腴斗早惊先出，霜蕊禁寒属后期。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523609'>便欲相称为二陆，居然桑苧与天随。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523609'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_523609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年3月</a>　陈与义离开汝州返洛阳，葛胜仲用诗留别。作品：次韵去非留别。<div id='poem_523462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵去非留别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523462")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523462'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523462'>馀子碌碌不足数，太丘晚出吾所许。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523462'>淹盘此境未金马，邂逅相逢慰铜虎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523462'>与超宗语不知寒，从季远游那觉暑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523462'>祥琴皋月歘戒行，征马谯门聊出祖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_523462'>平生种学与绩文，自信扶圭兼缀组。<div id='poem_sentence_4_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_523462'>分无桃叶把歌扇，只有松枝当谈麈。<div id='poem_sentence_5_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_523462'>行装未办缠头帛，衣食何施择木羽。<div id='poem_sentence_6_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_523462'>从来文豹深隐雾，此去老蛟真得雨。<div id='poem_sentence_7_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523462'>长卿蜀肆初涤器，伯鸾吴庑曾舂杵。<div id='poem_sentence_8_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_523462'>青云直上不作难，那复笑人忧邓禹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_523462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_523462'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_523462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　送侄。作品：送侄元延之官。<div id='poem_523400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送侄元延之官</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_523400")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_523400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_523400'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523400'>浮游五岭南，屐裙遍迁客。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523400'>宠以鳌冠诗，独步文章伯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523400'>十年未得调，浪有声华白。<div id='poem_sentence_2_523400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_523400'>来宁未死叔，知费几马策。<div id='poem_sentence_3_523400_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_523400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a><div id='poem_523672' class='_poem'><div -----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2515067b5d9344999f4e1a427c8cb196_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2515067b5d9344999f4e1a427c8cb196");'><span id='2515067b5d9344999f4e1a427c8cb196_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a><div id='poem_1214300' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214300' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214300?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汝州到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214300")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214300_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214300'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214300'>序道山之秘职，已荷疏荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214300_comment'></div>殿陆海之名邦，更蒙起废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214300_comment'></div>苦心易感，危涕自零<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214300_comment'></div>伏念臣器识无以加人，学问本期治己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214300_comment'></div>会睿神之博采，旅俊哲以同升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214300_comment'></div>遍历清涂，皆非素望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214300_comment'></div>直栈传厩，虽知戒于回邪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214300_comment'></div>方穿运车，顾每难于谐合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214300_comment'></div>昨承人乏，进长国庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214300_comment'></div>云汉为章于天，何裨化养；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214300_comment'></div>日月有明必照，独荷矜全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214300_comment'></div>数侍清閒，荐膺训奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214300_comment'></div>维时邦汋，方擅台评。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214300_comment'></div>凡可倾挤而中伤，无不诞慢而崇饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214300_comment'></div>傥非洪造，岂有馀年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214300_comment'></div>矧退黜仅及再周，而恩渥已更三至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214300_comment'></div>既察采苓之罔，遂叨剖竹之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214300_comment'></div>滨九死而复生，殒百身而曷报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214300_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下宏规吁俊，大德容愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214300_comment'></div>旷然兼覆之恩，仁为己任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214300_comment'></div>展也大成之业，善与人同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214300_comment'></div>故虽无庸，不使终否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214300_comment'></div>臣敢不益殚夙夜之力，少纾宵旰之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214300_comment'></div>惩沸羹而吹齑，更防后患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214300_comment'></div>羡渊鱼而结网，勉企前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214300_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1214300_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　为民谋利。作品：答颜教授书。<div id='poem_1214344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答颜教授书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214344")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214344'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214344'>衰羸不堪当世用，尚得窃吏二千石之禄，以糊其口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214344_comment'></div>私意吴兴人士渊薮，必有卓荦气义之士，握笔操牍，日相规磨，使不干于罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214344_comment'></div>而到官弥月，阒然未有闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214344_comment'></div>忽得来示，详复累千言，析理叙事，汪洋昭析若五河东倾，不见涯涘，固深服左右之工于文矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214344_comment'></div>不知仆之不肖，使有所建明，以苏民之急，又窃服左右处心积累之依于仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214344_comment'></div>昔王生尝以言警龚遂，而任延亦以礼感龙邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214344_comment'></div>仆无似，何以得此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214344_comment'></div>所条预买，诚中时病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214344_comment'></div>近岁县官经用不足，给直每后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214344_comment'></div>时又胥史赇私公行，更复轻重上下其手，使齐民重困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214344_comment'></div>矫革之急，诚当如奉漏瓮而沃焦釜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214344_comment'></div>然所陈四弊，亦尚有可论者，愿他日更仆议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214344_comment'></div>得暇时过郡斋，不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1214344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年1月</a>　上书两浙发运使乞免均糴。作品：与制置发运书。<div id='poem_1214343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与制置发运书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214343")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214343'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214343'>初春气和，恭惟神相忠嘉，台候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214343_comment'></div>某碌碌郡寄，实隶部封，日托大庇，宁不知德？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214343_comment'></div>伏奉咨目，委以经制羡缗均籴二万斛，具悉雅意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214343_comment'></div>施行则粟出于万室，违命则罪集于一身，某岂不知此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214343_comment'></div>某实以敝邑乃水国，蛙黾之与同处，东南岁漕百五十万斛，而吴兴独无半菽之输，则土地不产米明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214343_comment'></div>去岁仅得下熟，而暴风为孽于垂实之时，收数不能什六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214343_comment'></div>比郡荐饥，舟楫运致者尾相衔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214343_comment'></div>今在市之米殆可粒数，而中下户已无钟釜之积矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214343_comment'></div>朝廷方复转运之旧徵，邑当输米四万馀斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214343_comment'></div>日夜鞭笞科督，殆将如额，而民已病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214343_comment'></div>今米价正踊，一斗将三百馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214343_comment'></div>傥以百金籴一斗，何止倍蓰之偿，则必有流徙饥殍之困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214343_comment'></div>所以累承公檄，不敢从命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214343_comment'></div>又况执事元奏请止于平江、常、秀三郡均籴，初无吴兴之文，则是执事已知吴兴非产米之地矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214343_comment'></div>今乃欲移嘉禾所赋于不腆敝邑，瘠此以肥彼，未烛所以也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214343_comment'></div>就使旋降朝旨，此旨下，亦已过时难输矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214343_comment'></div>伏望台照惠顾此方，特寝前命，岂惟某受赐，实数千万户戴不赀之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214343_comment'></div>谨专介布腹心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214343_comment'></div>干冒使威，无任惶恐待罪之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1214343_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年3月3日</a>　与叶梦得同游乌程法华山。作品：临江仙·与叶少蕴梦得上巳游法华山九曲池流杯。<div id='poem_224469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/224469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙 与叶少蕴梦得上<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>巳游法华山九曲池流杯</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年3月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_224469")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224469'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224469'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_224469", 224469, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>小样</span>洪河分九曲，飞泉环绕粼粼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224469'>青莲往事已成尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224469'>羽觞浮玉甃，宝剑捧金人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224469_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224469'>绿绮且依流水调，蓬蓬釂鼓催巡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224469'>玉堂词客是佳宾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_224469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_224469'>茂林修竹地，大胜永和春。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_224469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年3月3日</a>　燕诸部使者。作品：临江仙·燕诸部使者。<div id='poem_224472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/224472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>燕诸部使者</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年3月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_224472")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224472'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224472'>自古吴兴称冷僻，菰城水浸粼粼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224472'>回星难望使车尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224472'>如何三日饮，并有五行人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224472_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224472'>文似枚皋加敏速，记书易若张巡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224472'>幕中无用郤嘉宾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_224472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_224472'>他年浮枣会，莫忘两溪春。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_224472_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年3月3日</a><div id='poem_224474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/224474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年3月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_224474")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224474'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224474'>千古乌程新酿美，玉觞风过粼粼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224474'>歌声未办起梁尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224474'>九天持斧客，来作绣衣人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224474_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224474'>夙有辞华惊乙览，传闻献颂东巡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224474'>未应握节久宾宾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_224474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_224474'>一封驰诏旨，却醉上林春。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_224474_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年3月16日</a>　至卞山访叶梦得。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年4月</a>　返江阴安葬亡妻。作品：妻硕人张氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1214539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>妻硕人张氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214539")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214539_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214539'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214539'>宣和四年五月乙丑，硕人张氏殁于汝州公府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214539_comment'></div>时某领郡，以妻亡谂于朝，求移守吴兴，诏许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214539_comment'></div>六月，护丧归常州，留二息奉柩而趋治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214539_comment'></div>既卜葬，得地于江阴县由里山之原，复谂朝取急以视窆，诏又许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214539_comment'></div>遂以五年四月己酉襄事，叙其行事而泣铭之曰：硕人世籍常州宜兴，讳濩，字靖姜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214539_comment'></div>考朝散郎、赠通议大夫讳磐、太硕人姚氏之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214539_comment'></div>宜兴之张，世以儒学显，而姚氏在金坛为旧门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214539_comment'></div>硕人于女宪妇顺，耳目濡染，不习以能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214539_comment'></div>元祐中通议公为涟水军，我先人开府仪同三司君佐之，同僚且同郡，复闻其女贤，为某授室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214539_comment'></div>既归，不逮事皇姑温国夫人，事先人尽孝，衣服饮食亲在视，寒煖早晏之节愈久滋益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214539_comment'></div>于食财痛自节缩，而储积其馀以共公上，铢发不自蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214539_comment'></div>初，叔、季二媦未行，先人念择对之不易，硕人请以女妹归伊兄，二姓交信之，遂与礼部侍郎、今知徐州张公合好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214539_comment'></div>后三年，季妹许嫁今丞相王公，时硕人从予官太学，先人敕使归董蚕织缝纫之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214539_comment'></div>既讫嘉礼，先人喜，津津谓某曰尚平之累已毕，若释重负，而妇助我居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214539_comment'></div>岁中迎养，后如京师，会先人弃诸孤，硕人送终，厥饰尽礼，持丧踊躄如制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214539_comment'></div>于时二兄俱未卜继室，幼稚满前无依，家徒四壁立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214539_comment'></div>硕人裒掇纤细，均己子保视，以济于艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214539_comment'></div>其后某比预廷选，二兄俱宦，辇毂下阖门数百指共室同爨，而姻戚并时显仕，岁时燕集，轩骑填里门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214539_comment'></div>硕人虽处介妇，而调娱永顺，曲致恩意，中外无怨訾一辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214539_comment'></div>祀葛氏之祖考，馔非手调芼弗进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214539_comment'></div>喜浮屠学，日诵其语，食不击鲜，奉观世音尤力，课所谓《大悲咒》者，数以万亿计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214539_comment'></div>尝得寒疾滨死，观世音现白衣璎珞像升卧榻，以杨枝荆芥祓其体，寻汗浃顿愈，人士纪以诗文者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214539_comment'></div>在临汝力疾朝中岳，既还，一夕神识去体，家人环泣，诸子若妾媵各剔股燬臂灼顶以祷，观世音像复现，光相满室，黎明骤苏，安全四十一日，始不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214539_comment'></div>转识不乱，谈者谓累善之报云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214539_comment'></div>初封同安县君，进封宜人、恭人，后遇恩及拟封，两封硕人，前后训词皆称其贤操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214539_comment'></div>春秋四十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214539_comment'></div>男立方，从事郎、国子监书库官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214539_comment'></div>立中，迪功郎、河北盐香勾当公事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214539_comment'></div>立器，国子生，前卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214539_comment'></div>立卓，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214539_comment'></div>女长适文林郎、越州州学教授许旸，前卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214539_comment'></div>次适承务郎、登闻鼓院刘封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214539_comment'></div>一未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214539_comment'></div>孙三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214539_comment'></div>硕人祥顺祗修，善区处事，于书通大致，持身玉霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214539_comment'></div>始予未第，闺房百须一不相关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214539_comment'></div>既仕，数以戆直贾祸，流离落漠，而硕人能以义命相譬晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214539_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214539_comment'></div>继自今无相我者矣，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214539_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1214539'>委禽兮结缡，嫔予三十年兮，家室之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214539_comment'></div>我辜于天兮，夺其所与齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214539_comment'></div>年不配德兮，梦人授之以蓍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214539_comment'></div>生于建平而殁于临汝兮，藏于大江之湄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1214539_comment'></div>幽窀之词不以诿人兮，聊写情而含悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1214539_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年5月</a>　贺朝廷收复燕山府。作品：贺收复燕山府表。谢收复燕云进马赐诏书表。<div id='poem_1214287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺收复燕山府表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214287")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214287'>取乱侮亡，曾未施于三箭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214287_comment'></div>向风慕义，遽求效于九州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214287_comment'></div>茕黎输款塞之诚，渠帅有倒戈之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214287_comment'></div>事光惇史，庆溢绵区<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214287_comment'></div>惟幽蓟之封疆，本华夏之土宇，粤从石晋，始失版图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214287_comment'></div>垂二百年，擅数千里，凡谋国之士，议弗敢及，致在天之圣志未克伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214287_comment'></div>恶稔罪盈，众怨神怒，寇戎越在草莽，师众日寻干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214287_comment'></div>仰怖德威，如洪炉之燎毛发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214287_comment'></div>蕲沾圣泽，若大旱之望云霓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214287_comment'></div>遂扫境以来庭，同叫阍而请命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214287_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下神武不杀，睿智有临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214287_comment'></div>救民水火之中，玩敌股掌之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214287_comment'></div>全付所覆，仰承穹昊之休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214287_comment'></div>道观厥成，大洒祖宗之惯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214287_comment'></div>旧壤再归于中土，经躔遂备于周星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214287_comment'></div>成兹不世之功，尽出非常之断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214287_comment'></div>臣叨膺郡绂，阻献寿觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214287_comment'></div>抚鸣剑而驰伊吾，徒深赞喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214287_comment'></div>登泰山而建显号，行庆升中。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1214287_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢收复燕云进马赐诏书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214293")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214293'>复境金台，师既殊于左次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214293_comment'></div>称觞玉殿，贡辄效于右牵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214293_comment'></div>敢意恩纶，俯光衡宇<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214293_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下智勇天锡，徇睿生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214293_comment'></div>稽古则断自唐尧以来，治外则杂用采薇而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214293_comment'></div>爰修羽干之舞，同乎舜功之巍巍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214293_comment'></div>不遗虮虱之臣，赐以周书之噩噩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214293_comment'></div>深维荣遇，实贲馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214293_comment'></div>愿加什袭之藏，更殒百身之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214293_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1214293_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年7月12日</a>　与叶梦得泛舟太湖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年7月16日</a>　与叶梦得、陈经仲待月湖州城东骆驼桥。作品：定风波·与叶少蕴陈经仲彦文燕骆驼桥少蕴作次韵二首。<div id='poem_224467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/224467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>定风波 与叶少蕴、阵经仲、彦<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>文燕骆驼桥，少蕴作，次韵二首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年7月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_224467")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224467'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224467'>千叠云山万里流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224467'>坐中碧落与鳌头。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224467'>真意见嬉吾已领。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224467'>烟景。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224467'>不辞捧诏久汀洲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_224467_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_224467'>老去一官真是漫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_224467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_224467'>溪岸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_224467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_224467'>独馀此兴未能收。<div id='poem_sentence_7_224467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_224467'>留与吴儿传胜事。<div id='poem_sentence_8_224467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_224467'>长记。<div "poem_title_224489")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224489_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224489'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224489'>溪岸沈深属泛蘋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224489'>倾城容貌此推轮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224489'>可怜虚度二年春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224489_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224489'>暮暮来时骚客赋，朝朝新处后庭人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224489_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224489'>天留花月伴羁臣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_224489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年9月</a>　离湖州前通判饯行。作品：瑞鹧鸪·和通判送别。<div id='poem_224503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/224503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>瑞鹧鸪 和通判送别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_224503")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224503'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224503'>两年人住岂无情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224503'>别乘辞华四水清。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224503'>何事千钟勤饮饯，故知一别未能轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224503_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224503'>解龟虽幸樊笼出，挂席还愁海汐平。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224503'>江草江花都是泪，骊驹休作断肠声。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_224503_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
邓州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='088841a8ed5842bfa4931d933fb2e495_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("088841a8ed5842bfa4931d933fb2e495");'><span id='088841a8ed5842bfa4931d933fb2e495_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1125')">1124-1125年</a>，53-54岁</div><div id='088841a8ed5842bfa4931d933fb2e495' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年9月6日</a>　移知邓州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　到邓州任后上表称谢。作品：邓州谢上表。邓州到任谢执政启。<div id='poem_1214305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邓州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214305")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214305'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214305'>危诚自列，本缘三互之嫌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214305_comment'></div>洪造曲从，改涖一麾之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214305_comment'></div>奔走奉职，经营戴恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214305_comment'></div>伏念臣早幸逢辰，过叨序爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214305_comment'></div>容台蕝礼，往来数预于讨论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214305_comment'></div>教府育材，伯季迭居于长贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214305_comment'></div>实佩闻于德意，敢申尽于初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214305_comment'></div>旋以拙疏，久坐流落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214305_comment'></div>既不肯逐巧点妍而射利，又不能变节易操以随时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214305_comment'></div>岁籥七更，徒或梦游于帝所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214305_comment'></div>国门三过，何阶入觐于天仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214305_comment'></div>进无扳联之因，退守靖共之素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214305_comment'></div>惟兹楚境，盖昔邓墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214305_comment'></div>令臣领之，为幸多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214305_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下蹈虞舜孳孳之善，廓成王斤斤之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214305_comment'></div>揽治具而毕张，鉴人材而翕受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214305_comment'></div>少原之簪惟旧，未忍弃遗，丰城之剑可求，聊加抆拭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214305_comment'></div>臣敢不布厖洪之惠泽，佩烦悉之训词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214305_comment'></div>为国矢谋，虽身远严、徐之列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214305_comment'></div>与民兴利，尚志睎召、杜之风。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1214305_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邓州到任谢执政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214400")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214400'>愚诚上达，恳求避于亲嫌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214400_comment'></div>朝论兼容，特改除于郡寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214400_comment'></div>抚封云始，为分知荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214400_comment'></div>伏念某才不足以治剧济繁，学不足以钩深索隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214400_comment'></div>早缘识擢，尝获在前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214400_comment'></div>晚以愚惷，久从外补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214400_comment'></div>留滞周南之境，奔趋吴会之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214400_comment'></div>岁琯七周，未始侥求于内举，国门三过，其谁肯致于里言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214400_comment'></div>每处顺以安时，姑深根而宁极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214400_comment'></div>惟兹巨屏，素号乐郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214400_comment'></div>敢图生成，举是寄属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214400_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官功弼乃后，道觉此民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214400_comment'></div>扩伊尹纳沟之仁，懋傅说济川之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214400_comment'></div>弛张因革，跻国势于安荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214400_comment'></div>小大浮沈，器人材而式序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214400_comment'></div>肆令孤拙，获此便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214400_comment'></div>韦状员推，岂敢责成于参佐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214400_comment'></div>召父杜母，庶几追继于循良。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1214400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　与前任范致虚启。作品：邓州谢范左丞启。与范左丞致虚启。再与范左丞启。贺范留守致虚启。<div id='poem_1214401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邓州谢范左丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214401")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214401'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214401'>祗膺宸检，谬当方伯连帅之权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214401_comment'></div>趣引郡章，获继钜德元勋之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214401_comment'></div>荷恩实重，揣分增荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214401_comment'></div>伏念某文不辈于时流，学仅传于家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214401_comment'></div>幸缘亲擢，稍躐常涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214401_comment'></div>方幅员遍庠序之时，五冒师儒之等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214401_comment'></div>暨朝廷兴礼乐之际，三居绵蕝之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214401_comment'></div>虽事功无毫发之微，而议论有金石之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214401_comment'></div>岂宜乘隙，遂尔易心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214401_comment'></div>中缘背驰，久困外补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214401_comment'></div>萧望之各从所好，晋荀息不食其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214401_comment'></div>岁籥七更，讵肯侥求于内举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214401_comment'></div>国门三过，何阶入觐于中宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214401_comment'></div>惟兹大邦，夙号乐土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214401_comment'></div>猥当出刺，深愧食浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214401_comment'></div>伐柯在前，既仰承于旧故；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214401_comment'></div>邻辉不远，又获借于馀光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214401_comment'></div>恭惟某官天庭宝臣，海内词伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214401_comment'></div>险夷否泰，在峻节以不渝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214401_comment'></div>进退行藏，视古人而无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214401_comment'></div>方庙堂之阙位，伫涣号以扬庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214401_comment'></div>独专国柄之崇，仰赞时雍之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214401_comment'></div>重惟疏贱，过荷奖知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214401_comment'></div>近缘假道以登门，幸获望尘而侍坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214401_comment'></div>加笾豆之践，仍许造于后堂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214401_comment'></div>窥《云汉》之章，遂遍观于崇宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214401_comment'></div>虽大贤折节以下士，而小心揣分以难酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214401_comment'></div>感幸之深，敷宣莫罄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214401_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1214401_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1214403' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214403' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214403?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再与范左丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214403")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214403_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214403'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214403'>确守《礼》经，盖欲表仪当世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214403_comment'></div>曲从诚请，是为体貌大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214403_comment'></div>郁四海之具瞻，笃三年之通制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214403_comment'></div>有识交颂，不谋同辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214403_comment'></div>恭惟某官气禀天和，学优王佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214403_comment'></div>谠议早扶于国是，忠规屡詟于邦朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214403_comment'></div>爰录勋庸，遂参机政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214403_comment'></div>王臣蹇蹇，方尽瘁以输忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214403_comment'></div>棘人栾栾，遽衔哀而去位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214403_comment'></div>祗膺夺服，聊免造朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214403_comment'></div>仁者安仁，固不忘于子职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214403_comment'></div>孝乎惟孝，深上动于天聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214403_comment'></div>岂惟君子之光，实使懦夫有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214403_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1214403_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　有诗寄湖州同僚。作品：至南阳却寄吴兴诸僚。<div id='poem_523405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/523405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>至南阳却寄吴兴诸僚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　有诗寄兄弟友卿。作品：友卿寄谢并月波酒和其韵。<div id='poem_523704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_523704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_523704'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_523704'>长须剥啄叩柴扃，令弟官清远寄声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_523704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_523704'>擿句已欣资艺圃，漱醪兼赖破愁城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_523704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_523704'>牵丝闻说恢材力，露板应连上姓名。<div id='poem_title_224507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224507'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224507'>望云门外。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224507'>油壁如流水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224507'>空巷逐朱幡，步春风、香河七里。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224507'>冶容炫服，摸石道宜男，穿翠霭，度飞桥，影在清漪里。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224507_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224507'>秦头楚尾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_224507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_224507'>千古风流地。<div id='poem_sentence_5_224507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_224507'>试问汉江边，有解佩、行云旧事。<div id='poem_sentence_6_224507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_224507'>主人是客，一笑强颁春，烧灯后，赏花前，遥忆年年醉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_224507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年3月</a>　始离邓州。作品：浪淘沙·将去南阳作。<div id='poem_224496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_224496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/224496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浪淘沙令 将去南阳作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_224496")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_224496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_224496'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_224496'>步屧对东风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_224496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_224496'>细探春工。<div id='poem_sentence_1_224496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_224496'>百花堂下牡丹丛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_224496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_224496'>莫恨使君来便去，不见鞓红。<div id='poem_sentence_3_224496_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_224496'>雾眼一衰翁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_224496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_224496'>无意芳秾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_224496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_224496'>年来结习已成空。<div id='poem_sentence_6_224496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_224496'>寄语国香雕槛里，好为人容。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_224496_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='48552408b877401cbd25102d370d38e4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("48552408b877401cbd25102d370d38e4");'><span id='48552408b877401cbd25102d370d38e4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>，54岁</div><div id='48552408b877401cbd25102d370d38e4' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='be648974a7f44a7590b646aba74b5605_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("be648974a7f44a7590b646aba74b5605");'><span id='be648974a7f44a7590b646aba74b5605_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>，55岁</div><div id='be648974a7f44a7590b646aba74b5605' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年10月</a><div id='poem_1214544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>平江祭外祖父母墓文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214544")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214544'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214544'>某薄祐不天，未弱冠失所恃，岁朔流迈，凯风寒泉之感，未尝辄忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214544_comment'></div>举杯棬而阻饮，抚奁镜以兴悲，况其所自出，其敢忘哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214544_comment'></div>仰惟二尊，德善在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214544_comment'></div>庆覃后裔，是生仲舅，为时名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214544_comment'></div>载诞淑女，来嫔祢庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214544_comment'></div>虽音容已邈，而肸蚃如存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214544_comment'></div>某伏念生不及膺宅相之褒，殁未能效立传之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214544_comment'></div>远诣幽宫，式瞻松槚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214544_comment'></div>因陈薄醊，仰觊迪尝！</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1214544_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年12月</a>　为妹夫施大伦之父作墓志铭。作品：朝议大夫施公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1214521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1214521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1214521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝议大夫施公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31324, "宋", "葛胜仲", "poem_title_1214521")'>葛胜仲</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1214521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1214521'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1214521'>熙宁六年，神宗廷策士，擢余中为天下第一，与开封礼部第一人皆著籍常州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1214521_comment'></div>是岁州举进士中第者四十馀人，号称东南儒学之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1214521_comment'></div>公弱冠在选中，志行高整，举止严重，识者推为远器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1214521_comment'></div>其后在政岁久，朝廷闵劳官职之事，以上大夫食宫祠之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1214521_comment'></div>而长子坰嗣以学识议论蒙擢序，除提举河北路学事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1214521_comment'></div>入对，以亲春秋高，恳易近乡一官，诏特改淮东路，遂迎公至部所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1214521_comment'></div>已而易使江东，其治在鄱阳，道险且远，复谂于朝，请移治他郡，不报，则迎公至金陵，往来色养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1214521_comment'></div>方是时，公之同榜彫丧略尽，独公岿然康强，数从子官，享安舆击鲜之奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1214521_comment'></div>盖公仕四朝，历官五十有五年，始归政天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1214521_comment'></div>于是搢绅又推公能耸其德，克享寿宠，为世可愿云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1214521_comment'></div>公讳大任，字和叟，姓施氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1214521_comment'></div>始名天任，有所避，更名某；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1214521_comment'></div>又有所避，更今名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1214521_comment'></div>其受姓自鲁施父，至汉，雠为博士，延为太尉，其昆裔散居南土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1214521_comment'></div>公之先居建康，李氏时徙常州，今为武进人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1214521_comment'></div>大王父某，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1214521_comment'></div>王父某，赠殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1214521_comment'></div>父某，朝奉郎、知临江军，赠金紫光禄大夫，世称笃行君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1214521_comment'></div>公幼奇颖，视书一再过辄记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1214521_comment'></div>十一岁以文见王平甫，大蒙赏识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1214521_comment'></div>长从王补之受业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1214521_comment'></div>时新传未出，诸儒于师说或未晤，退质于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1214521_comment'></div>公为剖析奥境，人人得所未闻，由是以通经致名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1214521_comment'></div>初调越州上虞县主簿，以真州军事推官知越州录事参军，遭临江忧去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1214521_comment'></div>卒丧，监杭州在城都税院，转左宣德郎，知泰州海陵县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1214521_comment'></div>以奉议郎、朝奉郎通判淄州，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1214521_comment'></div>以朝散郎、朝请郎、朝奉大夫通判舒州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1214521_comment'></div>以朝散大夫知南康军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1214521_comment'></div>以朝请大夫管勾衢州福康观、台州崇道观，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1214521_comment'></div>寻上章请老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1214521_comment'></div>渊圣即阼，迁朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1214521_comment'></div>公在越州，乡民有过失杀人者，县牍以故坐之，公为平反，得减死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1214521_comment'></div>仓吏受赇被考案，其所亲方为部使者，佐吏因连引以觊骫法，公案正，事情愈急，并置之理，人服其平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1214521_comment'></div>六校吏考阅，帅守皆贵卿，不敢以公礼相格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1214521_comment'></div>赵清献公尝语人曰：「施君年少而德老，非凡偶近器也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1214521_comment'></div>亟荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1214521_comment'></div>郑敏中每引以佐裁决，且使代笺奏，悉皆叹奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1214521_comment'></div>其服筦榷，能不薄其官，而亲靡密细务，课皆羡元额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1214521_comment'></div>在杭州，其僚有游子每负盛气陵公，公弗校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1214521_comment'></div>居亡何，其人以不法被案，公为申救甚力，乃始愧服，而公以此称长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1214521_comment'></div>海陵官寺与天庆观为邻，观方士徐守信方以知人祸福死生倾一时，中外皆神之，势燄薰灼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1214521_comment'></div>其徒因请县隙地以广观宇，公叱不许，则诿州将求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1214521_comment'></div>公曰：「令虽卑，然听事之地，朝夕虔君命与守等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1214521_comment'></div>虽寻丈，岂敢辄与人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1214521_comment'></div>令不去，地不可得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1214521_comment'></div>讫公在事，不能夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1214521_comment'></div>岁大水，按田者不肯以实蠲赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1214521_comment'></div>公固争于郡使，民得复乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1214521_comment'></div>其在淄也，会初颁学校、居养、安济、漏泽等法，使者督州县如束湿，公能佐其长以岂弟行之，事既振举，民不告病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1214521_comment'></div>剧贼邵四，有众数千人，剽劫为京东患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1214521_comment'></div>公被檄逐捕，能合精锐，设筹策，使渠率效首，民赖以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1214521_comment'></div>历佐舒守二人，前至者政病宽，后至者政病猛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1214521_comment'></div>公从容其间，随事调剂，政以无疵，而人不知自公出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1214521_comment'></div>南康当九江凑，故号难治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1214521_comment'></div>公至则求问民隐，得一二奸吏，摘其宿负而流之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1214521_comment'></div>阀阅恃荫，横恣闾里，讼至辄披籍计其累坐，当以不赎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1214521_comment'></div>于是强梗震栗，相戒无犯公法，郡中翕然称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1214521_comment'></div>庐山在数里，公畏烦扰，不一出游，人或异之，则曰：「吾清操虽惭前人，然政欲一杯水亦不饮尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1214521_comment'></div>结课为一路最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1214521_comment'></div>坐官属输绢不中幅，免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1214521_comment'></div>还里中，即市宅梁溪上，敝小仅足庇寒暑风雨，日从故人宾客棋酒为笑乐，未尝以荣槁婴意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1214521_comment'></div>晚，病靡寖殆，诸子在官者各取急驰归，时神检犹自如，阅古今诗不辍，倦则使人旁读以听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1214521_comment'></div>靖康元年，年数七十有六，某月甲子终于里第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1214521_comment'></div>公志尚刚介，师祖道德，耻于驰骤进取，故仕止吏二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1214521_comment'></div>王元泽尝使人求其所为文，将以校官荐之，公谢不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1214521_comment'></div>范忠宣公、苏子由皆公知旧，当辅政时，不以衣裾撇其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1214521_comment'></div>于交游无末隙，然一闻其贵，则绝不与通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1214521_comment'></div>性沈厚卑谦，虽遇后辈必逊言恭色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1214521_comment'></div>尺牍非亲札弗以与人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1214521_comment'></div>平居肫肫以名教自律，不敢差跌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1214521_comment'></div>奉亲笃孝，共养若行丧服皆不奸先王之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1214521_comment'></div>亲殁既久，言及之必与涕俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1214521_comment'></div>凡持官守身，一以临江府君为模表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1214521_comment'></div>尝循牒至齐之历城，府君旧治也，徘徊悲伤，从长老访求善政遗事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1214521_comment'></div>归，镌石示子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1214521_comment'></div>家政母夫人处画者，尽齿不敢易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1214521_comment'></div>岁时烝享，前期祗祓，躬视豆笾，竣事则亲涤而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1214521_comment'></div>二弟幼孤，教之儒业，不以爱故弛课责，不以贫故怠供亿，卒皆能取科第，为知名人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1214521_comment'></div>致仕恩，舍子若孙而上弟之子堪，乡闾言孝弟者指为矜式焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1214521_comment'></div>所著书三十卷，其文宏博辨丽，诗尤入作者阃域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1214521_comment'></div>娶舅女孙氏，封恭人，前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1214521_comment'></div>子五人：男长曰朝奉大夫、江南路提点刑狱坰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1214521_comment'></div>次曰从政郎、越州会稽县丞埙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1214521_comment'></div>次曰文林郎、扬州司士曹事埏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1214521_comment'></div>次曰迪功郎均；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1214521_comment'></div>次曰将仕郎垓，俱以器能自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1214521_comment'></div>女适陈玮、孙迢、俞恺，皆进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1214521_comment'></div>孙男五人：广仁、广成、广受、广孙、广誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1214521_comment'></div>女七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1214521_comment'></div>诸孤既以公没之年十二月癸酉葬公武进县怀德南乡朱夏村之兆，而见属为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1214521_comment'></div>某既辞不获命，退独念先人清孝公与公并时擢第，伯兄大司成为公友婿，而公季朝议大夫知海州大伦，予妹丈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1214521_comment'></div>幸缘奕世之好，从公周旋有年，实熟公行治，乃不敢终辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1214521_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1214521'>猗嗟公乎，何众德之丰乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1214521_comment'></div>岂间气所禀，不与人同乎，将能以其所学而扩充乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1214521_comment'></div>砥名砺行，其以古人为宗乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1214521_comment'></div>以身殉道，其肯枉己而取容乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1214521_comment'></div>紫绶丹毂，岂曰不逢乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1214521_comment'></div>顾不究于大用，岂天将焘其后而不于其躬乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1214521_comment'></div>朱夏之原，抑神閟此吉壤，而为公宫乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1214521_comment'></div>其松其槚，过者其敢不恭乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_99_1214521_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
